1.1 KAH Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh ut touohkomukqut Sinaii, ut mukkinneáekommukqut, negonne kesukok nahohtoe nepauz, nahohtôe kodtumꝏ̄ mahche sohhamwehettit wutch ohkeit Egypt, nꝏ̄wau.
1.2 Mamusse ogkémꝏ̄k wame mukkinneonk wunnaumonuh Israel, neaunag wutteateashiyéuꝏ̄onganꝏ̄, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, nashpe ogketamóonk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, nishnoh wosketomp, neaunag uppuhkukkꝏ̄ash.
1.3 Wutch neesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk nashpe sohhog kesauwameonk, ut Israelut, pish kummaiyae wehkomôog nashpe kesauwameongash, ken kah Aaron,
1.4 Kah weeche kenaau na pish wosketomp nishnoh wutch chippanꝏ̄onk: wosketomp pish uppuhkukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ ut weekit ꝏ̄shoh.
1.5 Kah yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash wósketompaog, neg pish weechekompaumukqueógig wutch Reuben Elizur wunnaumo-/ Shedeur.
1.6 Wutch Simeon Shelumiel wunnaumonuh Zurishaddai.
1.7 Wutch Judah, Nahshon wunnaumonuh Aminadab.
1.8 Wutch Issachar, Nethaneel wunnaumonuh Zuar.
1.9 Wutch Zabulon, Eliab wunnaumonuh Helon.
1.10 Wutch wunnaumonuh Joseph; wutch Ephraim, Elishama wunnaumonuh Ammihud: wutch Manasseh, Gamaliel wunnaumonuh Pedahzur.
1.11 Wutch Benjamin, Abidan wunnaumonuh Gideoni.
1.12 Wutch Dan, Ahiezer wunnaumonuh Ammishaddai.
1.13 Wutch Asher, Pagiel wunnaumonuh Ocran.
1.14 Wutch Gad, Eliasaph wunnaumonuh Deuel.
1.15 Wutch Naphtali, Ahira wunnaumonuh Enan.
1.16 Yeug neg wehkómutcheg ut mukkinneonganit, sontimóog wutchippanꝏ̄wonganit wutch ꝏ̄shꝏ̄óut, wobuhkuhkꝏ̄utcheg muttannonganogkussinutcheh ut Israel.
1.17 Kah Moses kah Aaron wunnemunouh yeuh wosketompuh, neg ꝏ̄wesuongane ogkemutcheg,
1.18 Kah nag moéeog wame mukkinneonk, negonne kesukok nahohtoe nepauz, kah wahteauwáhuwaog wutontseonganꝏ̄ash, neaunag wuttehettashiyeuonganꝏ̄, neaunag wekuoash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, nashpe ꝏ̄wesuongane ogketamóonk, wutch neesneechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, neâunag uppuhkukkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash.
1.19 Ne anannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh, ne wuttinnu neh ogkemon ut Sinâi touohkomukqut.
1.20 Kah wunnaumonuh Reuben mohtomegheoncheh Israel, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, nashpe ne adtohshiéhettit, nashpe week ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, nashpe nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ásh, nashpe uppuhkukkꝏ̄óut, nishnoh wosketomp wutch wunnesnechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk noh weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.21 Yeug ogkemutcheg, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Reuben, yauunchage kah nequtta muttannonganogkussuog, | kah nápanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.ÆMDNMØ
1.22 Wutch wunnaumonuh Simeon, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe weekꝏ̄oash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, yeug agkemutcheg, nashpe ogketamunat wesuonga[t]h, nashpe uppuhkukꝏ̄óash, nishnoh wosketomp wutch neesnechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, nish noh pasuk noh weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.23 Yeug agkemutcheg wutchippanꝏ̄onk Simeon, napanna tahshinchage, kah paskꝏ̄kun muttannonganog kussuog, kah nishwe pasuhꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.24 Wutch wunnaumonuh Gad nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄: nashpe weekꝏ̄óash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, na[s]hpe ogketamunat ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash,, wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk noh nashpe sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.25 Yeug agkemutcheg, wutchìppanꝏ̄onk Gad, yauunchage kah napanna muttannonganogkussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchagkussuog.
1.26 Wutch wunnaumonuh Judah, nashpe wutontseongash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄óash nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekuóut, nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, wutch wunn[e]esnechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, nish noh pasuk noh weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.27 Yeug agkemutcheg wutchippanꝏ̄onk Judah, nesausuk tahshinchag, kah yaue muttannonganogssuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.28 Wutch wunnaumonuh Issachar, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, nashpe wutteateachiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuoash, nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wutch neesnechage kodtumwohkomunat, & paameu, nish noh pasuk noh nashpe sohhog kesauwameonk,
1.29 Yeug agkemutcheg, wutchippenꝏ̄onk Issachar, napanna tahshinchag kah yaue muttannonganogkussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.30 Wutch wunnaumonuh Zabulon, nashpe wutontseongash. nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄oash: nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat, kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk noh nashpe sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.31 Yeug agkemutcheg, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Zabulon, napanna tahshinchage kah nesausuk muttannonganogkussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.32 Wutch wunnaumonuh Joseph, wutch Ephraim, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄oash nashpe wutteashinninneongash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄oash, nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash | wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat. kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk noh nashpe sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.33 Yeug nag agkemutcheg wutchippanꝏ̄onk Ephraim, yauunchage muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.34 Wutch wunnaumonuh Manasses nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄oush, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash: nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄óash, nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄óash, wutch wunneesnehchage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, wame neg weeche sohhogig kesauwameonk.
1.35 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, wutchippaꝏ̄onk Manasses, nishwinchag kah neeswe muttannonganogkussuog, kah neese pasugꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.36 Wutch wunnaumonuh Bejamin, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄óash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄ash: nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.37 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Benjamin nishwinchag kah napanna muttannonganogkussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.38 Wutch wunnaumonuh Dan, nashpe wutontseongash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄ash nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nishnoh pasuk weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.39 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Dan, nequtta tahshinchag, kah neese muttannonganogkussuog, kah nesausuk tahshe pasukꝏ̄oh.
1.40 wutch wunnaumonuh Asher, nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄oash: nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nish noh pasuk weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.41 Yeug nag ágkemutcheg, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Asher, yauunchage kah nequt muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
1.42 Wunnaumonuh Naphtali nashpe wutontseonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekuóash: nean ogketamuk ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wutch neesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nish noh pasuk weeche sohhog kesauwameonk.
1.43 Yeug nag agkemutcheg wutchippanꝏ̄onk Naphtali: napanna tahshinchage kah nishwe muttannonganogkussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄og.
1.44 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, nag Moses | agkemoncheh, kah Aaron, kah Israele Sontimóog, nabo neesuog wosketompaog nishnoh pasuk, wutch weekit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh.
1.45 Kah wame yeug agkemutcheg wunnaumonuh Israel; nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, weekꝏ̄ôash wutch neesnechage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nish noh pasuk noh weeche sohhog kesauwameonk ut Israel.
1.46 Wame neg agkemutcheg nag nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄e muttannoganogkussuog, kah nishwe muttannonganogkussuog kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchag.
1.47 Qut Levitsog, nashpe wutchippanꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, matta nag kenugke neg kꝏ̄togkemoneau.
1.48 Newutche Jehovah mahche kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau.
1.49 Webe wutchippanꝏ̄onk Levi matta pish kutogketamꝏ̄un, asuh matta kukkenugogkemóog wunnaumonuh Israel.
1.50 Qut ken, kukkehtim Levitsog nanauwunnumunat Tabernakle wauwaonk, kah wame wishquash nish noh ohtagish kah wame nish na wadchiigish nag pish kenunnumwog Tabernakle, kah wame ꝏ̄wishquash, kah nag pish ne ut wuttinneumun; kah nag pish tuppuksinwog waéenu Tabernakleut.
1.51 Kah pummuwuttauwaekommuk monchadtomuk, Levitsog pish wussohqunnumuneau, kah pummuwuttauwakommuk wekitteamuk, Levitsog pish ꝏ̄wekikoneau, kah penꝏ̄wot noh pasꝏ̄sukog, pish nushau.
1.52 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel pish tuppuksinwóg, nish noh wosketomp ut nehenwonche tuppuksinꝏ̄wonganit, kah nish noh wosketomp kishke nehenwonche ummuttaákinit, pannuppe ukkesauwameonkanꝏ̄óut.
1.53 Qut Levitsog pish wééne tupuksinwog pumme wuttauwae kommukque wauwaonganit, onk woh na matta kussopitáe musquantamꝏ̄onk, ummukkinneonganꝏ̄óut wunnaumonuh Israel, kah Levitsog pish nanawehteauog meechumehteaonk, papáume pumuwuttauwáe kommukque wauwáonk.
1.54 Kah wunnáumonuh Israel ne wutusseneau neaunag wame wutannꝏ̄naonk Jehovah Mosesoh, ne wutusseneau.
2.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh, nꝏ̄wau.
2.2 Wunnaumonuh Israel pish tuppuksinwog, nish noh howan kishke ummuttaágunit neaunag kukkinneasuongash, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuꝏ̄ash, piuhsukeh quinnuppe, mukkinneáe kommukqut pish tuppuksinwog.
2.3 Kah nag negonne tuppuksikeg en wompanaiyeu, ne pish ummuttaagene tuppuksinnowonk Judah, neaunág ukkesauwameongash, ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Judah, noh Nahshon wunnaumonuh Amminadab.
2.4 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, nesausuk tahshinchage, kah yauut mattannonganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄og.
2.5 Kah nag nahóhtoe tuppuksukeg, ne pish wutchippanꝏ̄onk Ishachar, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Ishachar, noh Nethaneel, wunnaumonuh Zuar.
2.6 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, napanna tahshinchage kah yauut muttannonganongkussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.7 Wutchippanꝏ̄onk Zabulon, kah ummugquom wunnaumonuh Zabulon, noh Eliab wunaumonuh Helon.
2.8 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, napanna tahshinchag kah netausuk tahshit muttannonganog kussuog kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.9 Wame neg ogkemutcheg wuttuppukkussinnꝏ̄onganit Judah nequt pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganog kussuog, kah shwosuk táhshinchage muttanonganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe muttannonganog kussuog kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, neaunag ukkesauwameonganꝏ̄ash: nag pish negonshauog.
2.10 Reuhen ummuttaagane tuppuksinꝏ̄ónk pish ne sowanìyeu neaunag ukkesauwámeonganꝏ̄ásh. kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Reuben, noh Elizur wunnaumonuh Shedeur.
2.11 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg. yauunchage, kah nequtta tahshe muttannonganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.12 Kah nag nahohtoeu tuppuksikeg, né pish wutchippanꝏ̄onk Simeon: kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Simeon, noh Shelumiel wunnaumonuh Zurishaddai.
2.13 Kah ukkcsauwameumuh, kah yeug nag []gkemutcheg, napanna tahshinchage kah pasukꝏ̄gun tahshe muttánnonganog kussuog, kah nish wudt pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.14 Kah wutchippanꝏ̄onk Gad, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Gad, Eliasaph, wunnaumonuh Reuel,
2.15 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, yauunchage, kah napanna tahshe muttannonganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchag kussuog.
2.16 Wame neg agkemutcheg ut tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit Reuben, nequt pasukꝏ̄e tahshe muttannonganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshinchag kah nequt muttannonganog kussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchag kussuog: kah nag pish nahohtôusháog.
2.17 Kah mukkinneáe kommuk pish monchemꝏ̄, wuttuppukkussinnꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ Levitsog, na nashaue tuppuksinꝏ̄wonganéhtu, neane tuppuksinhettit, ne pish wuttine | moncheneau, nish noh wosketomp ut wutayeuonganit, neaunag ummuttaáginꝏ̄oash.
2.18 Ephraim ummattaágane tuppuksinôonk, neaunag ukkesauwameonganꝏ̄ash, pish kehtahhaneiyeu, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Ephraim, noh Elishama wunnaumonuh Ammihud.
2.19 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg yauunchage muttannonganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og,
2.20 Kah nahohtóeu, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Manasses, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Manasses, noh Gamaliel wunnaumonuh Pedahzur.
2.21 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, nish winchage ka(h) neese muttannonganog kussuog, kah neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.22 Kah wutchippanꝏ̄onk Benjamin, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Benjamin, noh pish Abidan wunnaumonuh Gideoni.
2.23 Kah ukkesauwameumoh. kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, nishwinchage kah napanna tahshe muttannonganog kussuog, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.24 Wame neg agkemutcheg wuttuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit Ephraim, nequt pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganog kussuog, kah shwosuk tahshe muttannonganog kussuog, kah nequt pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, neaunag ukkesauwameonganꝏ̄oash: káh nag pish nishꝏ̄e moncheog.
2.25 Dan ummuttaágene tuppuksinꝏ̄onk pish nanumeiyeu, neaunag ukkesauwameonganꝏ̄ash: kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Dan, noh Ahiezer wunnaumonuh Ammishaddai.
2.26 Kah ukkesauwameumob, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, nequtta tahshinchage kah neese muttannunganog kussuog kah nesausuk táhshit pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.27 Kah nag nahohtôe tuppuksikeg, ne pish wutchippanꝏ̄onk Asher: kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Asher, noh Pagiel wunnaumonuh Ocran.
2.28 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, yauunchage, kah nequt muttannonganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.29 Kah wutchippanꝏ̄onk Naphtali, kah ummugquomp wunnaumonuh Naphtali, Ahìra wunnaumonuh Enan.
2.30 Kah ukkesauwameumoh, kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, napanna tahshinchage kah nishwe muttannonganog kussuog kah yauut pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
2.31 Wame neg agkemutcheg ut tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit Dan. nequt pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganog kussuog, kah napannatahshinchage kah neesausuk tahshe muttannunganog kussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, neg pish wuttat ꝏ̄mwog, neaunag ummuttaáganóash.
2.32 Yeug nag (a)gkemutcheg wunnaumonuh Israel, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄óash, wame neg agkemutchég ut tuppuksinnꝏ̄wongannehtu, neg nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganog kussuog, kah nis(h)we muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchag kus[s]uog.
2.33 Qut Levitsog matta ogkemóog ut kenugke wunnaumonuh Israel, nean annꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh.
2.34 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel wutusseneau neanannꝏ̄nont wame Jehovah Mosesoh ne wuttinne tuppuksinneau neaunag ummuttaaginꝏ̄ash, kah ne wuttinne moncheneau, nish noh wosketomp neaunag wutteashiyeuonk, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄óash.
3.1 KAh yeush wutontseôngash Aaron kah Moses, ne kesuhok Jehovah kónꝏ̄nont Mosesoh ut wadchuut Sinai.
3.2 Kah yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Aaron, Nadab mohtomegit. kah Abihu, Eleazur kah Ithamar,
3.3 Yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuenuog neg sasequnutcheg, neg namwohtomuk wunnutcheganꝏ̄óut, sephausue aninnohsuonk ussenat.
3.4 Kah Nadab kah Abihu nuppꝏ̄og ut anaquabit Jehovah nag sephaushettit penowe nꝏ̄tau, ut anaquabit Jehovah, ut touohkomukqut Sinai, kah matta wunaumoniéog. kah Eleazar ka[h] Ithamar, sephausue anninohsuonk usseog ut anaquabit, Aaron ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh.
3.5 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
3.6 Pasꝏ̄che padchwuhtoush wutchippanꝏ̄onk Levi, kah neepauwehteaush anaquabit Aaron sephausuen, kah nag pish wuttannumauóuh.
3.7 Kah nag pish nanawehteauog ummeechumuhkausuáonk, kah ummeechumuhkausuwaonk wame mukkinneonk anaquohtag mukkinneáe kommuk, ussénat Tabetnakle usséongash.
3.8 Kah nag pish wadchanumwog mukkinneâe kommukque auwohteaongash, kah ummeechumuhkonaonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, ussenat Tabernakle usseongash.
3.9 Kah pish kuttinnunnumah Levitsoh Aaron kah wunnaumonuh, anninnumm(o)nadtúe aninnumauónuh, wutch wunnaumonat Israel,
3.10 Kah ken pish kukkéhtim Aaron kah wunnaumonuh, kah nag pish nanawehteáog, wussephausuenue aninnohsuonk, kah penꝏ̄wot, noh pasꝏ̄tshadt, pish nushau
3.11 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau.
3.12 Kah nen, kusseh, nunneemun Levitsog, wutch kenugke wunnaumonat Israel, nompe | nishnoh mohtomegit, noh woshwunuk ôon(t)ómuk. wutch kenugke wunnaumonat Israel kah Levitsog pish nuttaihéog.
3.13 Newutche nishnoh mohtammegit nuttaihe: ne kesukok togkmomog nish noh mohtommegit ut ohkit Egypt, nꝏ̄neetupanatamwahtau nuhhog nìshnoh mohtommeginitche ut Israel, naneeswe wosketomp kah puppinashim, nag pish nuttaiheog, nen Jehovah.
3.14 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, ut touohkomukqut Sinai, nꝏ̄wau,
3.15 Ogkem wunnaumonuh Levi nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekꝏ̄óash, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nishnoh nompaas wutch pasukꝏ̄ nepauzoh appit kah paameu, neg pish kutogkemóog.
3.16 Kah Moses noh wutogkemoh, neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah ne an annꝏ̄nomukkup.
3.17 Kah yeuh wunnaumonuh Levi nashpe ꝏ̄wesuonganoash: Gershon, kah Kohath, kah Merari.
3.18 Kah yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Gershon, nishpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄: Libni, kah Shimei.
3.19 Kah wunnaumonuh Kohath, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄: Amram, kah Izhar, Hebron, kah Uzziel.
3.20 Kah wunnaumonuh Merari, nishpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, Mahli, kah Mushi: yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Levitsog, nashpe weekꝏ̄óash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh.
3.21 Wutch Gershon wutteateatshiyeuꝏ̄onk Libni, kah wutteateashiyeuꝏ̄onk Shimei: yeush wutteteashiyeuonganóash Gershonitsog.
3.22 Yeug nag agkemutcheg nashpe ogkemonat nis(h)noh nomp(á)as wutch wunnukqut nepauzapinneat kah paameu, n(a)g neg agkemutcheg, nesausuk tahshe muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
3.23 Wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Gershonitsog, nag pish tuppuksinwog, wuttamiyeu Tabernakleut, kehtahhanniyeu.
3.24 Kah Sontim wutch weekit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh Gershonitsog. noh pish Elias(a)ph wunnaumonuh Lael.
3.25 Kah ummeechumuhkonaonk wunnaumonuh Gershon ut mukkinneaekommukqut, ne pish Tabernakle, kah weetu, kah ne abbahquos, kah áhohkꝏ̄chik onkwhonk, wutch mukkinnneaekommukque squont.
3.26 Kah chippinnutunkane ahogkꝏ̄tik wanequonk, kah ahogkꝏ̄tik onkwhonk wutch chippinnutunkane squoant ne kishke Tabernakleut, kah kishke altarut waeene, kah nish pemeneohtonash wutche wame auwohteaongash.
3.27 Kah wutch Kohath, ne mo wutteashinnunneonkanꝏ̄ Amramitsog, kah wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Izharitsog, kah wutteateashiyèuonganꝏ̄ | Hebronitsog, kah wutteatteashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Uzzielitsog, yeush wutteateashinnunnoónganꝏ̄oash Kohathitsog.
3.28 Nashpe ogkemonat nish no(h) nompái, wutch wunnukqut nepauzápinneat, kah paammu, shwosuk tahshe muttannunganog kussuog kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄og, nanawehteauunát Sanctuarie meechumuhkonittuonk.
3.29 Wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Kohath, pish tuppuksinwog kishke Tabernakleut Sowaniyeu.
3.30 Kah Sontim wutch weekit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Kohathitsog, noh pish Elizaphan wunnaumonuh Uzziel.
3.31 Kah ne meechumuhkonaonganꝏ̄, ne Ark, kah Table kah wequananteganuhtug kah Altarsash, kah Sanctuarie wishquash, nish pish nashpe waussumahetticheh, ahogkꝏ̄tik adnikheg, kah wame ne nashpe waussumáonk.
3.32 Kah wussontìmomꝏ̄oh Levitse sontimóog noh pish Eleazar, wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen, noh wunnanawunnónat, neg nánawehteunkeg Sanctuarie meechumuhkꝏ̄nittuonk.
3.33 Wutch Merari, ne wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Mahlitsog, kah wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Mushitsog: yeush wutteateashiyeuongash Merari.
3.34 Kah yeug nág agkemutcheh, nashpe ogkemónat nish noh nompaás, wutch wunnukqut nepauzappinneat, kah paamu, neg nequtta tahshe muttannunganogkussuog, kah neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og,
3.35 Kah Sontim wutch wekit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wutteateashiyeuongash Merari noh pish Zuriel wunnaumonuh Abihail: kah nag pish tuppuksinwog, kishke Tabernaklut nanummiyeu.
3.36 Kah nanawunnumwe meechumuhkonittuonk, wunnaumonuh Merari, ne pish, Tabernakle pasꝏ̄nogquash, kah neg pummetunkqshitteunkqunog, kah nish nepattunkquonkanash, kah ummortisu(m)ꝏ̄oash, kah wame nish wishquash, kah wame nish auwohteaongash na ut.
3.37 Kah chippinnutunkáne pogkomunkquonkanash waeenu, kah ummortisumash, kah uppinumoash, kah uppemunneahtonoash.
3.38 Kah neg tuppuksikkeg anaquohtag Tabernakle, negonnumeiyeu, anaquohtag mukkinneaekommuk, wutchepwoaeu, noh pish Moses kah Aaton, kah wunnaumonuh, nanawehtéauunat Sanctuarie meechumuhkonittuonk, wutche meechumuhkonaonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel: kah penꝏ̄wot noh pasꝏ̄tshadt pish nushau.
3.39 Wame neg agkemutcheg wul-Levitsog neh Moses agkemoncheh kah Aaron, neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah, nashpe wutteateashìyeuonganꝏ̄oash, pish noh nompaas wutch | wunnukqut nepauzapinneat kah paameu, neesnechag kah nees tahshe muttannonganogkussuog.
3.40 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh ogkem nish noh nompaas mohtomegit wutch wunnaumonat Israel, wutch wunnukqut nepauz apinneat kah paameu, kah nemunash ogke(t)amoe ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ash,
3.41 Kah ken pish kenemunnumwansheh wul Levitsog, nen Jehovah, no(m)pe nish noh mohtommegit ut wunnaumonat Israel: kah wunnetasumꝏ̄oh Levitsog wutch nompe nish noh mohtommegit ut wunnetasumꝏ̄[ô]ut wunnaumonuh Israel.
3.42 Kah Moses ogkemau nean annꝏ̄nont Jehovah nishnoh mohtomeginåtche ut kenugke wunnaumonat Israel.
3.43 Kah wame nompaasse mohtomegitcheg nashpe ogketamunat ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash, wutch wunnukqut nepauz apinneat kah paameu, yeug nag agkemutcheg, neesnechag kah nees tahshe muttannonganogkussuog neese pasukꝏ̄og kah nesausuk tahshinchag kah nushw
3.44 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
3.45 Neemun Levitsog nompe nishnoh mohtomegit kenugke wunnaumonat Israel, kah wunnetaseumꝏ̄oh Levitsog, nompe wunnetasumꝏ̄oh, kah Levitsog pish nuttaiheog, nen Jehovah.
3.46 Kah wutche yeug woh manꝏ̄whutcheg, yeug neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og kah nesausuk tahshinchagkussuog kah nushuog mohtommegitcheg wutch wunnaumonat Israel, nag anue monacheg onk Levitsog
3.47 Pish keneemunam napanna tahshinash shekelsash nishnoh pasuk,, nashpe muhpuhkukquash: neaunak Sanctuarie shekel na pish keneemunnumun, ne shekel neesneechagkodtash Gerahsash.
3.48 Kah pish kummag teaguash en Aaronut kah wunnaumonuh, ne anóadtit neg manꝏ̄whutcheg, neg anue monacheg, na ut kenugke.
3.49 Kah Moses nemunnum manꝏ̄whuttue teaguash, wutch nag anuánukeg, onk nág manꝏ̄whutcheg nashpe Levitsog.
3.50 Neemunnum ne ánóadtéhettit teaguash, mohtomegitcheg wunnaumonuh Israel, nequt muttanunk kah nishwe pasuk, kah nequtta tahshinchag kah napanna tahshinash shekelsash, neaunag Sanctuarie shekle.
3.51 Kah Moses aninnumauau Aaronoh kah wunnaumanuh, ne anoadtehettit neg manohwhutcheg, neaunag wuttinnowaonk Jehovah, nean annꝏ̄nomp Jehovah Mosesoh.
4.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh nꝏ̄wau,
4.2 Ogkem wunnaumonuh Kohath wutch | kenugke wunnaumonat Levi, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe weekꝏ̄oash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄óuh.
4.3 Wutch shwinchage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nô pajeh napanna tahshinchage kodtumwohkomunat, nishnoh pasuk noh petuttead kesauwameonk, ussenat anakausuonk, ut mukkinneaekomukqut.
4.4 Yeu pish wutannohsuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Kohath, ut mukkinneaekomukqut ut nukôme wanetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄gish
4.5 Kah Aaron pish peyau, kah wunnaumonu(h), tuppuksinnꝏ̄onk monchemꝏ̄uk, kah nag pish nꝏ̄kinnumwog onkwhonkane adnikheg, kah ne wunnashpe puttughummun wauwâe ark.
4.6 Kah nag pish uppononeau badjerde ohkꝏ̄nie onkwhonk, kah nag pish sepagenumwog webe ꝏ̄noónagk waabe, kah nag pish wunohtôog nish qunuhtukquash.
4.7 Kah woskeche nahtitteae petukqunnungane tableut pish sepakenumwog ꝏ̄noônagk, kah ne pish ukquenuhtauunneau wunnonkanash, & wuttattamwaedchuash bowlesash, kah onkwhegash nish onkwhosimukish, kah nagwutteohteae petukqunnunk, ne pish ohteau.
4.8 Kah nag pish ne wuttit sepagkenumunneau msquonagk, kah pish wutunkhumuneau nashpe Badjerde ohkoni onkwhonk, kah nah pish wunohtauog nish qunuhtugquash.
4.9 Kah pish nemunumwog ꝏ̄noônagk, kah pish unkhumwog wequananteganuhtugk wutch wequai, kah nish lampsash, kah nish tongsash, kah nish snuffdishes, kah wame nish pummée wishquash, nish nashpe waussummuáhettiche.
4.10 Kah nag pish upponumunneau kah wame nish auwohteaongash, ut agwe badjerde onkꝏ̄nie onkwhonk, kah nag pish upponamunneau ut qunnuhtugqut.
4.11 Kah woskeche golde Altarut nag pish sepagkenumwog ꝏ̄noónag, kah wutunkhumuneau nashpe badjerde ohkꝏ̄nie onkwhonk, kah nag pish wunohtóog nish qunnuhtugquash.
4.12 Kah nag pish neemunnumwog wame aninnohsuongane auwohteaongash, nish nashpe aninnumwontamwuhettit ut Sanctuarieut, kah nag pish upponumunnaoash ꝏ̄noónaganit, kah pish wutunkhumunáoash nashpe badjerde ohkꝏ̄nie onkwhonk, kah nag pish upponumunaoash ut qunnuhtugqut.
4.13 Kah nag pish amaunumwog pukque wutch altarut, kah ne wuttit sepagkenumunneau msquonag.
4.14 Kah nag ukquenohtauuneau wame nish auwohteaongash noh wadchiikish, nish nashpe aninnumwontamwehettit naut, nꝏ̄tae pansash, weyause uhquonash. kah shovelsash kah wunnonkanash, wame auwohteaongash ut Altarut, kah nag pish ne wuttit sepágkennumuneau | badgerde ohkꝏ̄nie ohkwhonk, kah pish wunohtauog nish noh wadchiikish qunuhtugquash,
4.15 Kah Aaron kah wunnaumonuh, pish mahche onkhumwog ne Sanctuarie, kah wame nish Sanctuari[n]e auwohteáongash, tuppuksinꝏ̄onk monchemꝏ̄uk, kah ne mahche n nag, wunnaumonuh Kohath pish peyaog wuttahshinnumunnaóut, kah nag matta pis[n] mussunnumꝏ̄og wanetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄gish ishkont nuppꝏ̄og: yeush pish ꝏ̄weannunnꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Kohath, ut mukkinneaekommukqut.
4.16 Kah ut wunnanánumꝏ̄onganit Eleazar wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen, wadchiigish pummee wutche wequai, kah weetemungquok spicee incense, kah nagwutteohtae metsue sephausuonk, kah sussequeáe pummee, kah nanáánumunat wame Tabernakle, kah wame ne noh ohtag, ut Sanctuaryut, kah ut auwohteaonganit, nish noh wadc[n]iigish.
4.17 Kah Jehovah konꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, kah Aaronoh, nꝏ̄wau,
4.18 Ahque tummehthash wutchippánꝏ̄onk Kohathite wutteateashiyeuongash, wutch kenugke Levitsut.
4.19 Qut yeu nag unneh, onk woh keteaog kah mátta woh nuppꝏ̄og, pasꝏ̄sukommohettit, nukóme wanetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄gish, Aaron kah wunnaumonuh pish petutteaog, kah nag kehtimáog nish noh wosketompoh wuttannohsuonk, kah ꝏ̄weanun.
4.20 Qut nag matta pish petutteaꝏ̄og kuhkinneaumunat, Sanctuarie unkhumuk, ishkont nuppꝏ̄og.
4.21 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
4.22 Ogkem wunnaumonuh Gershon, kah nag wonk nashpe wekꝏ̄óash ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄óash.
4.23 Wutch wunishwinchag kodtumwohkomunnaôut kah paameu, nô pajeh napanna wutteashinchage kodtumwohkomunnaóut, nag pish kutogkemóog, nishnoh pasuk petutteadt ayeuhkonat ayeuhteaonganit, ussenat aninnohsuonk ut mukkinneaekommukqut.
4.24 Yeu pish wutannohsuonganꝏ̄ Gershonite wutteateashiyeuongash, ussenát, kah wutch weanun.
4.25 Kah nag pish kenunnumwog Tabernakle onkwhonkanog, kah mukkinneaekommuk kah ne onkwhonk, kah badgerde ohkꝏ̄nie onkwhonk ne woskeche ohtag, kah wohwoashunk onkwhonk, wutche mukkinneaekommukque squoant.
4.26 Kah tapestrie chippinnutunkane onkwhonk, kah wohwoashunk onkwhonk, wutch chippinnutunkane squont, ne kishke Tábernakleut, kah kishke Altarut wáeenu, kah pemunneahtonash kah wame aninnohsue auwahteaongash, nish noh wadchiigesh, kah | wame nish ne waj kesteomukish, kah nag pish aninnumwontamwog.
4.27 Nean kuhquttuk Aaron, kah wunnaumonuh, ne pish nnih wame wuttannohsuonganꝏ̄ Gershonitse wunnaumonuh, wame ne naꝏ̄tamwehettit, kah wame wuttannosuonganꝏ̄, kah kenaau pish kukkeihtimôóog meechummuhkonittue weannunnꝏ̄.
4.28 Yeu wuttannósuonganꝏ̄ neaunag wutteateashaiyeuongash wunnaumonuh Gershonitsog, ut mukkinneaekommukqut, kah meechumuhkkonaonganꝏ̄ pish agwe Ithamar wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen.
4.29 Wunnaumonuh Merari, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekuóash nag pish kutogkémóog.
4.30 Wutch wunnishwinnechage kodtumwohkomunnaóut kah paameu, nô pajeh napanna tahshinchage kodtumwohkomunaóut, nag pish kutogkemóog, nish noh pasuk petutteadt aninnôfinneat, ussenat mukkinneaekommukque aninnósuonk.
4.31 Kah yeu pish meechumehkonittue ꝏ̄weánunꝏ̄, neaunag wame wutannósuonganꝏ̄ ut mukkinneaekommukqut, Tabarnakleé pasꝏ̄nogquash, kah pummetshogshitteaongash, kah nish neepatuhquonkash, kah nish mortisash.
4.32 Kah chippinneutunkane neepatuhquonkash waéénu, kah nish mortisash, kah uppinnumꝏ̄ash, kah nish pemunneohtanash, weeche wame nish auwohteaongash, kah weeche wame nish ompatamunat kah nashpe nishnoh hettamun, pish kutogketamumwꝏ̄ auwohteaongash ut meechumuhkonittue ꝏ̄weànunnꝏ̄wóut.
4.33 Yeu wutannôsuonganꝏ̄ wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Merari, neaunag wame wutannôsuongánꝏ̄ ut mukkinneaekommukqut, ut agwe wunnutcheganit Ithamar wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen.
4.34 Kah Moses kah Aaron, kah Sontimóog ut mukkinneonganit, ogkemáog wunnaumonuh Kohathitsog, neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, kah nasbpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄oash.
4.35 Wutch wunnishwunnechage kodtumwohkomunnaóut kah paameu, nô pajeh napanna wutteashinnechage kodtumwohkomunnaóut, nishnoh pasuk noh petutteadt áninnóhsinnéat, wutche usseonk, ut mukkinneáekommukqut.
4.36 Kah yeug nag agkemutcheg, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, neese muttannunganogkussuog, nesausuk tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah napanna tahshinchagkodtog.
4.37 Yeug nag agkemutcheg wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Kohathitsog, nish noh pasuk aninnosit ut mukkinneaekommukqut, neh Moses kah Aaron agkemáhetteupoh, neaunag wuttinnowáonk Jehovah, nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses.
4.38 Kah yeug neg agkemutcheg wutch | wunnaumonuh Gershon, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄oash.
4.39 Wutch shwinchage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, nó pajeh napanna tahshinchage kodtumwohkomunat, nish noh pasuk petutteadt en áninnohsinneat, wutch mukkinneáekommukque usseongash.
4.40 Yeug nag agkemutcheg nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuóash, neese muttannonganogkussuog, nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah nishwinchag.
4.41 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, wutch wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Gershon nishnoh pasuk aninnôsit, ut mukkinneáekommukqut, ne Moses kah Aaron agkemáhetticheh, neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄wáonk Jehovah.
4.42 Kah yeug agkemutcheg wutch wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Merari, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuóash.
4.43 Wutch wunnishwunnehchage kodtumwohkomunnaóut kah paameu, nô pajeh napanna wutteashinnehchage kodtumwohkomunnaóut, nishnoh pasuk noh petutteadt aninnohsinneat, wutch mukkinneáekommukque usseongash.
4.44 Yeug nág agkemutcheg nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nishwudt muttannonganogkussuog, kah neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
4.45 Yeug nag agkemutcheg wutch wutteateashìyeuonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Merari, neh Moses kah Aaron agkemáhetticheh, neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄wáonk Jehovah, nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses
4.46 Wame yeug agkemutcheg, neh Moses kah Aaron, kah Sontimóog ut Israel agkemahetticheh wutch Levitsog, nashpe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, nashpe ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄ôash.
4.47 Wutch wunnishwunnehchage kodtumwohkomunnaôut kah paameu, nó pajeh napannatahshinchage kodtumwuhkomunnaout, nish noh pasuk petutteadt ussenat aninnohsuonk, ut mukkinneae kommukqut.
4.48 Yeug nag agkemutcheg, shwosuk tahshit muttannunganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshit pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah shwosuk tahshinchagkussuog.
4.49 Neaunag wuttinnowâonk Jehovah, ne wuttinogkemon nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses, nish noh wosketomp neaunag wutannóhsuonk kah neaunag ꝏ̄weanun: kah nag ogkemóog nashpe nagum, nean annꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh.
5.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
5.2 Annꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, ummoncheahéonaout, wutch tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit, | nish noh, wutchekꝏ̄, kah nish noh pasuk sohwutchuanit, kah nish noh howan nishkhit nashpe nuppꝏ̄e muhhog.
5.3 Naneeswe nompaas kah squaas, pish kummoncheahéóog, ut poquadchit tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit, pish kummoncheheóog, matta woh wunnishketeauꝏ̄unaout wuttuppukussunnꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash, nashauwe toh apeh.
5.4 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel wuttusseinneau kah ummoncheaheóh en poquadchit tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit neânont Jehovah Mosesoh, ne wuttusseneau wunnaumonuh Israel.
5.5 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
5.6 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, wosketomp asuh mittamwoffis usseit ne teague wame ummatcheséonganꝏ̄ash wosketomaog panneseae matcheneheahittit Jehovah. kah noh keteahogkou kesohkóadtog,
5.7 Neit pish sampꝏ̄aog ummatcheseonganꝏ̄ ne asehettit, kah noh pish nompenum uppanneusseonk, ne teag, kah napanna adtahshe chippagish pish kꝏ̄tnum, kah pish wuttinnumauon neh macheneheoncheh.
5.8 Kah wosketomp wanne wuttinnunkomoegk, ne woh adt kꝏ̄tinumun panneusseonk, panneusseonk pish kꝏ̄tnumauon Jehovah, en sephausuenuut, chabesit wunnauwadtuwae (r)am, ne woh nashpe wunnauwadtuonk ayimauut.
5.9 Kah nish noh wahwaapenumwe sephausuonk wutch wame ꝏ̄netupanatamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Israel, nish pish pasꝏ̄chewuttauwehetticheh sepausuenuut, nish pish wuttaiheash.
5.10 Kah nish noh wosketomp nish waneetupanatamwahtunkish, nish howan aninnumauont sephausuenuuh, nish pish wuttaiheash,
5.11 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
5.12 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel kah nag us; howan, ummittamwussoh panneusseit, kah unnehikquit panneusseonk.
5.13 Kah wosketomp wehpamont, kah mat wahteauuneg wessukeh, kah noh adtahshont wuhhogkuh, kah noh nishkheau, kah matta wáuwenuunoh, kah noh matta tohqunau.
5.14 Kah mꝏ̄sitteámoe nashauonk nuhkukkongquit, kah mꝏ̄sumont ummittamwussoh, kah noh nìshkhit; asuh mꝏ̄sitteàmoe nashauonk nuhkukkongquit, kah mꝏ̄sumont ummittamwussoh, kah matta nishkheont,
5.15 Neit wosketomp pish pasꝏ̄au ummittamwussoh sephausuenuut kah noh pish paudtauwanshuh sephausuonk, piukque chippag ephah barlie nꝏ̄khik, matta pish wussꝏ̄kanumꝏ̄un pummee, asuh matta pish upponamꝏ̄un frankincense: newutche ne mꝏ̄sitteamoe metsue sephausuonk, mehquontamoe | meetsue sephausuonk, mehquontamwáhuwonat matcheseonk.
5.16 Kah sephausuen pish uppasꝏ̄tshanuh, kah pish wunnepauweheuh anaquabit Jehovah.
5.17 Kah sephâusuen pish nemunum wunnetupanatamwe nippe, ut ohkee wishquadt kah puppissi ne Tabarnakle ohkeit sephausuen pish wunnemunnumun kah pish upponamun nippekontu,
5.18 Kah sephausuen pish nepauweheau mittamwussissoh anaquahit Jehovah, kah pish woshwunum mittamwossis uppuhkuk, kah ponam wunnutcheganit ne mehquoantamoe meetsue sephausuonk, ne mꝏ̄sitteamoe meetsue sephausuonk: kah wunnutcheganit sephausuen pish ne wesogkonne nippe, ne mamatche yeuwáhuwómꝏ̄uk.
5.19 Kah sephausuen pish ummeechumuhkonuh nashpe chadcheyeuwaonk, kah pish unnau mittamwossissoh; wanne howan wehpamukꝏ̄an. kah matta nishkeneungque panneussean, ut agwe kasukut, chippehtash weesadtippog ne mamatchenꝏ̄wáhuwómꝏ̄ug.
5.20 Qut ken panneôas ut agwe kasukut kah nishkhennumuk, kah howan wehpámukqueas, pénowe onk noh kasuk.
5.21 Kah sephausuen pish meechumuhkonau mittamwussissoh nashpe mamatchenanittue chadchekeyeuwaonk, kah sephausuen pish unnau mittamwossissoh Jehovah ayimungqush mamatchenanittuonk kah chadchekeyeuwaonk kenugke kummissinninneumut, Je[n]ovah kobpiáog anehteunk, kah mogquenteunk kenogkus.
5.22 Kah yeu nippe matchenittuwahuwówꝏ̄ug, pish petutteomꝏ̄ kenogkussit, ummogquenteauneat kenogkus, kah k[u]ppiáog anittit, kah mittamwossis pish nꝏ̄wau, Amen, Amen.
5.23 Kah sephausuen pish wussukham yeush matchenanittuongash ut bꝏ̄kut, kah pish wutjishkhomunash ut weesadtipagwut.
5.24 Kah pish wuttattamweheau mittamwossissoh weesadtippog. ne matchenanittuahuwômꝏ̄ug: kah ne matchenanittuahuwómꝏ̄ug nippe pish upp(e)tukunkqun, kah pish weesogkun.
5.25 Kah sephausuen pish nemunum wutch wunnutcheganit mittamwosfis, mꝏ̄sitteamoe metsue sephausuonk, kah pish paupaumenumun, ne metsue sephausuonk anaquábit Jehovah; kah pish wussepháusin ut Altarut.
5.26 Kah sepháusuen pish neemunum yánitchan ne metsue sepháusuonk, ne mequántamwáhuwómuk, kah pish chikkossumun ut Altarut, kah ompetak pish wuttattamweheáu mittamwossissoh nippe.
5.27 Kah mahche wuttattámweheunt nippe, neit pish n nih, toh neit nishkhit, kah panneseáe matcheneheunt wessukeh, ne nippe | matchenehuwómꝏ̄ug, nish noh petukongqun kah pish wesogkon, kah wunnogkus pish mogquen, kah wubpiáog pish ánit, kah ne mittamwossis pish matchenanumau ut kenugke ummissinninneumut.
5.28 Kah tohneit mittamwossis matta nishkheont, qut noh pahkesu, neit noh pish chipappu, kah neechau.
5.29 Yeu mꝏ̄sitteamꝏ̄e naumatuonk, mittamwossis pannesit, wutch agwe wasukit, kah nishkhit.
5.30 Asuh wosketomp mꝏ̄sitteamꝏ̄e nashauantiꝏ̄ nuhkuhkongquit, kah mꝏ̄sumugqut ummittamwussoh, kah pish neepauweheau mittamwussissoh, anaquabit Jehovah & sephausuen pish wuttinheon wame naumatuonk.
5.31 Kah wosketomp pish chippeu wutch matcheseonganit kah noh mittamwossis pish naiyeutam ummatcheseonk,
6.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
6.2 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, & nag us, Wosketomp asuh mittamwossis, chippeit, quoshomuwadt, Nazarite quoshómuwáonk chippinónt wuhhogkuh en Jehovahut.
6.3 Noh pish chippehtam wutch wineut, kah wutch menuhke wuttattamonganit matta pish wuttattamꝏ̄ see wine, asuh see beer, asuh matta pish wuttattamꝏ̄ ne teague wenomine wuttattamóonk, asuh matta pish meechu wenomineash, uttoh en ogqushke, asuh nu(n)nobpe,
6.4 Wame wun-Nazarite kesukodtumash, matta pish meechu ne teag wajteomuk weenomissippogqut, wutch ubbuhkumunit, yeáan wuhhogkomunit.
6.5 Wame ukkesukodtumash wun-Nazáritse quoshaumuwáonk, matta pish mꝏ̄sumꝏ̄ uppuhkuk, noh pajeh kesukodtash pahshane nnag, ne adt chippinont wuhhogkuh en Jehovahut, pish wunneetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄, ukqunonukquóonk nekinit, ummesunk ut uppuhkukqut.
6.6 Wame kesukodtash ne chabpunont wuhhogkuh en Jehovahut, matta pish pasꝏ̄sukauoou nuppꝏ̄e muhhogkuh.
6.7 Wutche ꝏ̄shoh. asuh wutche ohkasoh, wutche weematoh asuh wutch weetahtu, matta nah ꝏ̄tch nishkeaun wuhhogkuh nuppinit, newutche wun-Nazaritsuꝏ̄onk GOD, ohteau uppuhkukqut.
6.8 Wame wun-Nazaritsue kesukodtumash, noh pish wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄ en Jehovahut.
6.9 Kah howan nuppuk kishke wuhhogkat, kenꝏ̄hque, asq waahteoukup, kah mahche nishketeau wun-Nazaritsue uppuhkuk, neit pish nꝏ̄sum uppuhkuk ne kesukok pahkhet nesausuk tahskikquinogkodtut pish mꝏ̄sum.
6.10 Kah nishwosuk tahshikquinogkok pish pasꝏ̄au neesꝏ̄oh turtlesoh, asuh neesꝏ̄oh wuskuhwhunnannámesoh, en sephausuenúut, ut mukkinneaekommukque squontamut.
6.11 Kah sephausuen pish ayim, pasuk matseae sephausuonk, kah onkatuk chikohtae sephausuonk, kah pish ꝏ̄nauwadtuwáheuh, newutche matchesu ut nuppꝏ̄e muhhogkat, kah pish wunneetupanatamwahto uppuhkuk ne kesukok.
6.12 Kah pish chippeu en Jehovahut, wun-Nazarritse kesukodtumash, kah pish pasꝏ̄au lamboh ne kodtumuk wutch panneseae sephausuonk: kah negonne ukkesukodtumash pish penushaash, newutche wun-Nazaritsuꝏ̄onk nishketeauun.
6.13 Kah yeu Nazaritse naumatuonk, ne kesukok wun-Nazaritsuonk pahshane n nag, pish uppasꝏ̄oh mukkinneae-kommukque squontamut.
6.14 Kah noh pish magꝏ̄ wussephamauáonk Jehovahoh, pasuk nomposhimwe ne kodtumuk lamboh, pannuppeyeuꝏ̄ wutche chikohtáe magꝏ̄onk: kah pasuk squoshimwe ne kodtumuk lambe, pannuppéyeuit, wutche matcheseae magꝏ̄onk: kah pasuk pannuppeyeue ram wutche wunohteáe sephausuonk.
6.15 Kah munnꝏ̄tie mat seane petukqunnegash, pashquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pumme kah mat seane wafersash, sussequnausuash pumme, kah metsue sephausuonk ne noh wadchiik, kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash.
6.16 Kah sephausuen pish uppasꝏ̄che paudtauunash anaquabit Jehovah, kah pish ayim ummatcheseongane sephausuonk, kah wutchikohtae sephausuonk.
6.17 Kah ne pish ram ayim wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuonk en Jehovahut, weeche munnꝏ̄tae mat seane petukqunnegash: kah sephausuen pish ayim ummetsue sephausuonk, kah ꝏ̄tattamꝏ̄e sephausuonk.
6.18 Kah noh Nazarite pish mꝏ̄sum upuhkúk ut tabarnaklee mukkinneáekomukque squotamut, & pish neemunum meesunk wutch muppuhkukqut, & pish upponámun nꝏ̄taut, ne agwe wunohteae sepháusuongane magꝏ̄onganit.
6.19 Kah sephausuen pish nemunau, tôuppuhhosit ramme uhpegk kah pasuk mat seane petukqunnunk, wutch manꝏ̄taut, kah pasuk mat seaninꝏ̄g wafer, kah pish nish upponamunash ummꝏ̄sunutcheganit wun-Nazaritsenin, mahche mꝏ̄suk wun-Nazaritsuꝏ̄onk.
6.20 Kah sephausuen pish nish papaumunnumunash, wutch paupaumenumwae sephausûonk ut anaquabit Jehovah, ne wunnetupanatamwéyeuꝏ̄ wutche sephausuen weeche paupaumenumwe mohpanog, kah tahshinnumwe muhpégq: kah ne mahche noh Nazarit woh wuttattam wine.
6.21 Yeu Nazarite naumatuonk noh quoshóád | ummagꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut, wutche wun-Nazaritsuꝏ̄onk, chaubok ne wunnutcheg pish tapenumꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk: neaunag ukquoshꝏ̄waonk ne quoshoadt, ne pish wutussen, neaunag Nazaritse unnaumatuonk.
6.22 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
6.23 Kenꝏ̄s Aaron kah wunnaumonuh, us yeu pish wuttinne wunnanumoneau wunnaumonuh Israel, nag unnok.
6.24 Jehovah wunnaumukqush, kah nanawehìqush.
6.25 Jehovah wuskesuk wohsumwahukqush, kah kitteamonteanumukqush.
6.26 Jehovah tashinumungqush wuskesuk, kah aninnumungqush wunohteaonk.
6.27 Kah nag pish ponamwog nꝏ̄wesuonk, wunnaumonat Israel, kah nag pish nꝏ̄nanumóog.
7.1 ONk nnih, ne kesukok Moses mahche wunohtunk pummuwutauwaekommuk, ka[n] mahche sussequnuk, kah wunneetupanatamwahteunk, kah wame auwohteaongash nish noh wadchiigish, kah Altar, kah wame auwohteaongash nish noh wadchiigish kah mahche nish sussequnuk, kah nish wunnetupanatamwahtunk.
7.2 Neit magꝏ̄og Israelle Sontimóog wabuhkuhkꝏ̄utcheg ut ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuóut neg Sontimóog ut chadchapanꝏ̄onganehtu yeug nag nanawunoncheg neg agkemómukeg.
7.3 Kah nag paudtóog ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ anaquabit Jehovah: nequtta tahshinash onkwhôsue tatuppequanumukquash kah nabo neesꝏ̄og oxenog pasuk tatuppequanumuk wutch neesꝏ̄og Sontimóog, kah pasuk ox wutche pasuk, kah nag uppasꝏ̄tshanóuh anaquohtag Tabernakle.
7.4 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
7.5 Attumunumok, onk woh nish auwohkonash ut mukkinneáekommukqeu usseonganit, kah nish pish kittinnumauonáash Levitsog, nishnoh wosketomp neaunag wutannôsuonk.
7.6 Kah Moses nemunum tatuppequanumukquash, kah oxenog, kah nish wuttinnumauonash Levitsoh.
7.7 Nesinash tatuppequanumukquash, kah yauog oxenog wuttinnumauonuh wunnaumonuh Gershon, neaunag wutannohsuonganꝏ̄.
7.8 Kah yauunash tatuppequanumukquaash, kah shwosuk tahsuog oxenog wuttinnumauónuh wunnaumonuh Merari, neaunag wutannohsuonganꝏ̄, ut agwe wunnutcheganit Ithamar wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen.
7.9 Qut en wunnaumonat Kohath, wanne wuttinnumauoh, newutche Sanctuarihe aninnohsuonk ne wadchiik wuhhogkaóut, nag | mꝏ̄che upponumunau wuttugkeóont.
7.10 Kah sontimóog magꝏ̄og wutche wunnetupanatamwohtinat Altar, ne kesukok sasequnumuk: kah sontimôog magꝏ̄og ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄, ut anaquohtag Altar.
7.11 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, Pasuk sontim pasuk kesuk, pasuk sontim kesuk, nag pish magꝏ̄og ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄, wutche wunneetupanatamwahteauunat Altar
7.12 Kah noh maguk ummagꝏ̄onk negonne kesukok, noh Naasson wunnaumonuh Aminadab, wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit Judah.
7.13 Kah ummagꝏ̄onk, pasuk silvere wunnonk, nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchag shekelse unne tuhkéquan, pasuk silvere wunnonk, nesausuk tahshinchage shekelse tuhkéquan, nashpe Sanctuarihe shekel, nish naneeswe numwohteau pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee, wutche metsue sephausuonk.
7.14 Pasuk golde wuttamwaitch, piukque shekelse tuhkequan, numwohteau incense,
7.15 Pasuk ox, wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumue lambe, wutche chikohtae magꝏ̄onk.
7.16 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat, wutch goatsut wutche matchesongane sephausuonk.
7.17 Kah wutch wunohteae sephausuonk, nesuog oxenog napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahsuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog, yeu mo ummagꝏ̄onk Naasson wunnaumonuh Amminadab.
7.18 Nahohtôeu kesukok magꝏ̄ Nathaneel wunnaumonuh Zuar, Issachare sontim.
7.19 Noh magou ummagꝏ̄onk, pasuk silvere wunnonk, nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage shekelse tuhkequan, pasuk silvere wunnonk, nesausuk tahshinchag shekelse unuttuhkequan, nashpe Sanctuarihe shekel, naneeswe nish numwohteau pasquag nꝏ̄khik wutche metsue sephausuonk.
7.20 Pasuk golde wuttamwaitch, piogque shekelsuꝏ̄, numwohteau incense,
7.21 Pasuk ox wuskoshim wutche herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumꝏ̄k lamb, wutch chikohtáe magꝏ̄onk
7.22 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch goatsut, wutche matcheseáe sephausuonk,
7.23 Kah wutch wunoht[a]ae sephausue magꝏ̄onk, nesuog oxenog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog[,] napanna tahsuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog yeu mo ummagꝏ̄onk Nathaneel wunnaumonuh Zuaz.
7.24 Nashwe kesukok, wussontimomꝏ̄uh wunnaumonuh Zabulon, Eliab wunnaumonuh Helon.
7.25 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk, nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchag shekelse tuhkéquan, pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage shekelse unnuttuhkéquan nashpe | Sanctuarihe shekel, nish naneeswe numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee wutche meetsue sephausuonk
7.26 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogque shekelse tuhkéquan. numwohteau incensa,
7.27 Pasuk ox, wuskoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kôdtumꝏ̄k lamb, wutche chikohtae magꝏ̄onk.
7.28 Pasuk nomposhimwe goats wutch goatsut, wutche matcheseongane sephausuonk.
7.29 Kah wutch wunohteáe sephausue magꝏ̄onk, neesuog oxenog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahfuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog. yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Eliab wunnaumonuh Helon.
7.30 Yaue kesukok wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Reuben Elizur wunnaumonuh Shedeur.
7.31 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk, nequt pasukꝏ̄e nishwinchage shekelse tuhkéquan; pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage shekelse tuhkéquan nashpe Sanctuarihe shekle: naneeswe numwohteau pasquag nꝏ̄khik, kenugkenausu pummee, wutche meetsue sephausuonk
7.32 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogqueshekelse tuhkéqun, numwohtéau incense
7.33 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumꝏ̄k lamb wutche chikohtae sephausuonk.
7.34 Pasuk nomposhimwe goatsoh wutche matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.35 Kah wutche wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuongash neesuog oxinog napanna tahsuog ramsam, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahsuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsuh, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Elizur wunnaumonuh Shedeur.
7.36 Napanna adtahshikquinogkok wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Simeon Shelumiel wunnaumonuh Zurishaddai.
7.37 Ne ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage shekelse tuhkéquan: pasuk silvere wunnonk, nesausuk tahshinchage shekelse tuhkequan, nashpe Sancturihe shekle, na neeswe numwohteau pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee, wutche meetsue sephausuonk.
7.38 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch, piogque shekelse tuhkequan.
7.39 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk lambe wutche chikohtae sephausuonk.
7.40 Pasuk nomposhimwe goáts wutche matcheseáe sephausuonk,
7.41 Kah wutch wunohteáe magꝏ̄ongane sephausuonk, neesuong oxenog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog napanna tahsuog ne kodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Shelumiel wunnaumonuh Zurishaddai.
7.42 Nequtta tahshikquinogkok, wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Gad, Eliasaph wunnaumonuh Deuel.
7.43 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk filveré wunnonk, nequt pasukꝏ̄e & nishwinchage sheklse unuttuhkequn: pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklese tuhkequn, nashpe Sanctuari[n]e shekle: na neeswe nish numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pumme wutche meetsue sephausuonk.
7.44 Pasuk golde wuttattamwáitch piogque sheklse tuhkequn, numwohteau incense.
7.45 Pasuk ox, wuskoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk lambe wutch chìkohtae sephausuonk.
7.46 Pasuk nomposhim goats wutch matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.47 Kah wutche wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuongash, neesuog oxenog napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog ne kodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Eliasaph wunnaumonuh Deuel.
7.48 Nesausuk adtahshikquinogkok wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Ephraim, Elishama wunnaumonuh Ammi[n]ud.
7.49 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage shekelse tuhkequan, pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage shekelse tuhkéquan, nashpe Sanctuarie shekel & naneeswe numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄hkhik kenugkenausu pumme, wutche meetsue sephausuonk.
7.50 Pasuk golde wuttattumwaitch, piogque shekelse tuhkéquan, numwohteau incense.
7.51 Pasuk ox wuskoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambe, wutch chikohtáe sephausuonk,
7.52 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch goatsut, wutch matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.53 Kah wutche wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuongash, nesuog oxinog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanne tahsuog nekodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Elishama wunnaumonuh Amihud.
7.54 Shwosuk adtahshìkquinogkok, wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Manasses, Gamaleel wunnaumonuh Pedahzer.
7.55 Ummakꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk[,] nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage sheklese tuhkequn; pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklese tuhkequn, tashpe Sanctuariehe shekelsash. naneeswe numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pumme wutche meetsue sephausuonk:
7.56 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch, piogque sheklese tuhkequn, numwohteau ìncense.
7.57 Pasuk óx wushkoshim wutch heardut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk lamb wutch chikohtae sephausuonk,
7.58 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch goatsut wutch matcheseae sephausuonk:
7.59 Kah wutch wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuonk, nesuog oxinog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahsuog ne kadtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Gamaleel wunnaumonuh Pedahzur.
7.60 Pasukꝏ̄gun adtahshik quinogkok wussontimꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Benjamin Abidan wunnaumonuh Gidioni.
7.61 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage sheklse tuhkequn: pasuk wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklse tuhkequn neaunag Sanctuarie shekle, naneeswe numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee wutch meetsue sephausuonk.
7.62 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogque sheklse tohkequn, numwohteau incense.
7.63 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk Lamb wutch chikohtae sephausuonk.
7.64 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch goatsut, wutch matcheseae sephausuonk:
7.65 Kah wutch wunohteae magꝏ̄ongane sephausuonk, nesuog oxinog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napannatahsuog ne kodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Abidan wunnaumonuh Gideoni.
7.66 Piogquenuꝏ̄uk kesukod wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Dan: Ahiezer wunnaumonuh Ammishaddai.
7.67 Neumagꝏ̄onk, pasuk silvere wunnonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e, kah nishwinchage sheklse tuhkequn silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklse tuhkequn, nashpe Sanctuarie shekle na neeswe numwohtaash pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee wutch meetsue sephausuonk.
7.68 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogque shekelse tuhkequan numwohteau incense.
7.69 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kadtumuk lámbe wutch chikohtae sephausuonk.
7.70 Pasuk nomposhim goat, wutch matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.71 Kah wutche wunnohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuongash, nesuog oxinog, napa[x]na tahsuog ramsog napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog napanna tahsug ne kodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Ahiezer, wunnaumonuh Ammishaddai,
7.72 Nabo nequt kesukod wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Aser: Pagiel wunnaumonuh Ocran.
7.73 Ummagꝏ̄onk, pasuk silvete wunnonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage sheklse tuhkequn: pasuk silvere wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklse tuhkequn nashpe Sanotarihe shekle: naneeswe numwohteau pasquag | nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee wutche meetsue sephausuonk.
7.74 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogque sheklse tunkequán numwohteau incense.
7.75 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk lamb wutch chìkohtae sephausuonk.
7.76 Pasuk nomposhimwe goats wutch goatsut wutch matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.77 Kah wutch wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuonk, nesuog oxinog, napannatahsuog ramsog, napanna tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahsuog ne kodtumuk lambsog, yeu ummagꝏ̄onk Pagiel wunnaumonuh Ocran.
7.78 Naboneese kesukok wussontimomꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Naphtali, Ahira, wunnaumonuh Enan.
7.79 Ummagꝏ̄onk pasuk silvere wunnonk nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah nishwinchage sheklse tuhkequn: pasuk silvere wunnónk nesausuk tahshinchage sheklse tuhkequn, nashpe Sanctuarihe shekle: na neeswe numwohteau pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee wutch meetsue sephausuonk.
7.80 Pasuk golde wuttattamwaitch piogque shekelse tuhkequan numwohteau incense
7.81 Pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, pasuk ne kodtumuk lamb, wutch chikohsue sephausuonk.
7.82 Pasuk nomposhim goat wutch goatsut wutch matcheseae sephausuonk.
7.83 Kah wutch wunohteae magꝏ̄e sephausuonk, nesuog oxinog, napanna tahsuog ramsog, napana tahsuog nomposhimwe goatsog, napanna tahsuog ne kodtumuk lambsog ne ummagꝏ̄onk Ahira wunnaumonuh Enan.
7.84 Yeu mo wunneetupantamwatóônk Altar, ne kesukok sasequnômuk, nashpe Israele Sontimoog, nabonenash silvere wanishkechuash, & nabanenash silvere wunonkanash, nabonenash golde wuttattamwaitchuash.
7.85 Nish noh silver wanishkidj nequt pasukꝏ̄e & nishwinchag sheklse unuttuhkequan, kah nish noh wunnonk nesausuk tahshinchag, wame silvere wishquash, neese muttannungane, kah yauut pasukꝏ̄e shekelse unnuttuhkequnash, nashpe Sanctuarihe shekel.
7.86 Golde wuttattamwaitchuash naboneesinash numwohtau ìnnense: nish noh wuttattamwaitch piogque shekelse unuttuhkequan, nashpe Sanctuarihe shekel, wame golde wuttattamwaitchuash, nequt pasukꝏ̄e kah neesneechage shekelsash.
7.87 Wameoxenok wutche chikohteae magꝏ̄onk, nabo nesuog oxenog, ramsog nabonesuog, ne kodtumwe lambsog nabo nesuog kah meetsue wussephausuonganꝏ̄: kah nomposhimwe goatsog, wutch goatsut nabo nesuog wutche matcheseáe sephausuonk.
7.88 Kah oxenog wutché wunohteáe maꝏ̄e sephausuonk, neesnechagodtog kah | yauog oxenog, ramsog nequtta tahshinchagodtog, nomposhimwe goatsog nequtta tahshinchagkodtog, ne kôdtumuk lambsog nequtta tahshinchagkodtog: yeu mo wunnetupanatamwahtóonk Altar, mahche sussequnnumuk.
7.89 Kah Moses petutteadt, en mukkinneáe kommukqut, keketꝏ̄kauónat, neit nꝏ̄tam ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk ukkenꝏ̄nukqun, wutch waabe abuhquosik monaneteae appuonganit, ne waabese wauwae Arkut, wutch nanashaue neesuog Cherubimsog: kah ukkenꝏ̄nuh.
8.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
8.2 Kenꝏ̄s Aaron kah us, nashqussuman lampsash, nesausuk tahshinash lampsash pish woh sumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash papiuhsukeh wuskesukqut wequanantéganuhtug.
8.3 Kah Aaron wutussen, nashqussumup lampsash, papiuhsuke wequananteganuhtug neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh,
8.4 Kah yeu wequananteganuhtugque anakausuonk, ne golde sukquthausue anakausuonk, ne annunneg, kah nish uppeshauunash ne mo sukquehthausue anakausuonk, neaunag ne kuhkinneasuonk, ne Jehovah kohkꝏ̄tomauont Mosesoh, ne wuttinteauun wequananteganuhtug.
8.5 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
8.6 Nemun Levitsog wutch kenugke wunnaumonuh Israel, kah nag pahkeh.
8.7 Kah yeu pish kittinheoneau, nag pahkheadt. nag seauhkau pahkhuwae nippe, kah mꝏ̄sumwaéhquok pomushaumꝏ̄utch matuhquábit, kah kutchissittauhettich wuthogkꝏ̄unꝏ̄oash, kah pahkheahettich wuhhogkaóuh.
8.8 Kah nag nemunáhettach oxenoh wushkoshim wutch herdut, kah metsue sephausuonk ne ne wadchiik, pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pumme, kah nahohtoeu bullok wushkoshim wutch herdut. noh pish kenemun, wutch matcheseáe sephausuonk,
8.9 Kah pish kuppasꝏ̄chuun Levitsog, anaquohtag mukkinneáe kommuk, kah pish kummóunum mamusse mukkinneonk wunnaumonuh Israel.
8.10 Kah pish kuppasꝏ̄chuun Levitsog, anaquabit Jehovah, kah wunnaumonuh Israel pish ponamwog wunnutcheganoash ut Levitsut.
8.11 Kah Aaron pish paupaumunau Levitsoh, wutche paupaumenumwáe sephausuonk anaquabit Jehovah, wussephausuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, onk nag woh usseog waussumáonk Jehovah.
8.12 Keh Levitsog pish ponamwog wunnutcheganóash uppuhkukꝏ̄óut bulloksog, kah pish pasuk matcheseongane sephausuonk, kah onkatog chikohtae sephausuonk en Jehovahut, wunnauwadtheónat Levitsog.
8.13 Kah ken pish kuppon Levitsog anaquabit Aaron, kah anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh kah nag pish kuttahtashinóog wutche tahtoshinumwe sephausuonk en Jehovahut.
8.14 Kah pish kutchippin Levitsog wutch kenugke wunnaumonat Israel, kah Levitsog pish nuttaiheog.
8.15 Kah ne mahche n nag, Levitsog pish petutteaog aninnumwontamunat mukkinneaekommuk, kah nag pish kuppahkheóog, kah pish kꝏ̄wahwaabenoog wutch waabinnumwe sephausuonk.
8.16 Newutche magunóe nuttinnumonteanunk, wutche kenugke wunnaumónat Israel nompe neg woshwunukeg nishnoh ôontomuk nompe nishnoh mohtommegit ut wame wunnaumonat Israel, nag nunnemunnumonog.
8.17 Newutche nishnoh mohtommegit ut Israel noh nuttaihe, wosketomp kah puppinashim: ne kesukok tógkomog nishnoh mohtomegit ut ohkit Egypt, nag nꝏ̄neetupanatamwahteonápaneg.
8.18 Kah neemun Lévitsog wutch nompe nishnoh mohtomegit wutch wunnaumonat Israel,
8.19 Kah magꝏ̄e nummag Levitsog, en Aaronut, kah en wunnaumónat, wutch kenugke wunnaumonat Israel, ussenat ꝏ̄wawussummuwaongane wunnaumonuh Israel, ut mukkinneaekomukqut, kah ayimunat wunnauwadtuonk wutch wunnaumonuh Israel, onk woh matta enninneaonganinno, ut kenugke wunnaumonat Israel, wunnaumonuh Israel pasꝏ̄sukommohettit Sactuari.
8.20 Neit Moses kah Aaron, kah wame mukkinneonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, wuttinheoneau Levitsoh neaunag wame wutannꝏ̄naonk Jehovah Mosesoh, papaume Levitsog, ne nah wuttinheoneau wunnaumonuh Israel.
8.21 Kah Levitsog pahkesupáneg, kah kutchissittóog wuthogꝏ̄unóash, & Aaron nah uppaupaumenuh, wutch paupaumenumwe sephausuonk ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah Aaron nah ꝏ̄nauwadtheuh pahkheonat.
8.22 Kah ne mahche nnag, Levitsog pétutteáog ussenat wutusseonganꝏ̄, ut mukkinneaekomukqut, anaquabit Aaron kah anâquabenit wunnaumonuh, neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh, papaume Levitsog, ne nan wuttinheoneau.
8.23 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
8.24 Yeu unnaumatuonk wutch Levitsog: wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunnaóot kah napanna kah paameu, noh pish petutteau ayeuuhkontamwe ayeuuhkontamunat, | ut mukkinneaekommukque usseonganit.
8.25 Kah napanna tahshinchâg kodtumwohkomunat, pish qushkeu wutch ayeuuhkonittue usseonganit, kah matta pish wonk aninnohse.
8.26 Qut noh pish áninnohsu kenugke wemadut, ut mukkinneaekomukqut- nanawehtenat umeechumuhkonittuonk, kah noh matta pish usseu aninnohsuonk, kah yeu pish unnnheoneau Levitsog ut meechumuhkonaonganꝏ̄wóut.
9.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh ut touohkomukqut Sinai, ut negonne nepauz, nahohtoe ne kodtumuk, mahche sohhamwehettit wutch ohkeit Egypt, nꝏ̄wau.
9.2 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel ussehetich paumukoittuonk, ut wutahquompiyeume kuhquttumꝏ̄onganit.
9.3 Nabo yau qunohhog yeuoh nepauz, nanashauwe neesit wunnonkꝏ̄ut, pish kutusseneau, ut wutahquompiyeume kuhquttumꝏ̄onganit, neaunag wame nish kuhquttumꝏ̄ongash, kah neaunag wame nish wussittumꝏ̄ongash ne wadchiigish, pish kutusseneau.
9.4 Kah Moses kenꝏ̄nau wunnaumonuh Israel ussenat paumukóadtuonk.
9.5 Kah nag wutusseneau paumukkôadtuonk ut negonne nepauz, naho yauquinohhog nô nepauz, nanashauwe ut neese wunnonkꝏ̄ut, ut touohkomukqut Sinai, neaunag wame wutannꝏ̄naonk Jehovah Mosesoh, ne wutusseneau wunnaumonuh Israel
9.6 Kah na mo nawhutch wosketompaog nag nishkeneunkqussitcheg nashpe nuppꝏ̄hogkuh onk wutonteauunneau ussenat paumukôadtuonk ne kesukok kah nag pasꝏ̄sukauog Mosesoh kah Aaronoh ne kesukok.
9.7 Kah yeug wosketompaog wuttinôuh, Nenawun nunnishkeneunkqussimun náshpe nuppꝏ̄hog, tohwaj wuttamhetteaog, matta nummagꝏ̄unnanónut magꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut, ut ukkuhquttumwe ahquompiyeumut, ut kenugke wunnaumonat Israel?
9.8 Kah Moses nah wuttinuh, Chequnikkompauꝏ̄k, kah nukkehkitteu uttoh anannꝏ̄teamwit Jehovah papaume kenaau.
9.9 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesah nꝏ̄wau,
9.10 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel nꝏ̄wash, Howan wosketomp kenaau nishkeneunkqussit nashpe ahchunkquoh asuh nôꝏ̄sukongqueog ut pomushaonganit. ut kuppometuonganꝏ̄óut; onch pish ussu paumukôadtuonk en Jehovahut.
9.11 Ut nahohtôeu nepauz, ut nabo yauquinogkodtut, ut nanashauwe neeswe wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ut, nag pish wutusseneau nashpe mat seane petukqunnunk, kah weesadtippogquosh, | nag pish ummeechineau.
9.12 Matta pish nô wutch ushqushteamꝏ̄un nô pajeh mohtompanit, kah nag matta pish ponquanumóog woskon, neaunag nish noh paumukôadtue kuhkꝏ̄waonk, ne pish wutusseneau.
9.13 Qut wosketomp noh pahkesit, kah noh matta pomushauꝏ̄, kah mukkꝏ̄n(a)g ussenat paumukôadtuonk, noh ketéahogkou pish tummetahwhau wutch ummissinninneumut, newutche matta magꝏ̄ mꝏ̄gꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut ukkuhkꝏ̄wáe ahquompiyeumut, noh wosketomp pish naiyeutam ummatcheseonk.
9.14 Kah penꝏ̄wót enneapeyont kuhhogkaóut, kah usseit paumukóadtuonk en Jehovahut, neaunag paumukôadtue kuhkꝏ̄waonk, kah neaunag wussittumꝏ̄ongash ne wadchiigish; ne pish wutussen, pish nont k(e)nukqut ohtomꝏ̄ kuhkꝏ̄waonk, naneeswe wutch penuwot kah kohtohteaekit.
9.15 Kah ne kesukok Tabernakle mahche wunohtomuk, matohkqs nuhkuhkom Tabernakle kah wauwáe weetu; kah ut ne wanonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄k, na mo woskeche Tabernakleut, onatuh nôquok nꝏ̄teau, nó pajeh mohtompanit.
9.16 Ne nagwutteae n nih, mahtokqs wunuhkukkomun, kah nógquodt ut nꝏ̄teau nukoneau.
9.17 Kah matokqs, tohshinumuk wutch woskeche kommuk, ne mahche n nag, wunnaumonuh Israel pomusháoh, kah ná ayeuonganit matokqs ohtag, na wuttuppukkussinuneau wunnaumonuh Israel.
9.18 Ne anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah. wunnaumonuh Israel pomusháoh, kah ne anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah tuppukfinwog, wame kesukodtam matokqs ohtag woskeche Tabernakleut, ne wuttinne tuppuksunnunneau.
9.19 Kah mahtokqs sepohtag Tabernakleut mꝏ̄chetikquinne, neit wunnaumonuh Israel, nanawehteaog ummeechumuhkausuwáonk Jehovah, kah matta pomushauꝏ̄og.
9.20 Kah nish mattokqs ogguhsequinohtag Tabernakleut, neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄wâonk Jehovah, ne wuttinne tuppukfinneau, kah neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah, ne wuttinne pomushoneau.
9.21 Onk nnih matokqs ohtag wutch wunnonkꝏ̄ut nô pajeh mohtompanit, kah maaokqs waapenumun mohtompanae neit nag pomushaog, asuh kesukodáe asuh nukkonáeu matokqs waapenumuk neit nag pomusháog.
9.22 Asuh neese kesukquae, asuh pasuk nepàuz, asuh nequt kodtumwáe, matokas sepohtag Tabernâkleut woskeche ohtaut wunnaumonuh Israel tuppuksinwog, kah matta pomushauóog, qut waapenumuk, neit pomusháog.
9.23 Ne anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah nag tuppuksinwog, kah ne anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah, nag pomusháog, | nag nanawehteauog ummeechumuhkausuwáonk Jehovah, ut wuttꝏ̄nut Jehovah, nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses.
10.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
10.2 Ayimush neesinash silvere monopuhpéquonash, sukquéhthausue anakausuonk pish nish kutayimunash; kah nish pish môe wehquetumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ mukkinneunk, kah pomushaumꝏ̄ut tuppuksinꝏ̄wongash
10.3 Kah nag pish uppuhpequohtináoash, & wame mukkinneonk pish kummoáe peyogquog, ut mukkineae-kommukque squontamut.
10.4 Kah pasuk puhpequohtómuk, neit Sontimóog, wábuhkuhkꝏ̄utcheg Israelle muttannonkanogkussuog, nag pish kummoáe peyóquog
10.5 Kah puhpequóhtamóg wame quoshwéonk, neit wutchepwoáe tuppuksinnowongash pis monchémꝏ̄oash.
10.6 Kah nahohtoeu puhpequontamꝏ̄k wamequoshwéonk, neit Sóanae tuppuksinnowongash pish monchemoash, nag pish puhpequontamwog, wamequoshwéonk wutche ummoncheonganꝏ̄oash.
10.7 Kah moéóg mukkinneonk, pish kuppuhpequomwꝏ̄, kah matta pish kuppuhpequontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wamequashwéonk.
10.8 Kah wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuenuog, pish puhpequohtóog monopuhpequonash kah ne pish wutche micheme kuhkꝏ̄waonk, wutche kenaau, pannuppe kuppometuonganꝏ̄wóut.
10.9 Kah ayeuteaag ut kutohtuout, ayeuuhkone mukkꝏ̄kenuaenin, noh matchenehikqueyog, neit pish kuppuhpequontamumwꝏ̄ wame quashweonk nashpe monopuhpequonash kah pishkummequontamunneau, ut anaquabit Jehovah kummanittꝏ̄mwꝏ̄, kah pish kꝏ̄wadchanitteamwꝏ̄ wutch kummatwomꝏ̄wóut.
10.10 Kah ut kꝏ̄wekontamwe kesukodtumꝏ̄wout, kah ut kukkuhkꝏ̄wae mishadtuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wout, kah ut weske kutchissik kenepauzsômꝏ̄óog, neit kish kuppukpequohtomwꝏ̄ kummonopuhpéquonnꝏ̄oash, ut waabese, kutchikkohtae magꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wout, kah ut waabese kꝏ̄nohteáe magꝏ̄e sepbausuosuonganꝏ̄wóut, & nish pish wutch kummehquontamwahukqunnâoash, ut anaquabit kum-Manittmmwꝏ̄, nen Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mwꝏ̄.
10.11 Kah nnih, nahohtóeu kodtumꝏ̄k, ut nahohtôeu nepauz, ut wunneesneechadtikkunhamunat nepauz, matokqs waápenumunat wutch woskeche wauwaekommukqut.
10.12 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel monchéog en wuttauonganꝏ̄óut, wutch touohkomukqut Sinai, kah matokqs anwohsinꝏ̄mꝏ̄ ut | tauohkomukqut Pharan.
10.13 Kah nag moncheog ne wuske, neaunag wuttinnꝏ̄waunk Jehovah, nashpe wunnutcheg Moses.
10.14 Kah ummuttaakinne wuttuppukkussinnꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Judah, negonne moncheog, ukkenauwameonganꝏ̄oash, kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk Naasson wunnaumonuh Amminadab.
10.15 Kah noh nanauunuk kenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Ishachar, noh Nathaneel wunnaumonuh Zuar.
10.16 Kah nanauwunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Z[]bulon, noh Eliab wunnaumonuh Helon.
10.17 Kah pummewuttauwae-kommuk mo nꝏ̄kenumun: kah wunnaumonuh Gershon kah wunnaumonuh Merari, moncheog kenunnumwog pummuwuttauwae-kommuk.
10.18 Kah ummuttaakunne tuppuksinnꝏ̄onk Ruben moncheog, neaunag ukkenauwameonganꝏ̄ash, kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk; noh Elizur wunnaumonuh Shedeur.
10.19 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Simeon, noh Shelumiel wunnaumonuh Zurishaddai.
10.20 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippannꝏ̄onk wunnnaumonuh Gad noh Eliasaph wunnaumonuh Deguel,
10.21 Kah Kohathitsog moncheog kenunnumwog wunnetupanatamweyeukish, kah nâg weekitteáog pummuwuttauwáekommuk, quoshauwe yeu uppeyónaóut
10.22 Ummuttaákinne tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonk wunnaumonuh Ephraim moncheog neáunag ukkenauwameonganꝏ̄ash: kah noh nanáwunuk ukkenauwámeonk noh Elishama wunnaumonuh Ammihud.
10.23 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Manasses, noh Gamaliel wunnaumonuh Pedazur,
10.24 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Benjamin, noh Abidan wunnaumonuh Gjdioni.
10.25 Kah ummuttaákinne tuppukfinnꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Dan moncheog, wuttat waágig kenugke wame tuppukfinnꝏ̄wongash pannuppe ukkenauwameonganꝏ̄: kah noh nanauwunuk ukkenauwameonk, noh Ahiezer wunnaumonuh Ammishaddai.
10.26 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Asher, noh Pagiel wunnaumonuh Ocran.
10.27 Kah noh nanawunuk ukkenauwameonk wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Naphthali, noh Ahira wunnaumonuh Enan.
10.28 Yeush uppomushaonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Israel, neaunag ukkenauwameonanꝏ̄oash, monchehettit.
10.29 Kah Moses unnau Hobaboh wunnaumonuh Reguel um-Midianite, w(a)senumonche | Moses: kutómun ayeuonganit, ne papaume Jehvvah anꝏ̄wop, kuttinnumauununneau, weechaiinnean kah pish kꝏ̄nenehennumun, newutche Jehovah wunneyeuꝏ̄p papaume Israel.
10.30 Kah wuttinuh, matta nummonchꝏ̄h: qut en nutohkit, kah nuttinnonkumóut nuttom.
10.31 Kah nꝏ̄wau, kꝏ̄wehquetumoush, ahque nukkossinnan, newutche kꝏ̄wohteoh nuttupkussinnꝏ̄wonganunnónash touohkomuk, onk woh ken nꝏ̄skesukkumun kuhnog.
10.32 Kah pish n nih, wecchaiyeog, nux pish n nih ne wanegik Jehovah pisn anhukqueog, nenawun wonk pish kꝏ̄nenehennumun.
10.33 Kah nag moncheog wutch ꝏ̄wadchumut Jehovah, nish ukkesukquae pomushaonk: kah ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waongane wut-Arkum Jehovah, negonshauog, yeush nishikkesukquáeu pomus[n]aonk, wunnatinneahamauónat nah anwósinóonk.
10.34 Kah ummatokqussum Jehovah nag wunohkukkongqunneau kesukodaeu, monchehettit wutch tuppuksinnowonganit.
10.35 Kah n nih, Ark monchemꝏ̄ug, Moses nꝏ̄wau, omohkish, Jehovah, ka[h] kummatwomog seaéhettich, kah neg sekeneunkquéaneg wussemohettich wutch anaquabean
10.36 Kah anwôhshitteaumuk, nꝏ̄wau qushkish Jehovah, en Israelle piogque momuttannonganog kussuog.
11.1 KAh missinninnuog mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄skꝏ̄âhettit, neg matcheseog ut wehtauogkut Jehovah, kah Jehovah nꝏ̄tam, kah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk nashqunau, kah nꝏ̄teau wutch Jehovahut, nashqunau ut kenugke nahoh, kah nah ummahchukkeswôh, nah unquáe tuppuksinnowonganit.
11.2 Kah missinninnuog mauunnittauáog Mosesoh, kah Moses peantamauau Jehovah, kah nꝏ̄tau quttauémꝏ̄.
11.3 Kah ne ayeuonk wuttissowetamun Taberah, newutche wunnꝏ̄tom Jehovah nashquneau ut kenugke nahoh.
11.4 Kah kanukke muttaanukeg, neg noh kanukkushoncheg, kodtantamôe matchekodtantamwog: kah wonk wunnaumonuh Israel, qushkeog kah môog, kah nꝏ̄wáog, howan woh kutassamhukqun weyaus, mechinat?
11.5 Nummehquánumômun namohsog neg mꝏ̄whakutcheg ut Egypt, wutche monteag askꝏ̄tasquash, kah monaskꝏ̄tasquash, kah leeksash, kah weenuwasog, kah garlick.
11.6 Qut yeuyeunukketeahogkóunun nannàssu, yeu wanne teag, webe nuskesukqunnonash en Manna ut:
11.7 Kah Manna mo ogqueneunkquodt Coriandere wuskannemunneat, kah ne áunak | onatuh ne áunak Bdeliam.
11.8 Missinninnug popomsháog, kah ummukkinnumuneau, kah wuttoghumunneau ut togguhwhonggnit, asuh wussukquttahhamuneau ut togguhwhonganit, kah wuttappóunneau pannehtu, kah uppetukqunnonganuhkoneau, kah ne âshpukquok ogkuhpukquan wuske pummei(t).
11.9 Kah nehchippog panshunk ut tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit nukkonáe, ne Mánna uppogsummꝏ̄wontamun.
11.10 Kah Moses nꝏ̄tam ummauonganꝏ̄ missinninnuog pannuppe wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄óut, nishnoh pasuk ut weeke squontamut, kah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk Jehovah mishe nashqunneau, kah ut wuskesukqut Moses ne matchit.
11.11 Kah Moses unnau Jehovah tohwhutch matchenéheadt kittinneum, kah tohwutch matta namehteoꝏ̄ kitteamonteanittûonk ut kuskesukqut woh kupponamiinneat wuttuhkequnnꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wame yeug missinninnuog?
11.12 Sun wame yeug nꝏ̄neechaninneunk? yeug nunneechanunk; waj woh ussean, neg kénun ut kuppꝏ̄chenauónut, onatuh nanukkehteoassuwae wutꝏ̄shimau kónunnont nꝏ̄nukke mukkiesoh, en ohkeit ne chadchekei(m)op wutꝏ̄shimóog.
11.13 Uttoh woh nꝏ̄tahtauun weyaus nutassammón(a)óont wame ycug missinninnuog? newutche neg nummauunnitteunkquog, nꝏ̄waog, assaminnean weyaus onk woh nummetsimun.
11.14 Matta nuttapenummo nen nusse nehenwonche nukkenunnonat wame yeug missinninnuog, newutche wussaume tuhkequnwog wutche nen.
11.15 Kah yeu néhean, nusheh kꝏ̄wehquetumoush nusheh, namehteauon kitteamonteanittuonk ut kuskesqukqut, kah ahque naumutti nummatchetowonk.
11.16 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, mukkinnumah nesausuk tahshinchagkodtog wosketompaog wutch Elderse wunnaumonat Israel, neg waheadcheg, neg Eldersog wutch missinninnuut, kah wutannohsueneumꝏ̄uh, kah nag pasꝏ̄ ut mukkinneae kommukqut onk woh na kuttit weechekompaumukqunneau.
11.17 Kah mos nunnꝏ̄kem, kah mos naut kukkenꝏ̄nsh, nuhnꝏ̄tin nashauanit noh apehtunkquean, kah nag pish nupponamauwonáoh kah nag pish kꝏ̄weeche kenunnummómukquog wuttuhkequnnꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ missinninnuog, kah matta pish kenusse kenunnumꝏ̄un.
11.18 Kah us missinninnúog, Wunneetupanatamwahuk kuhhogkaóog wutche saup, kah pish kummeechumwꝏ̄ weyaus; newutche kummaumwꝏ̄ en wuhtauogkut, Jehovah kussimwꝏ̄, Howan assamhukqueog weyaus | mechinat, newutche nꝏ̄niyimunnónup ut Egypt, newajeh Jehovah assamukqueog weyaus, kah pis(h) kummetsimwꝏ̄.
11.19 Matta pish kummetsimwꝏ̄ pasuk kesuk asuh neesukkesukquáe, asuh napanna tahshe kesukquáe, asuh piogkukquinne, asuh neesneechatikquinne.
11.20 Nô pajeh mamusse nepauzsaut, nô pajeh sohhhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk wutch kutchanꝏ̄wout, kah uhquanittamok, newutche kutjishanumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ Jehovah, no(h) weamukshôóg kah kummaumwop ut anaquabit, kussimwop, Tohwutch sohhamog wutch Egypt?
11.21 Kah Moses nꝏ̄wau, Missinninnúok neg weamukshóuneg, neg nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganogkussuog mahtsitâushacheg, kah kussip nutassamoog weyaus, kah nag pish ummecheneau mamusse nepauz.
11.22 Sun woh floksog kah herdsog nehtauonáoh noh wussohkomꝏ̄nónat? asuh sun pish wame ketahhannâmaquog miayéog wutche nag wamepwuhheonóut?
11.23 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, sun Jehovah wunnutcneg nano tiohqui[?] yeuyeu woh kenaum, uttoh woh nuttinnꝏ̄waonk aunak wutche ken, asuh matta.
11.24 Kah Moses sohham, kah unnau missinninnúh wuttinnꝏ̄waongash Jehovah, kah mouneau nesausuk tahshinchagkodtoh wosketompoh, wutch wunnanannuaénumꝏ̄oh missinninnuog, kah ꝏ̄weénekompauwéheuh wetuómut.
11.25 Kah Jehovah nꝏ̄keu ut matokqs, kah ukkenꝏ̄nuh, kah noh wuttinau nashauanittꝏ̄h neh apehtunkqutcheh, kah ummagunuh en nesausuk tahshinchagkodtog wosketompaog, nananuwacheg, kah nnih nashauanit nah apehtáuont, nag quosháe missohhamwog kah matta wutahqueteauꝏ̄uneau.
11.26 Kah nesuog yeug wosketompaog appuog tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit, pasuk ussowesu Eldad, kah nahohtôeu ussowesu Medad, kah nashauanlt nah wutapehtauoh, kah nag mo wasukuhwhôsitcheg qut matta sohhamóog én Tabernakleut, kah nag quoshae missohhamwog ut tuppuksinowonganit.
11.27 Kah wusken quogqueu, kah wuttinnon Mosesoh, kah nꝏ̄wau, Eldad kah Medad quoshae missohhamwog ut tuppukssinnꝏ̄wonganit.
11.28 Kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun, wuttinneumoh Moses, pasukꝏ̄ tapeneauoncheh ꝏ̄skeneumoh, nampꝏ̄ham kah nꝏ̄wau, Nussontimom Moses, nag queihtus.
11.29 Kah Moses wuttinuh, Sun kutishkauôs newutche nen? woi napehnont wame Jehovah ummissinninnúmoh Manittowompahettit, onk wuh Jehovah wunnashauanittꝏ̄moh upponanumauoh.
11.30 Kah Moses nehenwonche mukkinneu en tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit, nagum kah Israelle Eldetsog.
11.31 Kah na ꝏ̄tch sohhamun waban wutch Jehova(h)ut, kah pasꝏ̄au quailsoh wutch ketahhannit, kah uppogsumwaheuh tuppuksinnowonganit nequttekesukquae pomushaonganit, yeu nogque wutch, kah nequttekesukquâe pomushaonganit ne nogque wutch, waeénu tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit: kah papaume neesisquanogkodtut, wutch waábe wosketohkit.
11.32 Kah missinninnuog neepóog nehteáge ne kesukok, kah wompanne ne nohkog, kah nehteáge na wonk kesukok, kah nag mukkinaog quailsoh, noh ogguhse mukkinont, mukkinnum piogque Omersash, kah sussuksumwe wussussukkussumóuh wutche nagumau waééne tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit.
11.33 Weyaus ash ohtag nashauwe meepit ut, asquam pasquodtamꝏ̄muk, ummusquantamꝏ̄onk Jehovah ayeuuhkonittue nashqunnag wutch missinninnúog, kah Jehovah togkomau missinninnúh, nashpe ahche mishe enninneaonk.
11.34 Kah ne wutussowetamun ayeuonk, Kibroth-hattaavah, newutche na wuttit posekinnóneau missinninnúh neh matchekodtontamunutcheh.
11.35 Wutche Kibroth-hattaavah, missinninnúog moncheog en Hazeroth, kah nag áyeuog Hazeroth.
12.1 KAh Miriam kah Aaron ayeuuhkonittue kenꝏ̄naog Mosesoh, newutche Ethiopiane mittamwossis neh wetauómoncheh, newutche wetauomau Ethiopiane mittamwossissoh.
12.2 Kah nag nꝏ̄waog, Sun Jehovah ketꝏ̄hkau, wunnamuhkut webe nashpe Mosesoh? sunnummatta wonk nashpe kenawun kuttꝏ̄kauàu? Kah Jehováh wunnꝏ̄tamun.
12.4 Kah Jehovah tiadche unnau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh kah Miriamoh, Sohhamꝏ̄k kenaau nishwe en mukkinneáekommukqut, kah nag nishwe sohhamwog.
12.5 Kah Jehovah nꝏ̄keu ut neepattunkquonkane matokqsut, kah neepau ut tabe[r]nacle wetuóme squontamut, kah wehkomau Aaronoh kah Miriamoh, kah nag neeswe sohhamwog.
12.6 Kah nꝏ̄wau, yeuyeu nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k nuttinnꝏ̄waongash, na apit manittowomp kenugke kenaau, nen Jehovah pish nꝏ̄wáhteauwah ut monamansuonganit, pish nukkinnꝏ̄n ut unnukquomuonganit.
12.7 Nuttunneum Moses matta ne wuttinnie(n), noh pabuhtanumukqussu ut wame nekit.
12.8 Ut mamuttꝏ̄nut pish nukkinnꝏ̄n, ut | monomansinneat, kah matta ut nupwóaonganehtu, kah wuttinnussuonk Jehovah noh pish naum, tohwaj matta wabeseóg áyeuuhkone kenꝏ̄nonat nuttinneum Moses?
12.9 Kah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk Jehovah ayeuuhkone nashqunneau wutche nagoh, kah moncheu.
12.10 Kah matokqs amaemo wutch wetuómut, kah kusseh Miriam wutchekꝏ̄ onatuh kꝏ̄nit, kah Aaron moneauau Miriam, kah kusseh noh wutchekꝏ̄.
12.11 Kah Aaron unnau Mosesoh, Woi nussontimom kꝏ̄wehquetumous[n], ahque ponamaiinnean matcheseonk, ne nashpe mattammagwe usseog, kah ne adt matcheseog,
12.12 {Koowehquetumoush} ahque onatuh(h)ꝏ̄utch pasuk napuk, noh so(h)hog wutch ohkasoh wutóontomuk, papohshe weyaus mohtupaémo.
12.13 Kah Moses mauunnitteauau Jehovah nꝏ̄wau, Woi GOD kenanompassumsh noh neetskeh yeuyeu.
12.14 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, kah ꝏ̄shoh, suhquontamwe suhquontog wuskesuk, sunnummatta woh akodchu nesausuk tahshikquinnu? kuppohwhunaj wutch tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit nesausuk tahshikquinne, kah ompetak pethimukinunaj.
12.15 Kah Miriam kuppohwhau wutch tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit nesausuk tahshikquinne, káh miffinninnuog matta pomushauꝏ̄og, nô pajeh Miriam wonk pethimukkinnónat,
12.16 Kah ompetak missinninnuog pomusháog wutch Hazeroth, kah tuppuksinwog ut touohkomukqut Pharan.
13.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
13.2 Annꝏ̄s wosketompaog onk woh natinneohkontamwog ohke Kanaan ne anumauog wunnaumonuh Israel. papasuk wosketomp wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit ꝏ̄shoh, pish kutannꝏ̄numwꝏ̄ nishnoh pasuk nanánuwaen en kenugke nagoh.
13.3 Kah Moses nah wutannꝏ̄noh wutch Pharane touohkomukqut, ne anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah, wame yeug wosketompaog uppuhkukꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh Israel.
13.4 Kah yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit Reuban Shammua wunnaumonuh Zaccur.
13.5 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit Simeon, Shaphat wunnaumonuh Hori.
13.6 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit Judah, Caleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh.
13.7 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onganit Issachar, Jigal wunnaumonuh Joseph.
13.8 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Ephraim, Hoshea wunnaumonuh Nun.
13.9 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄oonk Benjamin | Palti wunnaumonuh Raphu.
13.10 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Zabulon, Gaddiel wunnaumonuh Sodi.
13.11 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Joseph. wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Manasses, Gaddi wunnaumonuh Susi,
13.12 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Dan, Ammiel wunnaumonuh Gemalli.
13.13 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Asher, Sether wunnaumonuh Michael.
13.14 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Naphtali, Nahbi wunnaumonuh Vophsi.
13.15 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Gad. Geuel wunnaumonuh Machi.
13.16 Yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ash wosketompaog Moses annꝏ̄noncheh wunnatauwohtinnaóont ohke: kah Moses wutussowenau Hoshea wunnaumonu Nun, Joshuah,
13.17 Mah Moses nah wutannꝏ̄nuh wunnatinneahkóontamunnaóont ohkeit Kanaan, kah nah wuttinuh, ogquodchuag nogque en sowaniyeu, kah ogquodchuag en wadchuut.
13.18 Kah kuhkinneamꝏ̄k ohke uttôh ônag, kah missinninnuog neg noh wadohkitcheg, tóh wuttin menuhkesinneau, asuh nꝏ̄chumwesinneau, toh wuttin mononeau asuh ogguhsinneau.
13.19 Kah uttôh ônag ohke ne wadohkehettit, uttoh en wunnegen asuh matchet, kah uttôh ônag keihtotanash ne âhettit, toh weetuommúꝏ̄ asuh wonkonꝏ̄sinnúꝏ̄,
13.20 Kah tóh ônag ohke, toh en weenauohkomukkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ asuh matohkomukkꝏ̄ꝏ̄; toh wuttuhqunnúꝏ̄ asuh matta: kah wuttꝏ̄anatamꝏ̄k kah neemunûmꝏ̄k nawhutch meechummꝏ̄onk ne ohkeit, kah yeuyeu ahquompiyeup negonne adtuhtag wenominneash.
13.21 Kah ogquodchuwaog kah natinneahkontamwog ohke, kah touohkomukqut Sin, en Rehob, en weekqshik Hamath.
13.22 Kah ogquodchuauog en sowaniyeu, kah peyau Hebron, kah na wutapinneau Ahiman, Sheshai, kah Talmai, wunnaumonuh Anak: onk Hebton ayìmunah nesausuk tahshe kodtumwáe negonnâeu Zoan ut Egypt.
13.23 Kah peyaog sepuesut Eshkol, kah nà wutch tummehtamuneau wuttuhkq, kah nequttutcheauash, wenominneash, kah nesuog wuttéhtumuneau, kah paudtóog pomegranates, kah figsash.
13.24 Ne ayeuonk hettamun Eshkol sepues, newutche nequttutcheaush, nish wunnaumonuh Israel na waj tummehthamhetticheh.
13.25 Kah qushkeog wutch natinneakontamunat ohke, mahche yauunchadtikquinohkok.
13.26 Kah nag moncheog, kah peyaonáog Mosesoh, kah en Aaronut, kah en wame mukkinneonganꝏ̄ont wunnaumonuh Israel, en Parane touohkomukqut en Kadesh; kah nah uppaudtanchemꝏ̄kauóuh, kah wame | mukkinneonk, kah nah wunnohtinóuh ummeechummóonk ohke.
13.27 Kah nag wuttinnoneau, kah nꝏ̄waog, nuppeyaumun ohkeit na anannꝏ̄seog, kah wunnamuhkut ut tommogkon sogkodtunk kah honey, kah yeu nawhutch ummechummúonk.
13.28 Qut missinninnúog ne wadohkicheg menuhkesuog, kah wonkonꝏ̄sine kittꝏ̄tanash ahche mogkiyeuash, kah na nuttit nauónan wunnaumonuh Anak.
13.29 A[m]alek wutohtu sowanohkomukqut, kah Hittitsog, kah Jebusitsog, kah Amoritsog, wutohtuog wadchuut, kah Kanaanitsog wutohtuog kishke ketahhannit, kah kishke Jordan ohkéit.
13.30 Kah Kaleb sunnequáheau missinninnúog ut anaquabit Moses, kah nꝏ̄wau, ogquodchuae ogquodchuadtuh kah ohtauuttuh, newutche papáne kuttapenumumun sohkomunat.
13.31 Qut wosketompaog neh weeche ogquodchuómukqutche, nꝏ̄waog, matta kuttapenumꝏ̄mun ayeuhkone ogquodchuwáonónat missinninnuog newutche nag kutánue menuhkcsumukqunnónog.
13.32 Kah kesteauog mataunchemꝏ̄kaonk papáume ne ohke natinneahkontamwéhettit, en wunnaumonat Israel, nꝏ̄waog, Ne ohke pannupwusháog natinneahkontamunat, ne ohke máhchepꝏ̄ neh noh wodohkinutcheh, kah wame missinninnuog neg noh adt náugketcheg, quoquounkqussuog.
13.33 Kah na nuttit nauónan magoshketompáog wunnaumonuh Anak, neh wutontseonguh mogoshketompáog, kah nenawun ut nuskesuskqunnónut nutogqueneunkqussimun quaquequeshantóut, kah netatuppe ut wuskesukꝏ̄óut.
14.1 KAh wáme mukkinneonk mishontꝏ̄wae wuttauatonkqussuog, kah missinninnuog mauog ne nohkog.
14.2 Kah wame wunnaumonuh Israel, ayeuuhkone mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skomaog Mosesoh kah Aatonoh, kah wame mukkinneonk nah wuttinuh Woi napehnont nuppꝏ̄ogkus ut ohkeit Egypt, asuh ut touohkomuk napehnont nuppogkus.
14.3 Kah tohwhaj Jehovah pasꝏ̄kqueog yeu ohkeit, nuppunshonanónut wutch togkodteg, nummittawwussinnónog, kah nuppeissesumunnônog wutch tohqunnittuonk; sunnummatta negonne wunnegenninno nuqushkenanonut en Egypt?
14.4 Kah nag unnàog nishnoh howan wematoh, ayeuontuh mummugquomp, kah qushketuh en Egypt.
14.5 Kah Moses kah Aaron penushauttamwog wuskesukꝏ̄oash, ut anaquabhettit mukkinneáe | móecheg wame wunnaumonuh Israel
14.6 Kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun, kah Kaleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh, nag nawhutch natauohtunkuppanneg ohke nenekkuhkomwog wuthogkꝏ̄unash.
14.7 Kah nag unnaog wame mukkinneonguh, wunnaumonuh Israel, nꝏ̄waog, Ohke ne pannupwushaogkup natinneakontamunat, ne muttáe wunnegen ohke.
14.8 Tohneit Jehovah tapeneunkqueog, neit woh kuppasꝏ̄qun yeu ohkeit, kah woh kittinnumunkqunan, ohke ne tomogok sogkodtunk kah hony.
14.9 Webe ahque cheketók Jehovah: kah kenaau, ahque qusheuk missinninnúog ohkit, newutche nag kuppetukqunnunkanunnonog, wutonkkaúhqussꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wunnukkonukquneau, kah Jehovah kꝏ̄wetomukqun, ahque nag wabesuónꝏ̄k.
14.10 Qut wame mukkinneonk nꝏ̄wau, nashpe qussukquanash qussukquanehtahhꝏ̄k: kah wussohsumóonk Jehovah nogquot, ut mukkinneaekommukqut, ut anaquabhettit wame wunnaumonuh Israel.
14.11 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, Tohuttꝏ̄che yeug missinninnuog nummꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqhikquog? kah tohuttꝏ̄che matta pish nꝏ̄namptunkꝏ̄og, newutche wame kukkinneasuongash nish aseonish ut kenugke naghok.
14.12 Nag nuttogkomôóg nashpe enninneaonguh, nummananumóog nutahtoonk, kah nummishteo wutohtimóin wutche kuhhogkat, anue missi kah menuhki onk nag.
