14.13 Kah Moses unnau Jehovah, neit Egyptianéog pish wunnꝏ̄tamuneau, newutche kussohhꝏ̄wun yeug missinninnúog, nashpe kummenuhkesuonk wutch (k)enugke nagoh.
14.14 Kah n[a]g pish unnaog yeuh, yeu wadohkinutcheh ohkeit newutche nag nꝏ̄tamwog, ken Jehovah kꝏ̄weetom yeug missinninnúog, ken Jehovah mamuskesukque kenait, kah kummatokqussum waabe ohteau ut nag, kah ut matokqse pogkomunkquonkanit nag kinnegonuhkauóog kesukodtáeu, kah ut nꝏ̄táe pokomunkquonkanit nukkonaeu,
14.15 Yeuyeu nashadt yeug missinninnúog onatuh pasuk wosketomp, neit wutohtimónneunk woh nꝏ̄waog, neg nꝏ̄togig kꝏ̄waweenomiteaonk, nꝏ̄waog:
14.16 Newutche Jehovah nꝏ̄num uppásꝏ̄ónat yeuh missinninnuh, en ohkeit nnoh chadchekéimomp, newajeh nushont ut touohkomuk.
14.17 Kah yeuyeu kenanompassumsh, ummenuhkesuonk Jehovah missaj, neánꝏ̄wáop, kussip.
14.18 Jehovah sepe chequnehtam, kah muttae monaneteau, wutahquontamunat matcheseongash kah panneseongash, kah pahke matta pahteanumau matchesenutcheh, nátauwohtau wutꝏ̄shinneunk ummatcheseonganôash ut wunnaumonat, en nishwudt, | kah en yauudt pometuonganit.
14.19 Ahquontash kenanompassumush ummatcheseonganꝏ̄ yeug missinninnuog neane missag kummonaneteaonk, kah neane ahquontamauadt yeug missinninnuog, wutch Egypt en yeu pajeh.
14.20 Kah Jehovah nꝏ̄wau, Nummahche ahquontam neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
14.21 Qut wunnamuhkut neane pomantam, wame ohke pish numwohteau wussohsumóonk Jehovah.
14.22 Newutche wame wosketompaog neg nagig nussohsumóonk, kah nukkehkinneasuongash nish aseánish ut Egypt, kah ut touohkomuk, kah nukqutchhikquog yeush piogqut nompe, kah matta nꝏ̄tamóog nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk.
14.23 Nag namohettit ohke ne chadcheimog wutꝏ̄shinneunk, onk matta pish howan neg mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄skumutcheg wunnaumꝏ̄unneau
14.24 Qut nuttinneum Kaleb, newutche onkatoge nashauanitto mo appehtunk, kah pannuppe nutasukunk, nnoh nuppasꝏ̄ ohkit né aiyont, kah ꝏ̄skannemuneoh pish wutahtáenin.
14.25 (Neit Amalakitsog kah Kananitsog wutohtuppaneg ꝏ̄nauhkoiyeuut) saup qushkek, kah onkq touohkomuk nnogque mayut misque ketahhanit.
14.26 Kah Jehovah keneꝏ̄nau Moses kah Aaronoh nꝏ̄wau,
14.27 Toh uttꝏ̄che woh nutchequnehtam yeu matche pometuonk, neg mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skumutcheg? nunnꝏ̄tam ummꝏ̄mꝏ̄skꝏ̄waongnꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel ne mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skummehettit.
14.28 Nag us, Neane pomantam wunnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau Jehovah pish kuttunnehennumwꝏ̄ ne anꝏ̄waóg ut nehtauogkut.
14.29 Kuhhogkaóog pish penusháog ut touohkomukqut, kah wame neg agkemutcheg kenugke kenaau, neaunag mamusse kutogkemutteaonganꝏ̄, wutch neesnehchage kodtumwohkomunat kah paameu, neg ayeuuhkône mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skumutcheg
14.30 Mat chananetamwe matta pish kuppeyaumwꝏ̄ ohkeit papaume ne chadchekeyeuwâomp, na kꝏ̄tohkehhenunaóont, webe Kaleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh, kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun.
14.31 Kah kuppeissesumꝏ̄óog, neg anꝏ̄waogkuppanneg, pish tohqunoog, neg nuppethuóneau, kah nag pish wahteauog ne ohke ne sekeneâmog.
14.32 Qut kenaau kuhhogkaóog pish penusháog ut touohkomuk.
14.33 Kah keneechanꝏ̄óog pish meetsuog ut touohkomuk yauuncahge kodtumwae, kah pish kenunnumwog kummamussuwonganꝏ̄ash, nô pajeh kuhhogkaôog mohtuppaehettit, ut touohkomuk.
14.34 Neane ogketamuk kesukodtash, natinneakontamog | ohke yauunchatikquinne, (pasuk kesuk nequt kodtumꝏ̄, pasuk kesuk nequt kodtumꝏ̄) pish kukkenunnumwꝏ̄ kummatcheseonganꝏ̄oash, yauunchage kodtumwae, kah pish kꝏ̄wahteomwꝏ̄ kuppohquanumoadtuonganun.
14.35 Nen Jehovah nummahche ketꝏ̄kom, wunnamuhkut nuttinehteauun yeu wame matche mukkinneonk, neg ayéuuhkone mukkinnehtunkqueaneg yeu ut touohkomuk neg pish mohtupáéog, kah na pish wuttit nuppuneau,
14.36 Kah wosketompaog neh Moses annꝏ̄noncheh wunnatinneakontamunaout ohke, kah quashkehettit, wame mukkinneonk ayeuuhkone mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skomonat nagum, paudtauwehettit mataunchemꝏ̄kaontamoonk ohke.
14.37 Yeug wosketompaog nuppꝏ̄og, neg paudtunkig mataunchemꝏ̄kaontamꝏ̄onk ohke, nashpe enninneaonk, ut anaquabit Jehov[]h.
14.38 Qut Johsua wunnaumonuh Nun, kah Kaleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh, pomantamwog, nawhutch yeug natinneakontogkuppanneg ohke.
14.39 Kah Moses yeush kuttꝏ̄wongash wuttinnonash wame wunnaumonuh Israel, kah missinninnuog mishe mauog.
14.40 Kah neepóog nompoae, kah auog kódtuhkôag wadchuut, nꝏ̄waog, Kusseh nenawun kah pish nuttomun, ne ayeuonk Jehovah anꝏ̄wop, newutche nummatchesemun
14.41 Kah Moses nꝏ̄wau, Tohwutch yeuyeu panneussehtamog wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah? qut matta pish wunnegeninnꝏ̄
14.42 Ahque kuhkuhquegk, newutche Jehovah matta kꝏ̄wetomukꝏ̄, onk woh mat kuttogkomitteomwꝏ̄ ut anaquabhettit kummatwomꝏ̄óog.
14.43 Newutche Amalekitsog, kah Kananitsog, na anaquabeog, kah pish kuppenushomwꝏ̄ wutche togkodteg, newutche kukqushkemwꝏ̄ wutch asuhkauonat Jehovah, kah matta Jehovah pish kꝏ̄weetomukou.
14.44 Qut nag pittuanumwe koshkomme ogquodchuáog en kôdtuhkôag wadchuut, qut wunnꝏ̄wae wut-Arkum Jehovah kah Moses, matta amai wutch anome tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit.
14.45 Kah Amalekitsog wꝏ̄mussuog kah Kananitsog, neg wadohkitcheg ne wadchuut kah nah wuttogkommouh kah wutuhquanumweheouh yâ en Hormah.
15.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
15.2 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel kah nag us, Peyôog kutohtue ohkeyeuout, ne anumauunog.
15.3 Ayimog nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk en Jehovah | ut, chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, asuh sephâusuonk, chippinnumunat quoshauwaonk, asuh unnantamwe magꝏ̄onk, asuh ut kukkuhkꝏ̄wae mishadtuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wout, ayimunat weetemungquok en Jehovahut, wutch flokut, asuh herdut,
15.4 Neit noh maguk wussephausuonk en Jehovahut, pish pasꝏ̄chewuttau m(ee)chꝏ̄e magꝏ̄onk, paogque chippag paskquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu yaue chippag pasuk hinne pummee.
15.5 Kah yaue chippag pasuk hinne wine, wutche wuttattamóe sephasuonk, ne pish kukquoquoshwunnumun, wutche chikohtae magꝏ̄onk asuh wutche sephausuonk, wutch pasuk Lamb.
15.6 Asuh wutche ram, pish kutayim meetsué sephausuonk, neese piogque chippag pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu nashpe nashwe chippag hinne pummee
15.7 Kah wutch wuttattamóe magꝏ̄onk nashwe chippag hinne wine, pish kummagun wutch weetemungquok en Jehovahut.
15.8 Kah ayimun herde wuskoshimꝏ̄m, chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, asuh sephausuonk, chippinnumunat quoshowaonk, asuh wunohteae magꝏ̄ongash en Jehovahut.
15.9 Neit pish pasꝏ̄che pasꝏ̄au weeche herde wuskoshimwoh, meetsue sephausuonk nishwe piogque chippagish pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu paushe hinne pumme.
15.10 Kah pish kussephaus wutch wuttattamóe sephausuonk, paushe hinne wine, wutche nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk weetemungquok en Jehovahut.
15.11 Yeu pish unneheun wutch pasuk oxen, asuh wutch pasuk ram, asuh wutch shepse lambe asuh goatses
15.12 Neaunogketamuk ne pish ayimwog, ne pish kuttinteauunneau wutch nishnoh pasuk, neaunogketamuk.
15.13 Nishnoh pasuk noh kohothteaenekit, ne pish yeush wuttinteauun, ummagunat nꝏ̄tae sephausuonk weetemungquok en Jehovahut.
15.14 Kah tohneit penꝏ̄wot enneapeyont kuhhogkaout, asuh howan kenukshóog ut kuppometuonganꝏ̄out, kah kod ayik nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk weetemungquok en Jehovahut, neaseog ne pish wutussen.
15.15 Kenaáu moeuwehkomonk, pasuk kuhkꝏ̄waonk pish wutch kenaau, kah wutch penꝏ̄wot noh neyaneapeyont, michemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk ut kuppometuonganꝏ̄wout, neanayeog, ne pish wuttinniin penꝏ̄woat ut anaquabit Jehovah.
15.16 Pasuk unnaumatuonk, kah pasuk unniyeuonk ne pish wutche kenaau, kah wutch penꝏ̄wot, noh neaneapeont.
15.17 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
15.18 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel kah nag | us, Peyôóg ohkeit ne pasꝏ̄unog.
15.19 Neit pish nnìh meechog ne petukqunnunk ne ut ohkeit, pish kuttahshinumumwꝏ̄ tatashinumwe sephausuonk en Jehovahut.
15.20 Negonne kuttittuhpunnumꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ pish kuttatashinnumumwꝏ̄ wutch tatashinumwe sephausuonk, neane tatashinumwe sephausuonk wutch áhhuttannuppoghamuk, ne pish kuttìnne tatashinnumunneau.
15.21 Negonne kuttittuhpunumꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ pish kuttinnumauóneau Jehovah tatashinumwe magꝏ̄onk ut kuppometuonganꝏ̄out.
15.22 Kah mat wahteaue matchesecheg, kah matta usseog wame yeush wuttinnaumatuongash nish Jehovah anoncheh Mosesoh.
15.23 Wame nish Jehovah anꝏ̄nukqueagish nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses; wutch na kesukod Jehovah anꝏ̄nont Mosesoh, kah yeu pajeh pannuppe kuppometuonganꝏ̄out
15.24 Neit pish nnih, ne teag mat wahteaue ussemuk, wutch wuskesukqut mukkinneonk: neit wame mukkinneonk pish quaquashwunau pasukꝏ̄ bullokoh, wuskoshimꝏ̄m wutch herdut, wutche chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, wutche weetemungquok en Jehovahut, kah ummetsue sephausuonk, kah ꝏ̄tattamwe sephausuonk neáseog, kah pasuk nomposhimwe goats wutche matcheseongane sephausuonk.
15.25 Kah sephausuen pish ayim wunnauwadtuonk wutch wame ummukkìnneonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, kah pish monaneteae ahquontamauóneau newutch ne matta wahteauonk, kah nag paudtóog ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut, kah ummatcheseongane sephausuonganꝏ̄ anaquabit Jehovah, wutche mat ꝏ̄wahteaonganꝏ̄.
15.26 Kah ne pish monaneteae ahquontamauoneau wame ummukkinneonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, kah penꝏ̄wot noh na áneapeyont, newutche wame missinninnuog matta wahteauꝏ̄og.
15.27 Kah pasuk keteahogkou mat wahteaue matchesit, neit pish pasꝏ̄chewunau ne kodtumꝏ̄k squoshimwe goatsoh wutche matcheseae sephausuonk.
15.28 Kah sephausuaen pish wunnauwadtuwáheau keteahogkounoh neh mat wahteaue matchesenutcheh, mat wahteaue matcheseit anaquabit Jehovah, noh wunnauwadheonat kah pish monaneteae ahquontamauon.
15.29 Wutch noh adt nekit kenugke wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wutche penꝏ̄wot noh neadt penuwohteaut pasuk unnaumatuonk wutche kenaau, noh matta wahteaue matchesit.
15.30 Qut keteahogkou noh quanunkquanutcheae matchesit, ut toh an noh ne adt neekit, asuh penꝏ̄wot, noh kehkomau Jehovah, kah noh keteahogkou pish tummetahwhau wutch kenugke ummissinninnúmoh.
15.31 Newutche sekéneam wuttinnꝏ̄wàonk | Jehovah, kah pohquanum wuttinnowaonk noh keteahogkou, pish pannuppe tummetahwhau, ummatcheseonk pish wutappetunkqun.
15.32 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel ayeuog touohkomuk, kah tohqunóog wusketompuh aseenshauh Sábbath dayeu.
15.33 Kah nag aseenshanutcheh tohqunoncheg, uppasꝏ̄ch(e) wuttauwonáoh Mosesoh kah Aaronoh, kah wame mukkinneongoh,
15.34 Kah ukkupshagkinóuh, newutche asquam wahhikquodtinno toh woh ánhit.
15.35 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, wosketomp pish nuppꝏ̄e nushau, kah wame mukkinneonk ukqussukquontahwhoh qussukquonash ut poquodche tuppukfinnowonganit.
15.36 Kah wame mukkinéonk wunohhꝏ̄wunoh en poquodche tuppuskinnowonganit kah nag ukqussukquantahwhóuh qussukquanash, kah nuppꝏ̄ nean annꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mososoh,
15.37 Kah Jehovh kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau.
15.38 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israal, kah nag us, ayimmohettich wunnewus ut uhquae wuthogkꝏ̄unꝏ̄óut, pannuppe uppometuonganꝏ̄éut; kah ponamwehettich ut uhquae ꝏ̄nóe ribband:
15.39 Kah ne pish wunnewussiyeuꝏ̄ wutche kenaau, onk woh kenaumuneau, kah woh kummequontamumwꝏ̄ wame wuttinnaumatuongash Jehovah, nish ussenat, kah woh matta kenoswehtamomwꝏ̄ nehenwonche kuttahhꝏ̄woash kah nehenwonche kuskesukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, nish neahen nanwunꝏ̄dsquaóg.
15.40 Onk woh kummequantamumwꝏ̄, kah kutussémwꝏ̄ wame nuttinnaumatuongash, onk woh kꝏ̄neetupanatamweyeumwꝏ̄, en kum-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄wóut.
15.41 Nen Jehovah kum Manittꝏ̄wꝏ̄, noh sohhꝏ̄wunukqueóg wutch ohkit Egypt, kꝏ̄-Manittꝏ̄munnaóut, nen Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mwꝏ̄.
16.1 KAh Korah wunnaumonuh Izhar, wunnaumonuh Kohath, wunnaumonuh Levi, nemunau wosketompuh, kah Dathan kah Abiram wunnaumonuh Eliab, kah On wunnaumonuh Peleth, wunnaumonuh Ruben.
16.2 Kah nag neepꝏ̄og ut anaquabit Moses, kah wosketompaog nawutch wunnaumonuh Israel, neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og kah napanna tahshinchág sontimóog ut mukkinneonganit, wehkumutcheg, ut mukkinneáonganit, wanoncheumꝏ̄ónutcheg.
16.3 Kah ayeuuhkone moiéhtauáog Mosesoh kah Aaron, kah nág nah wuttìnóuh, kꝏ̄saumme mìshheaumwꝏ̄ kuhhogkaóog, newutche wame mukkinneonk, wame nag wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄og, kah Jehovah nah weamukshonuh, kah toh waj ánue ushpunóg | kuhhogkaóog ummoeuwehkomunk Jehovah.
16.4 Kah Moses wunnꝏ̄tamun, kah penushadtam wuskesuk.
16.5 Kah kenꝏ̄nau Korahoh kah wame ne adtahsꝏ̄it, nꝏ̄wau, mohtompôg, Jehovah pish wahteauwâhuau nah wuttaiheuh, kah howan wunnetupanatamweyeuit, kah howane pasꝏ̄tsháheont, neh uppepenauoh, pish uppasꝏ̄tsháheuh wuhhogkat.
16.6 Yeu ussek, nemunnumꝏ̄k censersash Korah, kah wame ne adtahsꝏ̄it.
16.7 Kah ne poamꝏ̄k nꝏ̄tau, kah ne ponamꝏ̄k incense, ut anaquabit Jehovah saup, Kah pish n nih, wosketomp neh Jehovah pepenauoncheh, noh pish wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄, kenaau kꝏ̄saume misheheamwꝏ̄ kuhhogkaóog, kenaau wunnaumonuh Levi.
16.8 Kah Moses unnau Korah, nꝏ̄tiek kꝏ̄wehquetumauunumwꝏ̄, kenaau wunnaumonuh Levi:
16.9 Sun yeu peamesan wutche kenaau, ne um-Manittꝏ̄moh Israel kutchippunukquneau, wutch ummukkinneonganit Israel, kuppasꝏ̄che wunnunnanónut en wuhhogkát, ussenat tabernakle usseonk Jehovah, kah nepauinneat anaquabhettit mukkinneonk, aninnumauónat?
16.10 Kah noh kuppasꝏ̄chewunuk; kah wame kcmatog wunnaumonuh Levi weeche ken, kah sun wonk kenatinneahamumwꝏ̄ sephausuâenue aninnohsuonk?
16.11 Ne waj ken wame ne adttahsꝏ̄wean, áyeuuhkonittue mukkinehtauadt Jehovah: kah Aaron, howan noh, waj mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skomôg?
16.12 Kah Moses annꝏ̄teamo wehkomônat Dathan kah Abiram, wunnaumonuh Eliab: kah nag nꝏ̄waog, matta woh nukkuhkukkꝏ̄mun.
16.13 Sun peásin yeu kuppasꝏ̄innean wutch ohkeit, ne tomogkok sogkodtunk kah hony, kenushinneanónut ut touohkomuk: qut wonk kussontimáeu kuhhog ânue onk nenawun;
16.14 Wonk matta kuppasꝏ̄ꝏ̄mun ohkeit ne tomogkok sogkodtunk kah hony, kittinnummiinneanónut ohteakone kah weenominneohtekone ahtôonk: sun kukkuthamumwꝏ̄ yeug wuskesukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash? matta woh nukkuhkukꝏ̄mun.
16.15 Kah Moses ahche musquantam, kah unnau Jehovah, ahque tapeneash wussephausuonganꝏ̄, matta nemunumauóog pasukꝏ̄ash, asuh matta pasuk nꝏ̄woskheuh.
16.16 Kah Moses unnau Korahoh, ken kah wame ne adtahsꝏ̄wean, neepok anaquabit Jehovah, ken kah nag, kah Aaron saup.
16.17 Kah nemunnumok nish noh wosketomp wus-censerhm, kah ponamok incense, kah pasꝏ̄che wuttauꝏ̄k anaquabit Jehovah nish noh wosketomp wus-censerum, neesepasukꝏ̄ censersash, kah napanna tahshinchag, kah ken | kah Aaron, nish noh wosketomp wus-censerum.
16.18 Kah nag nemunumwog nishnoh wosketomp wus-censerum, kah nꝏ̄tau upponamuneau, kah incense upponamuneau, kah nag neépóog ut mukkinneae kommukque squontamut, kah Moses kah Aaron.
16.19 Kah Korah ayeuuhkonittue mukinnéhtauau nahoh, wame mukkinneonk, en mukkinneâe kommukque squontamut, kah wussohsumꝏ̄onk Jehovah naeihtam wame mukkinneonk.
16.20 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh, nꝏ̄wau,
16.21 Chippinnꝏ̄k kuhhogkaóog wutch kenugke yeug mukkinneonk, kah tiadche nuppáguanôog.
16.22 Kah nag penushadtamwog wuskesukꝏ̄oash, kah nꝏ̄waog, woi Manit, um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh wunnashauonguh wame weyaus; pasuk matcheseit, sun pish kussopitae kummusquanum wame mukkinneonk.
16.23 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
16.24 Kenꝏ̄s mukkinneonk nꝏ̄wash, kuhkuhquegk wutch waeenu wetuomut Korah Dathan kah Abiram.
16.25 Kah Moses omohku, kah au Koroh ut Dathánut kah Abiram ut, kah Israelle eldersog wutasukauouh.
16.26 Kah kenꝏ̄nau mukkinneonguh nꝏ̄wau ámaegk kꝏ̄wehquetumauonumwꝏ̄, wutch weekuout yeug matchetowéenuog: kah ahque missunnumꝏ̄k ne teaguas wuttaiheeu, ishkont kummohtupaemꝏ̄ ut wame nag ummatcheseonganꝏ̄out.
16.27 Kah nag kuhkuhqueog wutch wetuomut Korah Dathan kah Abiram waeenu, kah Dathan kah Abiram sohhamwrg, kah neepoog squontam wekuôut, kah ummittamwussꝏ̄oh, kah wunnaumonꝏ̄uh, kah uppeissesumꝏ̄uh.
16.28 Kah Moses nꝏ̄wau, yeu wutch pish kꝏ̄wahteomwꝏ̄ Jehovah nuta§ꝏ̄nuk wame yeush ussenat, newutche matta nehenwonche nuttah ut nꝏ̄ch ussenash.
16.29 Tóhneit yeug wosketompàog nuppehettit, neane wamewosketompaog nuppehettit: kah unninnatauwahut neauaunag natauwahaonganꝏ̄ wame wosketompaog, neit Jehovah matta nutannꝏ̄nukꝏ̄h:
16.30 Qut Jehovah wuske kesteunk teag, kah ohke woshwuttꝏ̄ait, kah nah misseashquit, kah wame neg wadchiitcheg, kah keteae wꝏ̄mussehéttit en chepiohkomukqut, neit pish kꝏ̄wahteomwꝏ̄, yeug wosketompaog mꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheaog Jehovah,
16.31 Onk nish mahche nꝏ̄wadt wame yeush kutꝏ̄wongash, ohke passôagkemꝏ̄ ne apappéhettit.
16.32 Kah ohke woshwunum wuttꝏ̄n, kah nah ummissheasqunneuh, kah wekꝏ̄oash, kah | wame wosketompaog neg wadchiitcheg Korahut, kah wuttinnéetuonganꝏ̄.
16.33 Kah nag, kah wame noh wadchiitcheg keteae wꝏ̄mussuog en chepiohkomuk: kah ohke wéanehtauoh, kah nag paguanuog wutch kenugke moeuwehkomonk:
16.34 Kah wame Israel neg weenehkauonchég wussemóog, wadtauaonkqussinit, newutche nꝏ̄waog, ishkont ohke kummisheasquonukqun.
16.35 Kah nꝏ̄tau ꝏ̄mꝏ̄ꝏ̄ wutch Jehovahut kah mahchekuswau neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄oh, wosketompoh kah napanna tahshinchagkodtog neg sephausitcheg incense.
16.36 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
16.37 Kenꝏ̄s Eleazer wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen, woh wunnemunnumunat Censersash wutch nashqunaut, kah seahash nꝏ̄tau yeáut; newutche nish wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄ash.
16.38 Wussencersumꝏ̄ash yeug macheneheoncheg nehenwonche ukketeahogkounouh kah nish ayimunach mage kiskagish, wutche onkhumunat Altar, newutche nish wussephausinaoash ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah nish wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄ash, kah nish pish kuhkinneasuongash wutch wunnaumonuh Israel.
16.39 Kah Eleazar sephausuaen nemunum wompohshogque Censersash, nish nag chagohsuhpanneg sephaushetteupash, kah nish ayimunash mage kiskagish onkhumunat Altar.
16.40 Ummequontamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel; wanne howae penꝏ̄wot, neh matta ꝏ̄skannemunegeh Aaron, woh pasꝏ̄tshonat sephausinneat inecnse ut anaquabit Jehovah, ishkont yaneyeuꝏ̄ Korahoh, kah neadtashaiyeuéhettit, neanꝏ̄wodt Jehovah ut nashpe wunnutcheganit Moses en wuhhogkat.
16.41 Kah na nompunk, wame mukkinneunkanꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel ayeuuhkonittue mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skomaog Mosesoh, kah Aaronoh, nꝏ̄waog, kenushomwꝏ̄ ummissinninneumoh Jehovah.
16.42 Kah n nih mukkinneonk moiehettit ayeuuhkonittue Mosesoh, kah ayeuuhkoittue Aaronoh, nuhquaeog nogque mukkinneaekommukqut, kah kusseh matokqs wunnuhkuhkomun, kah wussohsumôonk Jehovah nogquodt.
16.43 Kah Moses kah Aaron peyauog anaquohtag mukkinneaekommuk.
16.44 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
16.45 Kuhkuhquegk wutch kenugke yeu mukkinneonganit, kah nukkenuppe paguanóog, kah nag penushaantamwog wuskesukꝏ̄ash.
16.46 Kah Moses unnau Aaronoh, nemunush ne Censer, kah ne ponsh nꝏ̄tau wutche | Altarut, kah ne ponsh incense, kah kenupshaush en mukkinneonganit, kah nag wunnauwadtuwah, newutche kussopiteae musquantamꝏ̄onk sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wutch anaquabit Jehovah, ut énninneaonk kutchishin.
16.47 Kah Aaaron nemunum ne anꝏ̄wadt Moses, kah quogqueu en nóe moeuwehkomonganit, kah kusseh enninneaonk kutchishin ut kenugke missinninnutu: kah ponamun incense, kah wunnauwadtuwaheau missinninnuh.
16.48 Kah noh neepau nashaue napunutche kah pamontamunutcheh, kah enninneaonk togkogqshau.
16.49 Kah nag napukeg ut enninneaonganit nabo yaue muttannonganogkussuog kah nesausuk tahshe pasuꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, chonchippe neg napukeg papaume wutusseonk Korah.
16.50 Kah Aaron qushkeu en Mosesut, en mukkinneaekommukque squontamut, kah enninneaonk togkogqshau.
17.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau.
17.2 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel: nemunnumwansh, mehtugkꝏ̄m, wutch nishnoh ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weeꝏ̄ash, wutch wame Sontimmohtu, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh weekuoash, nabo nenash metugkꝏ̄mesash, nishnoh wosketomp ꝏ̄wesuonk pish kꝏ̄sukkuhhumun ut ummehtugkꝏ̄mesut.
17.3 Kah Aaron ꝏ̄wesuonk pish kꝏ̄sukkuhhumun ut ummehtugkꝏ̄mesut Levi: newutche pasuk mehtugkꝏ̄mes pish wutch wabuhkuhkꝏ̄ut ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuout.
17.4 Kah pish kꝏ̄wadchanumunash ut mukkinneaekommukqut, anaquohtag wauwaonk uttoh adt nogkushkauun.
17.5 Kah pish nnih, wosketomp noh pepenꝏ̄og, ummehtugkꝏ̄mes pish negin, kah nutchequnahtóh ummꝏ̄skꝏ̄aongnꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, ne waj mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skumehettit,
17.6 Kah Moses kenꝏ̄nau wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wame sontimóog nag wuttinnumauóuh mehtugkꝏ̄mes wutch pasuk sontim, mehtugkꝏ̄mes wutch pasuk sontim neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekuóash, nabo nenash mehtugkꝏ̄mesash: kah ummehtugkꝏ̄mes Aaron weamukshau nag ummehtugkꝏ̄mesꝏ̄óut.
17.7 Kah Moses ponum mehtugkꝏ̄mesash anaquabit Jehovah ut wauwaekomukqut.
17.8 Onk n nih na nompunk, Moses petuttead en wauwáekommukqut, kah kusseh ummehtugkꝏ̄mes Aaron wutch wek Levi, nekinup, kah sonkin wunnehtꝏ̄nóhquomash, kah sonkin uppishaanash, kah wutcheken almondsash
17.9 Kah Moses wame sohwuttau mehtugkꝏ̄mesash wutch anaquabit Jehovah en wame wunnaumonuh Israel, káh nág naumwog | kah nemunnumwog nishnoh wosketomp ummehtugkꝏ̄mes.
17.10 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, Wonk paudtaush ummehtugquemes Aaron ut anaquohtag wauwáonk, woh wadchanumun wutch kukkinneasuonk ayeuuhkonittue cheketamwe wunnaumoniinneunk, kah pish kuppapakodche amaunumumwꝏ̄ mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skꝏ̄aonganꝏ̄ wutche nen, onk woh mat nuppꝏ̄og.
17.11 Kah Moses wutussen neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah, ne wutussen.
17.12 Ka[h] wunnaumonuh Israel unnaog Mosesoh nꝏ̄waog, Kusseh, nunnupumun, nuppaguanimun, nꝏ̄wame paguanimun.
17.13 Nishnoh pasuk noh pasꝏ̄tshadt, noh pasꝏ̄sukog wuttabernaklum Jehovah, pish nuppꝏ̄: sun pish nuppaguanumun nashpe nuppꝏ̄onk?
18.1 KAh Jehovah unnau Aaronoh, ken, kah kenaumonog, kah kꝏ̄sh week weeche ken, pish kugkenunumumwꝏ̄ matcheseongash ut sanctuaryeut, kah ken kah kenaumonunk weche, pis[n] kukkenunnumumwꝏ̄ kussephausue aninno[n]suenúe matcheseongash.
18.2 Kah wonk kematog, wutchippanꝏ̄onk Levi, wutchippanꝏ̄onk kꝏ̄sh pasꝏ̄chewuttoush weeche ken, onk woh nag kꝏ̄weechayeumukquog, kah woh kutannumunkquog: qut ken, kah kenaumonog weeche ken, pish aninnohsuog anaquohtag wauwaé kommuk.
18.3 Kah nag pish nanawehteauog kummeechumuhkausuwâonk, kah meechumuhkonáonk wame tabernakle: qut nag matta pish pasꝏ̄tshauꝏ̄og, wunneetupanatamwe wishquodt, kah ut Altarut, onk woh nag mat nuppꝏ̄og, na neeswe nag kah kenaau.
18.4 Kah nag pish kꝏ̄weechayeumukquog, kah pish nanawehteauog papaume meechumukhkontamïonk mukkinneae kommuk, wutch wame weetuôme usseongash, kah penꝏ̄wot matta pish kuppasꝏ̄sukꝏ̄gkou.
18.5 Kah pish kenanawehteamwꝏ̄ mechumuhkontamꝏ̄onk wunnetupanatamwe ayeuonk, kah mechumuhkontamꝏ̄kon Altar, onk matta wonk woh kussopitáe musquantamóonk ut wunnaumonat Israel.
18.6 Kah nen kusseh, nunneemun kemattꝏ̄wóog Levitsog, wutch kenugke wunnaumonat Israel: nag kittinnumonteánunk magꝏ̄onk wutche Jehovah, ussenat mukkinneáe kommukque usseongash.
18.7 Kah ken, kah kenaumonung weche pish kenanauwehteomwꝏ̄ kussephausue aninnohsuonganꝏ̄, wutch nish noh teag ut Altarut, kah ut anomut adtnikheganit, kah kenaau pish kutaninohsimwꝏ̄: kittinnummaunumwꝏ̄ kussephausuenûe aninnohsuonganꝏ̄, nanauwe | magꝏ̄ongane aninnohsuonk; kah penꝏ̄wot no[h] pasꝏ̄tshadt pish nushau.
18.8 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Aaronoh, kah nen kusseh kuttinnumaush meechumuhteaonk papaume wahwapenumwe magꝏ̄ongash, wutch wame ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Israel, nish kittinnumaúunash, wutche sussequnnaonk, kah en kenaumonat, nashpe michemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk.
18.9 Yeu pish kuttaihe, wutch ánue wunneetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄gish {wadchanumukish} wutch nꝏ̄taut: nishnoh ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wutch nishnoh meetsue sephausuonk, kah wutch nishnoh uppanneseáe sephausuonganꝏ̄oash, nish pish anumaumiéhetticheh, nish pish ánue wunneetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄ash, wutche ken kah wutche kenaumonunk.
18.10 Ut ánue wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit pish kummechineau: nishnoh nompaas pish ummeechin; ne pish wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄ wutche ken.
18.11 Kah yeu pish kúttaihe, waabenumwe sephausuonk, wutch ummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash. kah wame uppaupaumenumwe magꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Israel, nish kittinnumauununash, kah en kenaumonat kah en kuttanit weeche ken nashpe machemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk, nishnoh pahke missinnin ut kekit, pish ummeechin.
18.12 Wame ꝏ̄wésum wuske pummee, kah wame ꝏ̄wésum wusku wine, kah weatchiminneash, nish kakeneumunneash, nish pish anumauáhetticheh Jehovah, nish kittinnumáu[n]nash.
18.13 Kakeneumuneash wame pish nish ohkeit, nish pish paudtauáhetticheh Jehovah ut, nish pish kuttaiheash, noh pahkesit pish ummeechin.
18.14 Nish noh teag aninnumauon {God ut} Israelut, ne pish kuttaihe.
18.15 Nish noh ꝏ̄woshwuhkouôn wutôontomuk, wutch wame weyaus, nish pish pasꝏ̄chuwuttanutcheh Jehovah, wosketomp asuh puppinashim, noh pish kuttaihe: qut manouhuwáe pish kummanóh wosketompae mohtommegit, kah niskkeneungque puppinashimwe mohtommegit pish kummanóh.
18.16 Kah yeug {nashpe nagum} manꝏ̄whutcheg, wutch wunnukqut nepauzapinneat, nag pish kummanouwhóog, nashpe kꝏ̄nꝏ̄whaonk, wutch napanna tahshinash silvere shekélsash, neaunag sanctuariéhe shekel, ne neesnehchage gerahsash.
18.17 Qut kouashinne mohtomegit, asuh shepse mohtommegit, asuh goatsoh mohtommegit, matta pish kummanouwhoh, nag wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄og: ꝏ̄sqheonganꝏ̄ pish seahham Altarut, kah ꝏ̄wesumꝏ̄ pish kutchikohsum, wutche nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk, weetemungquok en Jehovah ut.
18.18 Kah nag ꝏ̄weyausꝏ̄ pish kuttaihe, neane paupaumenumwe mohpannog, kah | neane muttinnohkôunne uhpegq, ne pish kuttaihe.
18.19 Wame tahtashimumwe sephausuongash wadchiigish nish wanetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄kish, neh wunnaumonuh Israel maghetticheh en Jehovah, kittinnumoush, kah en kenaumonat, kah an kuttaunut weeche ken, nashpe machemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk: ne salte wunnꝏ̄waonk micheme, ut anaquabit Jehovah, wutche ken, kah kꝏ̄skannemeneunk nashpe ken.
18.20 Kah Jehovah unnau Aaronoh, matta pish kutohto ohtôonk ut wutohtꝏ̄ôut, asuh pish matta kutchippinumóadteamꝏ̄ kenugke nagoh, nen kutchippiyeum, kah kutahtôonk, ut kenugke wunnaumonat Israel.
18.21 Kah wutch wunnaumonuh Levi, kusseh nag nummagununkwame piukque chippagish ut Israel, wutche ahtoonk, wutche wutannósuonganꝏ̄ ne ussehettit, mukkinneáe kommukque usseonk.
18.22 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel matta pish pasꝏ̄tshauꝏ̄og mukkinneae kommuk yeu wutch, wunnayeutamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ matcheseonk, wunnuppunnaout
18.23 Qut Levitsog pish usseog mukkinneáe kommukque usseong, kah nag pish naiyeutamwóg ummatcheseonganꝏ̄: ne pish machemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk paupashpe kuppometuonganꝏ̄out, ut kenugke wunnaumonuh Israel matta pish ahtoꝏ̄og ahtóonk.
18.24 Qut uppiukque ch[]ppiyeumꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, nish pish anumauahetticheh Jehovah, wutche tatashinnumwe magꝏ̄onk, nuttinnumauoneau Levitsog wutche ahtôonk: newaj nag unog, kenugke wunnaumonat Israel matta pish ahtoꝏ̄og ahtóonk.
18.25 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
18.26 Kah en Levitsut pish kukkeketꝏ̄hkom kah nag us, nemunumog piukque chippag wutch wunnaumonuh Israel, nish anumauunogish, wutche nagoh, wutche kutohtoonganꝏ̄, neit pish kummagumwꝏ̄, nish wutch toshinnumwe magꝏ̄onk en Jehovah ut, piukque chippag wutch piukque chippiyeuut.
18.27 Kah kuttashinnumwe magꝏ̄onk pish kutogquontamonteaneau, onatoh weadchiminut ne ahhut tantuppoghamuk, kah onatuh wunnumwameechummuonk wine presse.
18.28 Yeu pish kittinne wonk maguneau, tahshinumwe magꝏ̄onk en Jehovah ut, wutch wame kuppiukque chippiyeumꝏ̄óut nish pish attumunmauogish wunnaumonuh Israel, kah pish kummagumwꝏ̄ tatashinnumwe sephamauaonk Jehovah en Aaronut sepháusuen.
18.29 Wutch wame kummagꝏ̄onganꝏ̄out, pish kummagumwꝏ̄ nish noh tashinnumwe sephamauaonk Jehovah, wutch wame wesut, ne wanetupanatamwe chippag noh wutch.
18.30 Kah nag pish kuttinnóog, mahche tahshinúmog wees na wutch, neit pish ogquntamauoneáu Levitsog, onatuh wohwutchiimuk ahut tonnupoghamuk, kah onatuh woh wutchiimuk winepresse,
18.31 Kah pish kummeechineau ut nish noh ayeuonganit, kenaau, kah kekꝏ̄oont newutche ne kutonkquatunkanꝏ̄; wutche kutannohsuonganꝏ̄ ut mukkinneaekommukqut.
18.32 Kah matta pish kukkinnumꝏ̄m matcheseonk newutch, mahche tahshinumwog ne wees noh wutch, kah matta pish kenishketeauomwꝏ̄ ꝏ̄néetupanatamweyeumꝏ̄ash wunnaumonuh Israel, onk matta woh kenuppꝏ̄mꝏ̄,
19.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosefoh kah Aar[o.]oh, nꝏ̄wau,
19.2 Yeu kuhkꝏ̄wae naumatuonk, ne Jehovah ananꝏ̄teamit, nꝏ̄wau, kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, kuppaudtunkqunnaout mashquesinitcheh, pannuppeye(u)e heifer, noh matta woskesegk, noh asquam ponamáuout yoak.
19.3 Kah pish kuttinnuumauonaoh Eleazer sephausuaen, kah noh pish wussohhꝏ̄wunoh en poquodche tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit kah pasuk pish wunnushoh, ut anaquabit.
19.4 Kah Eleazer sephausuen, pish nohwuttinnum ꝏ̄sqheonk, nashpe wuttinuhwhunitch, kah pish wusseauhkauoh ꝏ̄sqhéonk piuhsuke anaquohtag mukkinneae kommukqut nesausuk tahshit nompe.
19.5 Kah howan pish chikoswau heiferoh ut anaquabit wutaskonuh, kah ꝏ̄weyaus, kah ꝏ̄sqheonk, weeche ummꝏ̄e, pish wutchikoh[ss]umunash.
19.6 Kah sephausuen pish neemunum chikkuppeeûhtug kah hysop, kah musquag, kah pish wuttinuhkonash nashaue ut chiko(ss)it heifer,
19.7 Kah sephausuen pish kutchissittau wuthogꝏ̄unash, kah pish kutchissittau ꝏ̄weyaus nippeit, kah ompetak pish petutteau tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit, kah sephausuen pish nishkeneungqussu nô pajeh wunnonkꝏ̄ut[,]
19.8 Ka[n] noh neh chagoswoncheh, pish kutchessittau wuthógkꝏ̄unash nippekontu, kah pish kutchissittau ꝏ̄weyaus nippekontu, kah pish nishkeneunkq[]ssu pajeh wunnonkꝏ̄out.
19.9 Kah noh pahkesit wosketomp pish momounum uppukqueim heifer, kah pish upponamun paquadche tuppuksinꝏ̄ongnit pahke ayeuonganit, kah pish wadchanumauoneau wutche wunnaumonuh Israel, wutche chippinnumꝏ̄e nippe, ne pahketeóonk matcheséonk.
19.10 Kah noh magunuk uppukquem heifer pish kutchissittou wuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah pish nishkeneunkqussu nô pajeh wunnonkꝏ̄ut: | kah ne pish wutch wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wutch penꝏ̄wot noh ne adt penꝏ̄wohteaut machemohtag kuhkꝏ̄wáonk.
19.11 Noh masunont howáe ahchunkquoh, pish nishkeneunkqussu nesausuk tahshikquinne.
19.12 Pish wunnashpe pahkheon wuhhogkuh ut nishikquinogkodut, kah ut nesausuk tahshikquinogkodt ut pish pahkesu; kah matta pahkheunk wuhhogkuh ut nishikquinogkodut, kah ut nesausuk tahshikquinogkodtut noh matta pish pahkesu.
19.13 Howan masunont nuppꝏ̄oh, nuppoe wosketompae achchunk. kah matta pahkheunk wuhhogkuh noh nishketeau wuttabernaklum Jehovah, kah noh keteahogkou pish tummetahwhou wutch Israelut, newutche chippinumꝏ̄e nippe matta seauhkauoun noh pish nishkeneunkqussu, wunnishkeneunkqussuonkash wutappehtunkqun.
19.14 Yeu naumatuonk, wosketomp nuppuk ut wetuômut, wame neg paoncheg wetuómut, kah wame nish na ohtagish wetuómut pish nisheneunkquodtash nesausuk tahshikquinne
19.15 Kah nishnoh wôshwohtag wishq, ne mat kobsuhhausinꝏ̄g, ne nishkeneunkquodt
19.16 Kah howan masunont ut woskeche ohteakonit, noh noshit nashpe togkodteg, asuh ahchunk, asuh wuskon wosketomp; asuh weenohke, noh pish nishkeneunkgqussu nesausuk tahshikquinne.
19.17 Kah nag pish nemunumwánshaog neh nishkeneunkqussinutcheh wutch uppuppissiyeumut chogkosseup heifer, pahketeauunat matcheseonk, kah ne pish upponamun tohkekomeupog ut wishquadt'
19.18 Kah pahkesit wosketomp pish nemunum [b]ysoy, kah pish ukkomukqunumun nippiet, kah pish wusseauhkon woskeche wetuomut, kah ut wáme wishquadt, kah ut keteahogkounit neg, noh apitcheg, káh ut noh masunuk wushkon, asuh noh nashit, asuh noh napuk asuh weenohkee.
19.19 Kah noh pahkesit pish seauhkon ut neh nishneunkqussinutcheh ut nishikquinukodtut, kah ut nesausuk tahshikquinukukodtut kah pish kutchissittau wuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah pish kutchissitteauꝏ̄weyaus ut nippekontu, kah pish pahkesu ut wunnonkꝏ̄ut.
19.20 Kah wosketomp noh nisheneunkqussit, kah matta pahkheunk wuhhogkuh, noh keteahogkou pish tumehtahwhau wutch kenugke moeuwehkomonganit newutche nishkehteau wus-Sanctuaryhum Jehovah, chippinnumꝏ̄e nippe ásquam seauhkouout, noh nishkeneunkqussu.
19.21 Kah ne pish wutche nagoh michemohtag kuhkꝏ̄waonk, kah noh seauhteadt chippinnumꝏ̄e nippe pish kutchissittóu wuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah noh masunuk chippinnumꝏ̄e | nippe, pish nishkeneunkqussu nó paje wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄k.
19.22 Kah ne teag noh nishkeneunkqussit masunuk, pish nishkenunkquodt, kah keteahogkou noh masunuk, pish nishkeneunkqussu nó paieh wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄k.
20.1 KAh wunnaumonuh Israel, mamusse mukkinneonk peyaog touohkomukqut Zin ut negonne nepauz, kah missinninnuog ayeuog Kadesh, kah Miriam na wuttit nuppun, kah naut posekinan.
20.2 Kah na matta nippeno wutche mukkinneonk, kah nag ayeuuhkonitue miyaéog Moses kah ayeuuhkonittue Aaron.
20.3 Kah missinninnuog penuanumaog Mosesoh kah yeuog, nꝏ̄waog, napehnont nuppꝏ̄ogkus nematin napuk ut anaquabit Jehovah.
20.4 Kah tohwutch yeu paudtauog umoeuwehkomonk Jehovah en yeu touohkomukqut naut nuppunat, nenawun kah netasumunónog,?
20.5 Kah tohwutch kukkuhkꝏ̄áheog wutch Egypt, kuppasꝏ̄inneanônut yeu matche ayeuonganit ne matta tannegenninno wuskannem, asuh figsash asuh weenomesippogwash, asuh pomegranatsash, kah wanne nippeno wuttattamunat.
20.6 Kah Moses kah Aaron moncheog wutch anaquabit moeuwehkomonk: en mukkinneaekomukque squontamut, kah nag penshadtamwog wuskesukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, kah wussosumóonk Jehovah wunnáeihtunkquneau.
20.7 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
20.8 Nemunush pogkomunk, kah moetash mukìneonk, ken kah Aaron kemat, kah kenꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k qussuk ut anaquabhettit, kah pish nippeyeuꝏ̄; kah pish nah kussohhꝏ̄wutaauóog nippe wutch qussukquanit, kah pish kꝏ̄tattamweh mukkinneonk, kah wunnetassumꝏ̄oh.
20.9 Kah Moses nemunum pogkomunk wutch anaquabit Jehovah neanannꝏ̄nnont.
20.10 Kah Moses kah Aaron moenumwog moeuwehkomunk anaquohtag qussuk, kah nah wuttinuh, nꝏ̄tiegk yeuyeu kenaau cheketamógish, sun woh kussohhꝏ̄wuttauunumun nippe wutch yeu qussukquanit?
20.11 Kah Moses spunum wunnutcheg, kah togkodtam qussuk nashpe uppogkomunk neesit, kah mꝏ̄cheke nippe sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ kah mukkìnneonk wuttattam, kah wunnetassuꝏ̄oh.
20.12 Kah Jehovah, unau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh, newutche matta kꝏ̄namptiyeumwꝏ̄ kꝏ̄neetupanatamwahinneaóut ut anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Israel, ne waj matta pish paudtauonog yeu moeuwehkomonk, en | ohkeit uttiyeu anumauógkup.
20.13 Yeu Meribahe nippe, newutche wunnaumonuh Israel penuánumáog Jehovah: kah noh wunnetupanatamwaheau nashpe nagoh.
20.14 Kah Moses annꝏ̄nau anꝏ̄naeneuh wutch Kadesh en ketassꝏ̄tamwut Edom: yeu wuffin kemat Israel, Kꝏ̄wahteoh wame pomushaonk ne namhikqueog.
20.15 Kah nꝏ̄shinnonog womussuog en Egypt kah nꝏ̄tohtimun Egypt mꝏ̄chetikquinne, kah Egyptiansog nummatchenehikqunnonog kah en nꝏ̄shinnonut.
20.16 Kah nummauunnitteomun Jehovah kah nꝏ̄tam nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonganun, kah annꝏ̄nau Angelsoh, kah nussohhꝏ̄wunukqun wutche Egypt, kah kusseh, yeuyeu nutáyimun Kadesh, keitotan ongkoue kꝏ̄quaiyeumut.
20.17 Paumushaudtunkanan, kꝏ̄wehquetumoush kutohkit, matta pish nuppannupwushomun kutohteakonit, asuh pashpe kꝏ̄weenominneohtekonit, asuh matta nꝏ̄tattammun nippe wuttuhhamonganit: pish nuppomushaumun ketassꝏ̄t vuttóuꝏ̄maogqut, matta nukquìnnupumun en unninohkouneiyeu, asuh menadcheaneiyeu, no pajeh paumukomog kussissepoiyeumut.
20.18 Kah Edom wuttinuh, matta pish kuppánnupuhkiyeuh, ishkont kutayeuuhkonittue sohwehtoush, nashpe togkodteg.
20.19 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel wuttinuh, Pish nukkuhkukquemun én touꝏ̄máogquehtu, kah, wuttattamog kenippem, nen kah netassumunnonog: neit kutoadtuhkoush, weebe matta wonk toh ussenat, nuppaumusham ut nusseetut.
20.20 Kah nꝏ̄wau matta pish kuppaumushoh. kah Edom wutayeuuhkonittue peyaonuh weeche mꝏ̄cheke missinninnuog, kah nashpe menuhke menutcheg.
20.21 Kah Edom sekeneám wuttenanumonat Israeloh pannupwushonat wutohke, kah Israel panneau wutche nahoh.
20.22 Kah nag ꝏ̄mwog Kadesh, kah wunnaumonuh Srael, mamusse mukkinneonk peyaog wadchuut Hor.
20.23 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh kah Aaronoh, ut wadchuut Hor kishke wôhkoe wutohkinit Edom, nꝏ̄wau,
20.24 Aaron pish mukkinnu en ummissinninnumut, newutche matta pish petutteau ohkeit ne anumauog wunnaumonuh Israel, newutche kutcheketamumwop nuttinnꝏ̄waonk ut Meribahe nippekontu.
20.25 Neemun Aaron kah Eliazer wunnaumonuh, kah ogquodchuwaunꝏ̄k wadchuut Hor.
20.26 Kah poshkin Aaron wuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah wuthogquanonash Eliazeroh wunnaumonuh, kah Aaron pish miyaeu kah na pish wuttit nuppun.
20.27 Kah Moses wutussen nean annꝏ̄non(t) Jehovah, kah ogquodchuwaog wadchuut Hor, ut wuskesukqut wame mukkinneonk.
20.28 Kah Moses poshkinau Aaronoh wuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah upponamauónash Eleazaroh wunnaumonuh; kah Aaron na wuttit nuppun ut koduhkôag wadchuut. kah Moses kah Eleazar wꝏ̄msuog wutch wadchuut.
20.29 Kah wame mukkinneonk nauáog Aaron nuppꝏ̄, kah maueemaog Aaronoh shwinchadtikquinne wame wek Israel,
21.1 KAh uk-Kanaanit ketassꝏ̄t Arad, noh wadahkit sowaniyeu, nꝏ̄tam Israel peyau, ut mayut neg natauatunkeg: kah ayeuuhkonau Israeloh, kah nah nohwhutch ummissinnohkonuh
21.2 Kah Israel quoshomau quoshomáonk Jehovah, kah nꝏ̄waog, magꝏ̄e magꝏ̄an, yeug missinninnung ut nunnutchegani, neit pish nuppapaquáne paguatoh, nag kah wutotanâoash.
21.3 Kah Jehovah nꝏ̄tam ꝏ̄wadtauwatonkqussuonk Israel, kah magꝏ̄ uk-Kananitoh, kah neh uppapaquanne paguanóuh, kah wutꝏ̄tanaoash kah wutussꝏ̄wetamun ne ayeuonk Hormah.
21.4 Kah nag moncheog wutch wadchuut Hor, en nogque musque ketahhannit, uhquinnuppuhkomunnaóut wutotu Edom, kah ukketeahogkounꝏ̄oh mishanántamwog, newutche may,
21.5 Kah missinninnuog ayeuuhkone kenꝏ̄naog Goduh, kah ayeukone Mosesoh, toh wutch sohhꝏ̄wusseog wutch Egypt, nuppunnanónut ut touohkomuk? newutche matta petukquenunkaninno, asuh matta nuppeno, kah nukketeahogkôunun uhquontam yeu nunkane petukqunnunk,
21.6 Kah Jehovah anꝏ̄nau en kenugke missinninnûut nꝏ̄tae askꝏ̄koh, kah nag sogkepwaog missinninnúh, kah monáog Israelle missinninnuog nuppꝏ̄og.
21.7 Kah missinninnuog peyaonáog Mosesoh, kah nꝏ̄waog, Nummatchesemun, newutche nutayeuuhkene kenꝏ̄nômun Jehovah, kah ayeuuhkone ken, peantamau Jehovah, wutamaunónat askꝏ̄koh wutch nuhhogkanonut, kah Moses peantamwansheau missinninnuh:
21.8 Kah Jehevah unnau Mosesoh, Ayeu nꝏ̄tae askꝏ̄k, kah ponsh qunnuhtugqut. kah pish nnih, nishnoh sagkepwut, noh moninneog, pìsh pomantam.
21.9 Kah Moses ayeuau wompohshogque askꝏ̄koh, kah upponuk qunnuhtugqut, kah pish n nih, tohneit askꝏ̄k sogkepwont wosketompuh, monunneauont wompuhshogque askꝏ̄koh pomantamup:
21.10 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel moncheog, kah tuppuksinwog ut Oboth.
21.11 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Oboth, kah tuppuksinwog ut Ije-Abarim, ut touohkomukqut ne anaquohtag Moab, nogque adt pashpishont,
21.12 Na ꝏ̄muneau[,] kah tuppuksinwog ꝏ̄nôuhkoiyéuut Zared.
21.13 Na ꝏ̄muneau kah tuppuksinwog ogkomuk Arnon, ne ut touohkomukqut, ne wadshunk wutch ꝏ̄hquaiyeumꝏ̄óut Amoritsog, newutche Arnon weekqshik Moab, nanashauwe Moab kah Amorite.
21.14 Newajeh nꝏ̄womuk ut bꝏ̄kut, Wutayeuwehteaongash Jehovah, uttoh aseip ut musque ketahhannit, ut sepuesehtu Arnon.
21.15 Kah ukkussitchuannꝏ̄onk sepuwussash, ánitchuogish wutayeuonganit Ar, kah paudshunk uhquae Moab.
21.16 Ne wutch en Beer, ne wuttahhamunk ne papaume anomp Jehovah Mosesoh, Moin missinninnuog, kah nuttinnumauóog n(i)ppe.
21.17 Neit Israel unnꝏ̄hamáog yeu unnꝏ̄homaonk, Sohwutchuanish woi wuttahhamonk, nampꝏ̄hamwontamꝏ̄k kenaau,
21.18 Wuttahhamonk, sontimóog ukkuthamuneau ahtúshkouwaog ut missinninnutú, ukkuthamuneau. weeche nanaweheunt naumatuongash, nashpe wutanwohꝏ̄unꝏ̄oash. Kah wutch touohkomukqut auog Máttanah:
21.19 Kah wutch Mattanah en Nahaliel, kah wutch Nahaliel en Bamoth.
21.20 Kah wutch Bamoth en ꝏ̄nôwohteaiyeuut ne ohteuhkonit Moab, uppuhkuk Pisgah, kah unnꝏ̄hquashin nogque Jeshimon.
21.21 Kah Israel annꝏ̄nau annꝏ̄naéneuh en Sihon Amoritse kesassꝏ̄t, nꝏ̄wau,
21.22 Pannupshad° kutohk, matta pish nuppanneaumun en ohteakonit, asuh en weenominneahtekonit, matta nꝏ̄tattamꝏ̄mau wuttahhamungane nippe, pish nuppomushaumun ketassꝏ̄tamwe toumáogquehtu, nô pajeh paumuhkomog kussissippóiyeumash.
21.23 Kah Sihon matta unnanumau paumushag Israeloh wutohkit: qut Sihon mukkinnau wame ummissinninneumoh, kah ayeuuhkonittue sohhamꝏ̄onáog Israeloh en touohkomuk, kah peyau Jahaz, kah ayeuuhkonau Israeloh.
21.24 Kah Israel wuttogkomuh nashpe kenag togkodteg, kah ahtóog wutohke wutch Arnon en J(a)bbok, nô pajeh wunneechanoh Ammon: newutche wussissippoiyeumꝏ̄ Ammon menuhki.
21.25 Kah Israel wunnéemunumunash wame yeush keitotanash, kah Israel wutohtu ut wame ukkehtotanaôut Amoritsog, ut Heshbon, kah wutꝏ̄tanamesehtu.
21.26 Newutche Heshbon wutꝏ̄tan Sihon Amoritse ketassꝏ̄t kah noh mahche ayeuuhkonont negonne ketassꝏ̄timwoh Moab, kah | kah nemon[u]m wame wutohke wutch wunnutcheganit pajh Arnon.
21.27 Newajeh neg napwꝏ̄acheg, nꝏ̄waog, Peyonk Heshbon, ukkei(t)otan Sihon ayimunach kah quoshauwehtamunach.
21.28 Newutche nꝏ̄tau sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wutch Heshbon, nashqunag wutch keitꝏ̄tonat Sihon, paguanomp Ar wutch Moabut, mugquompaog ut ukqunuhkꝏ̄kꝏ̄mmukꝏ̄mut Arnon.
21.29 Missi kuttonkapunáonk Moab kuppagwan woi Chemoshe missinninnuog wunnaumonuh neh pohquohwhunutcheh, yeu kah wuttaunoh ummag(u)nuh en missinnoewunneat, en Sihon Amoritse ketassꝏ̄t.
21.30 Kah nuppepumounonog wutch Heshbon paguanoog, nó pajeh Dibon, kah nag nummahtshannonónog nô pajeh Nophah, né weekqshik Medeba.
21.31 Kah Israel wutohtu wutohtuout Amoritsog.
21.32 Kah Moses anꝏ̄teamꝏ̄ natauwohtinat Jaazer, kah nag neemunumwog ꝏ̄tanamesash, kah quósꝏ̄kauwáog Amoritsoh neh na apinitcheh.
21.33 Kah nag qushkeog, kah auog Bashane mayut; kah Og ketassꝏ̄t ut Bashan wutayeuuhkonittue sohwetauoh, nagum kah wame ummissinninneumoh, ayeuuhkonitinneat ut Edrei
21.34 Kah Jehovah unnou Mosesoh, Ahque qush, newutche en kenutcheganit nummagun nagum kah wame ummissinninnumoh, kah wutohke; kah pish kuttineh, ne anheop Sihon Amoritse ketassꝏ̄t, noh wádohkit Heshbon.
21.35 Kah noh wuttogkomóuh kah wunnaumonuh, kah wame ummissinninnumoh nô pajeh wanne howane ushqunnumauoneat kah nag ahtoog wutohke.
22.1 KAh wunnaumonuh Israel kutchittousháog kah tuppuksinwog Moabe mukoshquttaut, wutushamese Jordan, kishke Jericho.
22.2 Kah Balak wunnaumonuh Zippor, naum wame ne anheont Amoritsoh.
22.3 Kah Moab muttae wabesuóneau missinninnuh, newutche muttaanwog, kah Moab wuttamantam newutche wunnaumonuh Israel.
22.4 Kah Moab unnau Midiane eldersoh yeuyeu yeug ne adtahshiyeuéhettit, pish mahche nꝏ̄squamáog wame neh weenuhkunkqueogeh, onatuh ox mahche nꝏ̄squodtog ashkoshquosh ohteakonit, kah Balak wunnaumonuh Zippor noh ketassꝏ̄t ut Moab na ahquompak.
22.5 Kah annꝏ̄nau annꝏ̄naénuh en Balaam wunnaumonuh Beor, en Pethor, ne kishke sepuut wutohtuôut ummissinninnumoh wunneechanꝏ̄oh; wehkomonat, nꝏ̄wau, kusseh missinninnuog sohhamwog wutch Egypt, kusseh onkhámꝏ̄mꝏ̄og wuskesuk ohke kah nag nuppiuhsukappehtungquog.
22.6 Newutche yeuyeu peyaush kꝏ̄wehquetumoush, matchenanumwehteah yeug missinninnuog, newuche nag nutanuwanꝏ̄mukquog, paguodche woh nuttapenum nag nuttogkomononaóont, kah pish nussohhꝏ̄(h)kauóog wutch ohkit, newutche nꝏ̄wahteoh no wunanumad noh wunnanumau, kah noh matchenanumadt, noh matchenanumau.
22.7 Kah Moabe eldersog, kah Midiane eldersog moncheog nashpe pauwauog onkquatauongánꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash ut wunnutcheganit, kah peyauog Balaam, kah wuttinonnaoash ukkuttꝏ̄wongash Balak.
22.8 Kah nah wuttinuh, yeu kóeuk yeu nohkog, & wonk pish kuppaudtauunumwꝏ̄ kuttꝏ̄wonk, ne woh asit Jehovah: kah Moabbe sontimôog appewonaog Balaamoh.
22.9 Kah God peyaónau Balaamoh, kah nꝏ̄wau, howae wosketompaog yeug weechogqueaneg.
22.10 Kah Balaam unnau Goduh, Balak wunnaumonuh Zippor ketassꝏ̄t ut Moab, annꝏ̄teamo en nuhhogkat.
22.11 Kusseh missinninnuog neg waj sohhogig wutch Egypt, kah nuhkuhkomwog wuskesuk ohke, yeuyeu peyaush, nag matchenanatamah, paguodche pish nuttapenum nag nutayeuuhkononeat, kah pish nussohhꝏ̄kaôog.
22.12 Kah Manit unnau Balaamoh, matta pish nag kꝏ̄weechauóog matta pish kummamatchenoh missinninnuog, newutche nag wunnanumóog.
22.13 Kah Balaam nompoaeu omohkeu, kah unau ukkehtauomoh Balak, onkq kutohtuont, newutche Jehovah sekeneam nuttenanumukqunat kꝏ̄weechaununnaóut.
22.14 Kah Moabe keihtauóog neepoog, kah peyaog Balak, nꝏ̄waog, Balaam sekeneam nꝏ̄weechogqunnanónat.
22.15 Kah Balak wonk annꝏ̄nau keihtauoh anuwanwog, kah anue quttianumukqussuog onk nág.
22.16 Kah nag peyaog Balaam, kah wuttinóuh yeu wussin Balak wunnaumonuh Zippor, ahque wuttamteaush, kꝏ̄wehquetumoush kuppeyauósinat.
22.17 Newutch quttianuttue mꝏ̄cheke kukquihtianumoush, kah uttoh asean, ne nutussen: newutche peyaush kꝏ̄wehquetumoush, kah mamatchetamah yeug missinninnuog.
22.18 Kah Balaam nampꝏ̄ham kah unnau wuttinneumoh Balak, tohneit Balak aninnumaiit weekit numwae silvr kah gold, woh | mo nutanuwuhkomoh wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, oggusussenat asuh mꝏ̄cheke:
22.19 Kah yeuyeu kꝏ̄wehquetumauunumwꝏ̄ kenaeu wonk yeu appek yeu nuhkog, onk woh nꝏ̄wahteoh uttoh woh wonk asit Jehovah[.]
22.20 Kah God peyaonau Balaam nukkonaeu kah wuttinuh, wosketompaog peyahettit wehkomukquean, omkish kah weechau: qut ohch kuttꝏ̄wonk ne anun, ne pish kutussen.
22.21 Kah Balaam omohkeu nompoaeu, appappuwunnéheau wutassumoh, kah weechaau Mo[]b(e) sontimôog.
22.22 Kah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk God nashqunau, newutche monchu, kah wutangelumoh Jehovah ponau wuhhogkuh mayut ayeuuhkonittue ne(h): kah nayeumukqut wutássumoh, kah neesꝏ̄oh wuskenumoh weechog.
22.23 Kah asse naau wutangelumoh Jehovah neepau mayut, kah wuttogkodteg kodtunausu ohteau wunnutchegnit, kah asse pahchau wutch mayut, kah au ohteuhkonit, kah Balaam togkomau assoh ukquinnuppunnonat en mayut.
22.24 Kah wutangel neepau weenominneohteakone mayut, wonkonous yeu nogque kah wonkonous nanogque.
22.25 Kah asse naau wutangelumoh Jehovah kah kussukshau wonkonnꝏ̄sinut; kah asseetuhkom wusseet Balaam wonkonꝏ̄sinut; kah wonk wuttogkomuh.
22.26 Kah wutangelumoh Jehovah óngkoue au, kah neepau nanahkonchiyeuut, wanne máuunꝏ̄ quinnuppenat, unninuhkóunit, asuh menadcheanit.
22.27 Kah asse naau wutangelumoh Jehovah kah kepshau ut agwe Balaamut; kah Balaam musquanittamꝏ̄onk nashqunau, kah togkomau assoh anwohou,
22.28 Kah Jehovah woshunnum wuttꝏ̄n asse, kah unnau Balaamoh, Toh kittinhesh waj nishwudt nompe togkomean?
22.29 Kah Balaam unnau assoh, newutche kuttôôntóhkoneh, napehnont tokkodteg ohtag nunnutcheganit, newaj yeuyeu woh nushin.
22.30 Kah asse unau Balaamoh, sunummtata nen kutassum, nayeumukquean, na wutch adt wadcháneap yeu pajeh yeu kesukok, sun yeu kuttìnhenunas? kah nꝏ̄wau, Matta.
22.31 Kah Jehovah woshwunnum wuskesukquash Balaam, kah nâau wutangelumoh Jehovah neepau ut mayut, kah wuttogkodteg kodtinausu ohteau wunnutcheganit, ka(h) nauánum uppuhkuk, kah nauánum wuhhog ut wuskesukqut.
22.32 Kah wutangelumoh Jehovah wuttinuh, tohwutch nishwudt nompe togkomadt kutassum? kusseh ayeuuhkonittue nussohham, | newutche kummay panneyeuꝏ̄ ut anaquabeh.
22.33 Kah asse nunnogq, quinuppu ut anaquabeh nishwudt nompe: matta quinuppegis wutch nuhhogkat, wunnamuhkut wonk ken woh kenushish, kah noh woh nuppomantamwah.
22.34 Kah Baleam unau wutangelumoh Jehovah, nummatchesem, newutche matta nꝏ̄wahteoꝏ̄p kutayeuuhkonittue neepauwehtah ut mayut. kah yeuyeu matcheuk ut keskesukqut wonk nukqushkem.
22.35 Kah wutangelumoh Jehovah unnau Balaamoh, weechau wosketompaog, qut webe kuttꝏ̄wonk ne pish anun, ne pish kussin: kah Balaam weechaau ukkeihtauaéneumoh Balak.
22.36 Kah Balak nꝏ̄tam Balaam peyau, kah monchu wunnogskouoh en Moabe ꝏ̄tanat, ne kishke uhquae Arnon, ne aongkoue uhquae.
22.37 Kah Balak unnau Balaamoh sunnummatta nutanꝏ̄teamwe wehkomunꝏ̄? tohwutch matta peyaausean? sunnummatta wunnamuhkut nuttapenumꝏ̄ kukqueihtianumunat.
22.38 Kah Balaam unau Balakoh, kusseh kuppeyaonsh, yeuyeu sun nuttapenum toh unnꝏ̄won? kuttꝏ̄wonk né ponuk nuttꝏ̄nut GOD, ne pish nuffin,
22.39 Kah Balaam weechaau Balakoh, kah peyaog Kirjath Huzoth.
22.40 Kah Balak sephausu oxinoh kah sheepsoh, kah annꝏ̄teamo en Balaamut, kah sontimoh neh weetomukqutcheh.
22.41 Onk nnih mohtompog Balak neemunau Balamoh, ukkuhkuhkꝏ̄unuh en kussokoiyeuut Baal, onk woh na wutch nauon uhquae missinninnúh.
23.1 KAh Balaam unau Balak, yeu ut ayimah, nesausuk tahshinash Altarash, kah yeu ut quoshwunumah nesausuk tahsuog oxinog kah nesausuk tahsuog ramsog.
23.2 Kah Balak wutussen Balaam ne anꝏ̄wadt, & Balak & Balaam sephausuog pasuk ox kah pasuk ram nish noh ut Altaru(t).
23.3 Kah Balaam unnau Balakoh neepaush kishke chikohtae sephausuonganit, kah nummonchem: páguodche Jehovah mos peyau nunnogskunk, kah uttoh kuttꝏ̄wonk mashamiit, mos kuttinnonun, kah au qunnunkqui ayeuonganit.
23.4 Kah GOD nogkuskáuau Balaamoh: kah wuttinuh, nummahche quagwoshwetam nesausuk tahshinash Altarsash, kah nussephausip pasuk ox, kah pasuk ram, ut pasuk Altarut.
23.5 Kah Jehovah ponam kuttꝏ̄wonk Balaam wuttꝏ̄nit, kah nꝏ̄wau, qushkish en Balakut | kah pish yeu kussin;
23.6 Kah noh en qushkeu, kah kusseh neepau kishke wutchikohtaeu sephausuonganit, nagum, kah wame moabe Sontimoh.
23.7 Kah wunnupwoaonk nemunum, kah nꝏ̄wau, Balak ketassꝏ̄t, ut Moab, nuppasꝏ̄ wutch Aram, wutch wutchepwoie wadchuhkontu, nꝏ̄wau, peyaush mamátcheuttama Jakob, kah peyaush matchéus Israel.
23.8 Uttoh woh nuttin mamatchenon, neh God matta mamatche unnonkeh, kah uttoh woh nuttin matcheunnon, neh God matta matcheunnonkeh.
23.9 Newutche wutch woskechepiskquttu nunnau, kah wutch wadchuuhkontu nukkéhkinneau: kusseh missinninnuog pish nussiyeuog, kah matta pish weetogkemóog wutohtimoneat.
23.10 Howan woh woogketog uppuppissiyeum Jakob, & ne adtahshik weyauut chippissuonk Istael, nukketeahogkou nuppitch ut wunnuppꝏ̄onganit sampwéusseáen, kah nꝏ̄wohkukquoiyeum ogqunneunkquotch wuttaiheit.
23.11 Kah Balak unnau Balaamoh, toh kuttinheh? keneemunush kummamatchenonat nummatwaog, kah kusseh kꝏ̄nanittue wunnanumóg.
23.12 Kah nampꝏ̄ham kah nꝏ̄wau, sunnummatta woh nununnukqussuontamꝏ̄h enneyat Jehovah ponuk nuttꝏ̄nut.
23.13 Kah Balak wuttinuh, weechaueh kꝏ̄wehquetumoush en onkatoganit ayeuoogánit onk woh na kꝏ̄che nauoneau, pish webe kenaum ꝏ̄hquayéumꝏ̄ónt, kah matta pish kenauóog wame, kah nag mámatcheuttamah na wutch.
23.14 Kah wunnemunoh en Zophimeh ohteakonit, en koduhkoag pifgah, kah ayim nesausuk tahshinash Altarash; kah sephausu pasukꝏ̄ oxinoh, kah pasukꝏ̄ ramoh nish noh ut Altar.
23.15 Kah unnau Balakoh, yeu kishe neepau kutchikohtae sephausuonganit, kah ya nuttit nogkushkauon.
23.16 Kah Jehovah nogkushkauau Balaamoh, kah ponam kuttꝏ̄wonk wuttꝏ̄nit kah nꝏ̄wau, qushkish en Balakut, kah yeu woh kussin.
23.17 Kah uppeyaonuh kah kusseh neepau kishke wutchikohtae sephausuonganit, kah Moabe sontimóog, weetomuk, kah Balak wuttinuh, toh unnꝏ̄wau Jehovah?
23.18 Kah nemunum wunnupwoaonk kah nꝏ̄wau, nepaush Balak, kah nꝏ̄tash, kukkehtah ken wunnaumonuh Zippor.
23.19 GOD matta wosketomp woh pannꝏ̄wadt, asuh wunnaumonuh Adam woh áiuskoiánatam: ne anꝏ̄wádt, sun woh mat wutusséin[?] kah ne anꝏ̄wadt, kah sun woh mo umménuhkehteaꝏ̄un?
23.20 Kusseh nutattumunum wunanitteae | kuttꝏ̄wonk, kah wunnanitteau, kah matta woh nukqushkenumꝏ̄un.
23.21 Matta naumꝏ̄ matcheséonk ut Jakobut asuh matta naumꝏ̄ panneusseonk ut Israel, Jehovahoh um-Manittꝏ̄moh ꝏ̄weetomuh, kah ketassꝏ̄tamwe mishontꝏ̄waonk ukkenugkushôneau. 23.22 God nah wussꝏ̄hꝏ̄wunoh wutch Egypt, ohtou ummenuhkesuonk onatuh nequttuun.
23.23 Wunnamuhkut na mo ohtano pauwauwonk ayeuuhkonittue Jakob, asuh mat mamontamóowonk ayeuuhkonittue Israel, neaunag yeu ahquompak, pish unnꝏ̄won papaume Jakob kah Israel, uttoh God ananakausit?
23.24 Kusseh missinninnuog pish neepóog onatuh menuhkesue qunnonou, kah pish waápenau wuhogkuh onatuh sꝏ̄kshanuáe qunnónou, matta pish sepsinnau nó pajeh ummahchepwónat neh tohqunoncheh, kah ꝏ̄tattamunat ꝏ̄sqheonk nashit.
23.25 Kah Balak unnau Ba[]aamoh, ahque mamatchenae mamatcheus, asuh wunnanittue wunnanum.
23.26 Kah Balaam nampꝏ̄hamauau Balakoh kah wuttinuh, sunnummatta kuttinnꝏ̄mus, nussip, wame ne Jehovah anꝏ̄wadt ne mꝏ̄che nutussen?
23.27 Kah Balak unnau Balaamoh, peyaush kꝏ̄wehquetumoush, keneemunush en onkatogane ayeuonganit, paguódche ne pish sampoi ut wuskesukqut God, woh nag kummamatcheuttamwanshin na wutch.
23.28 Kah Balak nemunau Balaamoh en koduhkôag Peor, unnuhquaénat nogque Jeshimon.
23.29 Kah Balaam unnau Balakoh, yeuut ayimah nesâusuk tahshinash Altarash, kah yeuut quaquoshwunnumah nesausuk tahsuog oxenog, kah nesausuk tahsuog ramsog.
23.30 Kah Balak wutussen ne anꝏ̄wadt Balaam, kah sephausu oxenoh kah ramoh nish noh Alterut.
24.1 KAh Balaam naum ne wunnegenut wuskesukqut Jehovah, wunnaumonat Israel, kah matta monchu neane negonne neasip, nógkushkomunat pauwauwonk, qut unnunum wuskesuk nogque touohkomuk.
24.2 Kah Balaam ushpunnum wuseksukquash kah naau Israel appuog weetuomtu, neaunag wutchippanꝏ̄onganóoash, kah wunnashánittꝏ̄moh GOD wutapehtunkquoh.
24.3 Kah neemunnum wunnuppowaonk, kah nꝏ̄wau, Balaam wunnaumonuh Beor wunnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau, kah wosketomp noh wuskesukquash woshwohtag, wunnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau.
24.4 Noh wunnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau, noh nꝏ̄tog wutorakisumash GOD, noh nag monomansuonáonk | wame manuhkesit; panshont, kah wuskesukquash woshwemoash.
24.5 Uttoh en wunnenonkquodt kekash woi Jakob, kuttabernaklumash woi Israel?
24.6 Onatuh ꝏ̄nauwohteaiyeuut nag sepakemꝏ̄ug, onatuh tanohketeaongash ut kishketuk: onatuh legn aioes mehtugquash, nish Jehovah ahketeacheh, onatuh utchikkuppuhtugqut kehchippam.
24.7 Noh pish sokenum nippe wutch ꝏ̄thuppaeechꝏ̄ut, kah ꝏ̄skannemunneoh pish ohtaash mꝏ̄natut nippeut, kah ukkehtassꝏ̄tamomoh pish ánue qunnunkqussumau Agagoh, kah ukkehtassꝏ̄tamóonk pish mishehteauun.
24.8 GOD wussohhꝏ̄wunoh wutch Egypt, ohtau menuhkesuonk onatuh nequttuunáut: noh pish mahchippꝏ̄ wutohtimóneash neh onkkuppunanukqutcheh, kah pish upquohquanumauoh wuskonnꝏ̄ash, kah pish uppashpshánuh nashpe ukkóuhquadtash.
24.9 Wishquossun kah sepsin onatuh sꝏ̄kshanuáe qunnónou, & onatuh wuttꝏ̄anumóe qunnônou, howan pish uppassukkꝏ̄kauoh? wunnanumunach noh wánanumukquean, kah mamatchenunach, noh mamatchenukquean.
24.10 Kah Balak ummusquantamꝏ̄onk nashqunnau ayeuuhkone Balaam, kah tokkꝏ̄wóhteau wunnutchegash, kah Balak unnau Balaamoh, kꝏ̄wehkomunup kummamatchenonaôont nummatwomog, kah kusseh wunnanittue kꝏ̄nanumóog nishwudt nompe.
24.11 Kah yeuyeu ushshash kutayeuonganit, nussip quttianittue kukquttianumoush, qut kusseh Jehovah kukkuphamunk wutch quttianittinneat.
24.12 Kah Balaam unnau Balakoh, sunnummatta ne wonk nuttinnonaóus kutannꝏ̄naénûog, neg annꝏ̄nutcheg en nuhhogkat, nussip.
24.13 Tohneit Balak aninnumaiit numwâe wckit silver kah gold, matta woh nutanuúhkomꝏ̄h wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah, wunnesenat asuh matchesenat wutch nehenwonche nuttahhut. uttoh anꝏ̄wadt Jehovah, ne nussin.
24.14 Kah yeuyeu kussee nuttóm nummissinninneumut: yehoh kuttinsh uttoh pish anheáhettit, yeug missinninnuog kummissinninnúmoh, ut ogkomae kesukodtut.
24.15 Kah nemunum wunnuppoáonk, kah nꝏ̄wau, Balaam wunnaumonuh Beor wúnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau, kah wosketomp noh wuskusukquash woshwohtag, wunnamuhkut nꝏ̄wau.
24.16 Noh mahche nꝏ̄wau, noh nꝏ̄tog wutoraklsumash GOD, kah wahteunk ꝏ̄wahteauonk quanunkquapit, noh nag monomansuonáonk wame manuhkesit, noh panshont, kah wuskesukquosh woshwohtaash.
24.17 Noh pish nunnau qut yeuyeu matta, pish nukkeikeneau, qut matta paswe, na pish | ꝏ̄ch sohhamun anogqs Jakobut, kah scepter pish waabemꝏ̄ wutch Israelut kah pish pannuppe togkomau wunnahnaiyeumash Moab kah pish paguanau wame wunneechanoh Seth.
24.18 Kah Edom pish ahtóonganuꝏ̄, kah Seir pis[n] ahtóonganuꝏ̄ wutche ummatwómuh, kah Israel pish menuhke ussu.
24.19 Kah noh pish ohtau nanauwunnuwaonk wutch Jakob: kah pish p(a)guanau neh ashqunutcheh ut otanahtu.
24.20 Kah monunneau Amalekoh, & nemunum wunnuppꝏ̄aonk kah nꝏ̄wau, Amalek mo negonne wutohtimmowonganuꝏ̄, qut ꝏ̄wohkukquoiyeumun ne, noh pish micheme awakompanau,
24.21 Kah unnuhquaeu Kenitut, kah nemunum wunnuppꝏ̄aonk kah nꝏ̄wau, Menuhki kutayeuonk, kah kupponam kꝏ̄wad(t)ch qussukquanit.
24.22 Qut Kain pish mâhtshau, nô pajeh Ashur pish kummissunohkônukqunat.
24.23 Kah nemunum wunnuppꝏ̄aonk kah nꝏ̄wau, Touwane, howan woh pomantog, God yeu usseit?
24.24 Kah kuhtonogquosh pish Peyaumóash wutch wohkoe Kittim, kah pish onkapunanau Ashuroh, kah pish onkapunanou Heberoh, kah noh pish wonk micheme awakompanau.
24.25 Kah Balaam neepau, kah monchu, kah qushkeu au nehenwonche wutayeuonganit, kah Balak wonk moncheoh.
25.1 KAh Israel ayeuog Shittim, kah missinninnuog nꝏ̄che mamussuog wuttaunoh Moab.
25.2 Kah nag wehkomaog missinninnuh en wussephamauonganꝏ̄óut ummanittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh: kah missinninnuog meetsuog kah nauwaeitauwaog nag ummanittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh.
25.3 K(a)h Israel mosogquehtauaog Baal Peoroh: kah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk Jehovah nïshqunneau ayéuuhkonittue Israel.
25.4 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh neemunush wame uppuhkukkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash missinninnuog kah wóoshas anaquabit Jehovah piuhsuke nepáuzsaut, onk woh ummishe musquanittamꝏ̄onk Jehovah qushkemo wutch Israelut.
25.5 Kah Moses unnau Israelle wussittumwaenuh nushꝏ̄k nish noh kittinneumꝏ̄óog neg mósogquehtauoncheg Baal Peoroh,
25.6 Kah kusseh wosketomp wunnaumonuh Israel peyau, kah pasꝏ̄chewunnau weematut Midianite mittamwossis, ut wuskesukqut Moses, kah wuskesukꝏ̄out wame ummukkinneonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel kah nag mauwe appuog mukkinneaekommukque squoantamut.
25.7 Kah Phineas wunnaumonuh Ele[]zer, wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen wunnauoh | kah neepau wutch kenugke mukkinneonkanit, kah neemunum kenanwohhou wunnutcheganit.
25.8 Kah asuhk[a]e petutteaumꝏ̄ Israelle wosketompuh en wetuomut, kah wunnaneeswe konnukkehtahwhoh Israelle wosketompoh, kah mittamwossisoh, pannuppe wunnogkussit, kah enninneaonk togkogqushomꝏ̄, wutch wunnaumonat Israel.
25.9 Kah yeug adt nuppukig enninneaónganit neesneechage kah yauwe muttannonganog kussuog.
25.10 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄náu Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
25.11 Phineas wunnaumonuh Eli(a)zer, wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuen, qushkinum nummusquantamꝏ̄onk wutch wunnaumonuh Israel, Zealussuit newutche neen, ut kenukke nagoh, newaj matta mahtuppannóagkup ut nu(m)mꝏ̄sitteamonea(t).
25.12 Newutche nꝏ̄w(a)sh: kusseh nuttinnonnumau wunohteae nꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk,
25.13 Kah pish ohtou, kah ꝏ̄skannemunneoh nahohtoeu, wunnꝏ̄waonk wutch michemohtag. sephausue aninnohsuenuonk, newutche mꝏ̄sitteamowanshau um Manittꝏ̄moh, kah wunnauwadtuwaheau wunnaumonuh Israel.
25.14 Kah ꝏ̄wesuonk Israelle wosketomp, noh togkomut, noh weeche togkomomukkup Mideanite mittamwossis Zimrì, wunnau(m)onuh Salu, Sontim ut ꝏ̄shoh wekit, wutch Simeonitsog.
25.15 Kah ꝏ̄wesuonk Midianite mittamwossis noh togkomomukup Cozbi wuttaunuh Zur; noh wobuhkuhkꝏ̄it ut wutohtimmoinneat, ꝏ̄shoh weekit ut Midian.
25.16 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
25.17 Mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄squeh Midianitsog, kah nag togkommꝏ̄k.
25.18 Newutche nag kummamꝏ̄skhikkꝏ̄ôog nashpe ꝏ̄nompuwussuonganꝏ̄oash, nish nashpe asꝏ̄kekomukqueôgish wadchiikish Peorut, kah wadchiukish Cozbi wuttaunoh Sontim ut Middian, weetompassuoh, noh togkomomukup, ut enninneaongane kesukodtut, newutche Peor.
26.1 ONk nnih mahche enninneaonganeug, Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, kah en Eleazarut, wunnaumonuh Aaron sephausuaen nꝏ̄wau,
26.2 Ogkem wame mukkinneonk wunnaumonuh Israel wutch wunneesinchage kodtumwohkomunnáout kah paamu, neaunag ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wekꝏ̄óash, nishnoh pasuk noh sohhog ut ukkenauwameonganit Israel.
26.3 Mah moses kah Eleazar sephausuen nah ukkekétꝏ̄hkauóuh ut Moabe mukoshquttaut, | kishke Jordan, kishke Jericho, nꝏ̄waog.
26.4 Wutch wunneesnechage kodtumwohkomunnaout. kah paamu, neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh, kah wunnaumonuh Israel, neg sohhogig wutch ohkit Egypt.
26.5 Ruben mohtommegit ut Israelut, wunnaumonuh Ruben, Enoch neh wadchekhetticheh Enochitsog, Phallu neh wadchekhetticheh Phalluitsog.
26.6 Hezron neh wadchekhetticheh Hezronitsog; Carmi neh wadchekhetticheh Carmitsog.
26.7 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Rubenitsog, kah yeug nag ag(ke)mutcheg, yauunchage kah nishwe muttannong(a)nogkussuog, kah ncsausuk tahshit pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, kah nishwinchag.
26.8 Kah wunnau[m]onuh Phallu Eliab.
26.9 Kah wunnaumonuh Eliab, Nemuel, kah Dathan, kah Abiram, yeouh noh Dathan kah Abiram, waeenomutcheg ut mukkinneonganit, neg ayeuuhkononcheg Mosesoh, kah Aaronoh, ut kenugke waabecheg Korah, ayeuhkonáhettit Je[n]ovah.
26.10 Kah ohke woshwunum wuttꝏ̄n, kah ummisseashquìnneuh, kah Korahoh, mukkinneonk napꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk, nꝏ̄tau chagoswont neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄oh wosketompuh kah napanna tahshinchag, kah nag kuhkinneasuonganuꝏ̄panneg.
26.11 Qut wunnaumonuh Korah matta nuppꝏ̄og.
26.12 Wunnaumonuh Simeon neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash. Nemuel, wadchekhetticheh Nemuelitsog, Jamin, wadchekhetticheh Jaminitsog; Jachin wadchekhetticheh Jachinitsog.
26.13 Ze(r)ah, wadchekhetticheh Zarhitsog, Shaul wadchekhetticheh Shaulitsog.
26.14 Yeush wutteateashiyeuongash Simeonitsog, neeneechage kah neese muttannonganog kussuog, kah neese pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.15 Wunnaumonuh Gad neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash: Zephon neh wadchekhetticheh Zephonitsog: Haggi neh wadchekhetticheh Haggitsog: Shuni neh wadchekhetticheh Shunitsog,
26.16 Ozni, neh wadchekhetticheh Oznitsog: Eri, neh wadchekhetticheh Eritsog.
26.17 Arod, neh wadchekhetticheh Aroditsog: Areli. neh wadchekhet[t]tcheh Arelitsog.
26.18 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Gad, kah yeug neg agkemutcheg, yauunchage muttannonganog kussuog kah napanna tahshe pasuk.
26.19 Wunnaumonuh Judah, Er kah Onan: kah Er kah Onan nuppꝏ̄og ut ohkit Kanáan.
26.20 Kah wunnaumonuh Judah neaunag wutteateáshiyeuonganꝏ̄oash: Selah neh | wadchekhettichoh Selahitsog: Phares neh wadchekhettic(h)eh Pharezitsog: Zerah neh wa(dch)ekhett(i)cheh Z(e)rahitsog
26.21 Kah wunnaumonuh Pharez: Hesron neh wadchekhetticheh Hezronitsog: Hamul neh wadchekhetticheh Ham(u)litsog.
26.22 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ash Judah, yeug neg agkemutcheg nesausuk tahshinchage kah nequtta muttannonganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasuk.
26.23 Wunnaumonuh Isachar neaunag wutteateashiyeuo(n)genꝏ̄oash: Thola neh wadchekhetticheg Thol(a)hitsog: Phua neh wadchekhetticheh Phunitsog:
26.24 J(a)shub, neh wadchekhetticheh Jashubitsog: Simron neh wadchekhetticheh Si(m)ronitsog.
26.25 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Issachar, yeug neg nah agkemutcheg, nequtta tahshinchage kah yaue muttannonganogkussuog kah nishwe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.26 wunnaumonuh Zabulon neaunag wutteateashiyeuo(n)ganꝏ̄oash, Serad neh wadchekhetticheh Sarditsog: Elon neh wadchekhetticheh Elonitsog: Jahleel neh wadchekhetticheh Jahleelitsog.
26.27 Yeush w(u)tteateas(h)iyeuonganꝏ̄oash Zabulonitsog. neg nah agkemutcheg, nequtta tahshinchage muttannonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasuk.
26.28 Wunnaumonuh Joseph neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Manasses kah Ephraim.
26.29 Wunnaumonuh Manasses: Machir neh wadchekhetticheh Machiritsog: kah Machir wunnaumonieu Gilead kah neh wadchekhetticheh Gileaditsog.
26.30 Yeu wunnaumonuh Gilead: Jeezer neh wadchekhetticheh Jeezeritsog: Helek neh wadchekheticheh Helekitsog.
26.31 Kah Asrìel neh wadchekhetticheb Asrielitsog: Shechem neh wadchekhtticheh Shechemitsog
26.32 Shemida neh wadchekhetticheh Shemidaitsog: Hepher neh wadchekhetticheh (H)epheritsog.
26.33 Kah Zelophehad wunnaumonuh Hepher wanne wunnaumonieu, qut wuttaunieu: kah ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ wuttaunoh Zelophehad, Machlah, kah Noah, Hoglah, Milchah, kah Tirzah.
26.34 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Manasses, kah neg nah ágkemutcheg, napanna tahshinchage kah neese muttanonganogkussuog, kah nesausuk tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.35 Yeush wunnaumonuh Ephraim neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash. Shuthelah neh wadchekhettiche Shuthelahitsog: Becher neh wadchekhetticheh Becheritsog Tahan ne wadchekhetticheh Tahanitsog.
26.36 Kah yeuh wunnaumonuh Shuthelah: Eran neh wadchekhetticheh Eranitsog.
26.37 Yeush wutteateashiyeonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Ephraim, neg nah agkemutcheg, nishwinchage kah neese muttanonganogkussuog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, yeuh wunnaumonuh Joseph neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash.
26.38 Wunnaumonuh Benjamin nenunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Bela, neh wadchekhetticheh Belaltsog: Ashbel neh wadchekhetticheh Ashbelitsog: Ahiram neh wadchekhetticheh Ahiramitsog.
26.39 Shephupham neh wadchehetticheh Shephuphamitsog: Hupham neh wadchekhetticheh Huphamitsog.
26.40 Kah wunnaumonuh Bela, Ard kah Naaman, neh wadchekhetticheh Arditsog, kah Naaman neh wadchekhetticheh Naamitsog.
26.41 Yeuh wunnaumonuh Benjamin neaunag wutteateshiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, kah nag nah agkemutcheg yauunchage kah napanna tahshe muttannonganogkussuog, kah nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.42 Yeuh wunnaumonuh Dan neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, Shuham neh wadchekhetticheh Shuhamitsog: yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Dan neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash.
26.43 Wame Shuhamitsog wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash neg nah agkemutcheg, nequttá tahshinchage kah yaue muttannonganogkuss(u)og, kah yaue pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.44 Wunnaumonuh Aser neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Jimnah neh wadchekhetticheh Jimnitsog: Jishvi neh wadchekhetticheh Jishvitsog: Beriah neh wadchekhetticheh Beriitsog.
26.45 Wunnaumonuh Beriah: Chebar neh wadchekhetticheh Cheberitsog: Malchiel neh wadchekhetticheh Malchielitsog,
26.46 Kah ꝏ̄wesuonk wuttaunoh Aser, Serah.
26.47 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Aser, neg nah agkemutcheg napanna tahshinchage kah nishwe muttannonganogkussuog, kah yaue pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.48 Wunnaumonuh Naphtali neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash: Jahzeel neh wadchekhetticheh Jahzeelitsog: Guni neh wadchekhetticheh Gunitsog.
26.49 Jazer neh wadchekhetticheh Jezritsog Shillem neh wadchekhetticheh Shillemitsog,
26.50 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Nahpthali, neaunag wutteateashiyeuongannꝏ̄oash, kah neg noh agkemutcheg, yauunchage kah napanna tahshe muttannonganogkussuog kah yaue pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
26.51 Yeug adt ogkemutcheg wunnaumonat Israel nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganagkussuog kah nequt muttannonk kah nesausuk tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og kah shwinchag.
26.52 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
26.53 Yeug en ohke pish chadchabenumun wutch(e) ahtóonk, neane ogketamuk wesuongash,
26.54 Neg monacheg pish kummꝏ̄che aninnumauóog ohtóonk, kah neg ogguhsikeg, pish kutogguhse aninnumauóog ahtïonk, neane yeug agkemutcheg ahtóonk pish aninnumauau nishnoh wosketomp.
26.55 Qut oh(c)h ohke pish chachábenumun nashpe tanohtóadtuonk: neaaunag ꝏ̄wesuongꝏ̄oash wutchippanꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh wutꝏ̄shimóog, nag pish wutohtauuneau.
26.56 Neaunag tanohtóadtuonk, ohtóonk pish chadchaubenumun, ut nashauwe monachek kah ogguhsikeg.
26.57 Kah yeug nag agkemutcheg nashpe Levitsog, neaunag wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash, Gershom neh wadchekhetticheh Gershomitsoh Kohath neh wadchehetticheh Kohahitsog, Merari neh wadchekhetticheh. Meraritsog.
26.58 Yeush wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄oash Levitsoh, wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Lihnitsog, wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Hebronìtsog, wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Mahlitsog, wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Mushitsog, wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ Korachitsog kah Kahath wunnaumonieu Amram.
26.59 Kah ꝏ̄wesuonk Amram ummittamwussoh Jachebed wuttaunoh Levi, noh wadchekhetteup Levi ut Egypt, kah noh neeketeauau Amramoh, kah Aaronoh kah Mosesoh kah Miriamoh neg weetompassꝏ̄oh
26.60 Kah Aaronut wutchetu Nadab kah Abihu Eleazar kah Ithamar.
26.61 Kah Nadab kah Abihu nuppꝏ̄og, neg sephaushettit penowe nꝏ̄tau ut anaquabit Jehovah.
26.62 Kah yeug nah wetogkomutcheg neesneechage kah nishwe muttanunganog kussuog wame nompaassog, wutch wunnukqut nepáuz apinneat, kah paamu, newutche matta nag weetogkemóog wunnaumonát Israel newutche wanne ahtóonk aninnumauóog, ut kenugke wunnaumonat Israel.
26.63 Yeug nag ogkemutcheg nashpe Moses kah Eleazer sephausuaen, neg ogkemutcheg wunnaumonát Israel, ut Moabe mukóshquttaut, kishke Jotdan; kishke Jericho.
26.64 Kah kenugke yeug, wanne mo pasuk wosketomp yeug agke(m)omukuppanneg nashpe Moses kah Aaron sephausuen, neg agkemahetteupoh wunnaumonuh Israel ut touohkomukqut Sinai
26.65 Newutche Jehovah wuttinópoh, nuppꝏ̄e pish nuppꝏ̄og ut touohkomukqut, kah matta pasuk wosketomp ꝏ̄che pomantamꝏ̄un webe Kaleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh, kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun,
27.1 NEit peyáog wuttaunoh Zelophehad wunnaumonuh Hepher, wunnaumonuh Gilead, wunnaumonuh Machir, wunnaumonuh Manasses, wutch wutteateashiyeuonganit Manasses, wunnaumonuh Joseph, & yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wuttaunoh, Mahlah, Noah kah Hoglah, kah Milchah kah Tirzah.
27.2 Kah nag neepóog anaquabit Moses kah Ele(a)zur sephausuen, kah anaquabhettit Sontimóog, kah wame mukkinneonk, ut mukkinneae kommukque squantamut, nꝏ̄waog.
27.3 Nꝏ̄shun nuppꝏ̄ ut touohkomukqut, kah matta nah weetshóunuh en ummukkinneonganit neg ayeuhkonittue moehtauoncheg Johovah, ut ummukkinneanganit Korah: qut ut ummatcheseonganit nuppꝏ̄, kah wanne wunnaumonaeu.
27.4 Tohwutch woh ꝏ̄wesuonk Nꝏ̄shun mahtsheau, wutch kenugke wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄, newutche matta wunnaumonieu? aninnumaiinnean ahtoonk ut kenugke weemat ut nꝏ̄shun.
27.5 Kah Moses pasꝏ̄au wuttinniyeuonganꝏ̄ ut anaquabit Jehovah.
27.6 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
27.7 Wuttaunoh Zelophehad wunnomwaog, magꝏ̄an pish nag kittinnumauóog ahtoonk ut kenugke weemattꝏ̄óut ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh: kah pish paumushahto wutahtóonganꝏ̄ wutꝏ̄shinneunk na en.
27.8 Kah pish kukkinnꝏ̄n wunnaumonuh Israel, pish kussim, wosketomp nupuk, kah wanne wunnaumononieg, neit pish kupaumusháhto wutohtóonk en wuttonit.
27.9 Kah matta wuttauneg, neit pish kummag wutahtóonk en wematut.
27.10 Kah matta ꝏ̄weemateg, neit pish kummag wutahtóonk en ꝏ̄shoh weematoh.
27.11 Kah ꝏ̄shoh matta ꝏ̄weemattinneg, neit pish kummag wutahtóonk, en wuttinnonkumóut neh asukongqutcheh ut wutteashiyeonganit, kah noh pish wutahtauun kah ne pish wutch wunnaumonuh Israel wussittumóe kuhkꝏ̄wáonk, nean annꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh.
27.12 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, kukkúhquish yeu en wadchuut Abarìm, kah naish ohke ne anumauog wunnaumonuh Israel
27.13 Kah mahche nauman, kah ken wonk pìsh kummaiyáim, en kummissinninnúmut, neâne Aaron kemat maiáyip,
27.14 Newutche kutcheketamumwꝏ̄ nuttinnꝏ̄waonk (ut touohkomukqut Zin, mukkinneonk penuánutit) en waneetupanatamwaheóg ut nippeit, ut anaquabhettit, ne Meribahe nippe, ut Kadesh, ut touohkomukqut Zin.
27.15 Kah Moses kenꝏ̄nau Jehovah nꝏ̄wau.
27.16 Jehovah ummanittꝏ̄moh wunnashánittꝏ̄onganash wame weyaus, pononch wosketompuh nananumunat mukkinneonk.
27.17 Noh woh sohhog ut anaquabhettit, kah woh petutteau ut anaquabenit: kah noh woh neh sohwhe sagkompagunoncheh, kah noh woh pethuunont, onk woh mat ummukkinnumoh Jehovah ogqueneunkqusseo(h) shepsut wannch wananauwushepsaweneumégig.
27.18 Kah Jehovah unnau Mosesoh, nemun Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun, wosketomp noh app(e)htunkqut nashauanittꝏ̄h. kah ponumau kenutcheg.
27.19 Kah neepauweh ut anaquabit Eleazar sephausuen, kah anaquabit wame mukkinneonk, kah meechumuhkos ut nag anaquabhettit.
27.20 Kah pish kuthogquon kukquehtianumitteaonk, onk woh wame ummukkeneonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel nꝏ̄tamwog.
27.21 Kah noh pish n(e)epau anaquabit Eleaz(e)r sephausuen, kah noh pish wunnatꝏ̄tomwehteaunshuh nashpe wussittumôe Urim, anaquabit Jebovah: ut ukkuttꝏ̄wonganit pish sohhamwog, kah ut ukkuttꝏ̄wonganit pish petutteaog, kah wame wunnaumonuh Istael weechog kah wame mukkinnéonk.
27.22 Kah Moses wutussen neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah, kah nemunau Joshuahoh, kah wunneepauweheuh anaquabit Eleazer sephausuen kah anaquabit wame mukkinneonk.
27.23 Kah upponumau wunnutchegash. kah meechumuhkonuh, ne anꝏ̄wop Jehovah, nashpe wunnutchegani(t) Moses.
28.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau.
28.2 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel kah us, nuttinnussephamonteaonk, nuppetukqunnunk wutch nutchikohteae sephamonteaongash, wutche nꝏ̄weetemungquottꝏ̄m, pish kehkinneafimwꝏ̄ kussephamaiinneaóut ut kuhquetumóe uttꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ut.
28.3 Kah nag pish kuttinóog, yeu chikohtae magꝏ̄onk ne pish sephamauog Jehovah, neesuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog pannuppeyeuutcheg, asekesukokish wutche nagwutteae sephausuonk.
28.4 Pasuk lamb pish kukquaqoshwun nompoáe, kah onkatuk lambe pish kukquaquoshwun, ut nashauwe neeswe wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ut.
28.5 Kah piukque chippag Ephath pasquag nꝏ̄khik, wutche meetsue sephausuonk, kenugkenausu yaue chippag hin sukquethausue pumme.
28.6 Nag wutteae chihohtae sephausuonk ayimun ut wadchuut Sinai, wutche weetemungquok, nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut.
28.7 Kah wuttattamóe sephausuonk ne wadchiik, | yaue chippag Hin wutch pasuk lamb, ut wunnetupanatamwe ayeuonganit, pish kussokenumwohtoh wuttattamoe sephausuonk manuhkag wine en Jehovah ut.
28.8 Kah onkatuk lambe pish kukquaquoshwun ut nashaue neeswe wunnongkꝏ̄ꝏ̄k, neane mohtompanáe meetsue sephausuonk, kah neane wuttattamóe sephausuonk pish kutayim, nꝏ̄tae magꝏ̄onk weetemungquok en Jehovahut.
28.9 Sabbath dayeu, neesuog nomposhumwe nekodtumꝏ̄k lambsog pannuppeyeuutcheg, kah neesit piukque chìppag pasquag nꝏ̄khik, wutche meetsue sephausuonk, kenugkenausu pummeit, kah wuttattamôe sephausuonk.
28.10 Ne Sabbathâe chikohtae sephausuonk nish noh Sabbath, chabok nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, kah wuttattamóe sephamauaonk.
28.11 Kah waj kutchisfinnéhettit kenepauzsómꝏ̄óog, pish kummagumwꝏ̄ chikohtae sephamauaonk Jehovah: neesuog oxinog wuskoshimwussog wutch herdut, kah pasuk ram, nesausuk tahsuog nékodtumꝏ̄k lambsog pannuppeyeuutcheg.
28.12 Kah nashwut piogque chippag pasquag nꝏ̄khik, wutche metsue sephausuonk, kenugkenausu pumme, wutch pasuk ox, kah neesit piukque chippag pasquag nꝏ̄khik wutche meetsue magꝏ̄onk kenugkenausu pummee, wutche pasuk ram.
28.13 Kah chadchabe piogque chippag pasquag nꝏ̄khik, wutche meetsue sephausuonk kenugkenausu pummeit, wutche pasuk lamb. wutche chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, weetemungquok, nꝏ̄tae sep(h)ausuonk en Jehovahut.
28.14 Kah ꝏ̄tattamꝏ̄e magꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash, paushe hin wine wutche pasuk ox, kah nashwe chippág hin wutche pasuk ram, kah yaue chippag hin wutche lamb: yeu nepauzsae chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, ut nish noh nepauz, pannuppe kodtumwae nepauzsuog
28.15 Kah pasuk nompóshimwe goats wutche matcheseongane sephausuonk en Jehovahut, pish quaquoshwunumun chaubok nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, kah wuttattamwe sephausuonk.
28.16 Kah ut negonne nepauzsaut, ut nabo weyóqunnahhamunat nepauz, pish paumukóadtuonk en Jehovahut.
28.17 Kah ut napuh napanna wutteashikqunhamunat yeuoh nepauz, pish mishadtuppꝏ̄onk nesausuk tah[]hikquinne, matta seanu(n)ꝏ̄g petukqunneg pish mèechin.
28.18 Negonne kesukok pish wunneetupanatamwe miyayéonk, matta pish toh kutussumwꝏ̄.
28.19 Qut pish ku(mm)águ(m)wꝏ̄ ch°kohtae magꝏ̄onk, chikohtae magꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut, neesuog oxinog, wu[]ko[]himwog wutch | herdut, kah pasuk ram, kah nésausuk tahsuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog pannuppeyeuutcheg, neg pish wutch kuhhogkaôut.
28.20 Kah meetsue wussephausuonganꝏ̄, pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummeit, nashwé piogque chippag pish kukquaquoshwunumumwꝏ̄, wutche pasuk ox, kah neesit piogque chippag wutche ram
28.21 Chadchabe papiogque chippagish pish kukquaquoshwehtam wutch nishnoh pasuk lambe, pannuppe nesausuk tahsuog lambsog.
28.22 Kah pasuk nompóshimwe goat wutche matcheseongane sephausuonk, ayimunat wunnáuwadtuonk wutche kenaau.
28.23 Chaubohkish mohtompanáe chikohtâe sephausuongash, ne wutch nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, yeush pish kukquaquoshwunnumunaoash.
28.24 Yeu neane kukquaquoshwehtamumwꝏ̄ nish noh kesukod, nesausuk tahshikquinne, petukqunnungane nꝏ̄tae sephausuonk, weetemunquok en Jehovahut pish quaquoshwunumun, chabuk nagwutteae sephamauáonk. & ꝏ̄tattamóe sephamaonk
28.25 Kah nesausuk tahshikquinogkok, pish kutayimumwꝏ̄ wunnetupanatmwe miyayéonk, matta pish toh kutussúmwꝏ̄.
28.26 Kah kákeneúmune kesukodtut, sephauseog wuske meetsue sephausuonk en Jehovahut nahohtóeu kꝏ̄weeksumꝏ̄ash, pish kutayimwꝏ̄ wunneetupanatamwe miyaéonk, matta pish toh kutussúmwꝏ̄.
28.27 Kah pish kummagumwꝏ̄ chikohtáe magꝏ̄onk wutche weetemungquok en J[e]hovahut neesuog oxenog wuskoshimwussog wutch herdut, pasuk ram, nesausuk tahsuog nomposhimwe ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog
28.28 Kah ummeetsue sephausuonganꝏ̄ pasquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausu pummee, nashwe piukque chippag wutch pasuk ox, neese piogque chippag wutche pasuk ram.
28.29 Chadchaube pìogque chippagish wutche [p]asuk lamb, pannuppe nesausuk tahsuog lambsog.
28.30 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch goatsut, ayimunát wunnauwadtuonk wutche kenaau.
28.31 Neg pish kukquaquashwunóog, chaubok nagwutteáe sephausuonk, kah meetsue wussephamauáonk, pannuppyeuꝏ̄og pish en kuhhogkaóog, kah wuttattamóe sephausuonkash.
29.1 KAH ut nesausu(k) adtahsꝏ̄ut nepauz negonne kesukok ne nepauz, pish kꝏ̄(n)eetupanatamwe miaeé(m)ꝏ̄, matta pish kut(u)seumwꝏ̄ wut(c)hiyeue an(a)kaus(uon)k, ne pi[]h monopuhpequáe kesukod wutche kenaau.
29.2 Kah pish kukquaquoshwunnúmumwꝏ̄ chikohtáe sephausuonk, weetemungquok wutch Jehovah, pasuk oxenémes, wushko[]hi(m)[] wutch herdut, pasuk ram, nes(a)usuk tah[]huog nomposhimwe ne kodtumꝏ̄k pannuppeyeuutcheg lambsog.
29.3 Kah ne wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk, pashquag nꝏ̄khik kenugkenausik pummeit, nishwudt piukque chippag wutch pasuk ox, neese piogque chippag wutche ram
29.4 Kah pasuk piogque chippag wutch (p)asuk lamb, papashpe nesausuk tahshe l(a)mbsog.
29.5 Kah pasuk nom(p)oshimwe goat, wut[]h goatsut wutche matcheseongane seph[]us(u)onk, ayimunat wunnauwadtuonk wutche kenaau.
29.6 Châbok nepauzáe chikohtae sephausuonk, kah noh wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk, kah nagwutteae chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, kah ne woh wadchiikish metsue sephausuonk kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash, neaunág, weetemungquok, nꝏ̄tae sephamauaonk Jehovah.
29.7 Knh piukukquinhog yeuoh nesausuk adtahsuut nepâuz, pish kꝏ̄netupanatamwe miayemꝏ̄, kah pish kutûhquanumweheomwꝏ̄ kukketeahogkonꝏ̄ôog, matta pish toh kutussúmwꝏ̄.
29.8 Kah pish kummagumwꝏ̄ chikohtae sephausuonk en Jehovahut wutch weetemungquok, pasuk ox wushkoshim wutch herdut, pasuk ram, nesausuk tahsuog nekodtumꝏ̄k nomposhimwe lambsog, nag pish pannuppeyeuꝏ̄og wutche kenaau.
29.9 Kah ne noh wadchiik meetsue magꝏ̄onk, pish pashquag kenugenausik pumme, nashwe piogque chippag wutch pasuk ox, kah neese piogque chippag wutche psauk ram.
29.10 Chadchabe pìukque chippag wutche pasuk lamb, papashpe nesausuk tahsuog lambsog,
29.11 Pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch kenugke goatsut, wutche matcheseongane magꝏ̄onk, chabokish wunnauwadhuwáe matcheseáe sepháusuongash, kah nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuongash, kah nish noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash, kah wuttattámôe sephausuongash.
29.12 Kah nabo napanna tahshikquinuhhog, nesausuk adtahsꝏ̄it nepauz, pish kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe mowemꝏ̄ matta pish wutchayeue anakausuonk kutusseumwꝏ̄, kah pish mishadtupóe kummishadtupumwꝏ̄ en Jehovahut nesausuk tahshikquinnu.
29.13 Kah pish kummagumwꝏ̄ chikohtáe magꝏ̄onk, nꝏ̄táe sephausuonk weetemungquok en Jehovahut, nabo nishuog oxenog, wushkoshimwog ut herdut, neesuog ramsog, nabo yauog ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog, neg pish pannuppeyeuꝏ̄og.
29.14 Kah ni[]h noh wadchiikish meetsue | se(p)hausuongash pi[]h pashquag nꝏ̄khik kônugkenausik pumme, nishwe piogque chippag wutch pasuk ox, papashpe nabo nashꝏ̄itcheg oxenog; neese piogque chippag wutch pasuk ram, naneeswe ramsog.
29.15 Kah chad[]h(a)be piogque chippagish wutch pasuk lamb, papashpe nabo yauꝏ̄utcheg lambsog.
29.16 Kah pasuk nompishimwe goat wutch kenugke goatsut, wutch matcheseáe sephausuonk, chaubok nagwutteáe chikohtáe sephausuonk, ne noh wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk kah wuttattamóe sephausuonk.
29.17 K(a)h ut nahohtóe kesukodtut, nabo neesuog oxenog, wuskkoshimwog wutch herdut, neesuog ramsog, nabo yauog nekodtumꝏ̄k nompo[]himwe lambsog, pannuppeycuutcheg.
29.18 Kah nish noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash, wutche oxenog, kah wutche ramsog kah wutche lambsog, ne adtahséhettit, neanusséhettit.
29.19 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goats wutch kenugke goatsog, wutch match[]seae sephausuonk, ch[]bok nagwutteáe sephausuonk, kah nish noh wadchiikish meetsue magꝏ̄ongash, kah wuttattamôe sephausuongash,
29.20 Kah nishikquinogkodtut, nabo nequttuꝏ̄og oxenog, neesuog ramsog, nabo yauꝏ̄og ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog, pannuppeyeuutcheg.
29.21 Kah nish noh wadchiikish meetsue magꝏ̄ongash kah wuttattamóe mgaꝏ̄ongash, wutche oxenog, wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog, ne adtahsꝏ̄hettit, ne anussehettit.
29.22 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch matcheseáe sephausuonk, châbok nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, nah ne noh wadchiik meetsue magꝏ̄onk kah wuttattamôe magꝏ̄onk.
29.23 Kah ut yauquinogkodtut, piogqussuog oxenog neesuog ramsog, nabo yauꝏ̄og ne kodtumꝏ̄k nomposhimwe lambsog, pannuppeyeuutcheg.
29.24 Nish noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash, wutch[] oxenog, wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog ne adtahsehettit neanussehettit.
29.25 Kah pásuk nomposhimwe goat wutch matcheseáe sephausuonk, chabok nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, ne noh wadchiåk meetsue sephausuonk kah wuttattamóe sephausuonk.
29.26 Kah ut napanna tahshikquinogkodtut, pasukꝏ̄gun tahsuog oxenog, neesuog ramsog, kah nabo yauꝏ̄og ne kodtumꝏ̄k lambsog, pannuppeyuutcheg.
29.27 Kah nìsh noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash, kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash, | wutche oxenog, kah wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog, ne adtahsehettit, ne anussehettit.
29.28 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch matcheseáe sephausuonk, chabok nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk kah ne noh wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk wuttattamóe magꝏ̄onk.
29.29 Kah ut nequtta tahshikquinogkodtut, shwosuk tahsuog oxenog, neesuog ramsog nabo yauꝏ̄og ne kodtumꝏ̄k nomposhimwe lambsog, pannuppeyeuutcheg,
29.30 Kah nish noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash, kah wuttattamôe sephausuongash wutche oxenog, wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog, ne adtahsehettit ne anus(se)hettit
29.31 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutche matcheseae sephausuonk chabok nagwutteae chiko(h)tae sephausuonk, ne noh wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk, kah wuttattamóe sephausuonk.
