29.32 Kah ut nesausuk tahshikquinogok nesausuk tahsuog oxenog, nesuog rams[]g, nabo yauꝏ̄og ne kodtumꝏ̄k nomposhimwe lambsog, pannuppeyeuutcheg.
29.33 Kah nish noh wadchiikish metsue sephausuongash kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash, wutche oxen(o)g, wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog, neadtahsehettit, neanussehettit.
29.34 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch matcheseae sephausuonk, ch(a)b[]k nagwutteae chikohtae sephausuonk, kah ne noh wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk, kah wuttattamôe sephausuonk
29.35 Ut nishwosuk tahshikquinogkodtut pish kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe mꝏ̄emꝏ̄, matta pish kutusseumwꝏ̄ wutchiyeueu anakausuonk.
29.36 Kah pish kummagumwꝏ̄ chikohtae magꝏ̄onk, nꝏ̄tae sephausuonk weetemungquok en Jehovahut, pasuk ox. pasuk ram, nesausuk tahsuog ne kodtumꝏ̄k nomposhimwe lambsog, pannuppeyeuutcheg.
29.37 Nish noh wadchiikish meetsue sephausuongash, kah wuttattamóe sephausuongash: wutche oxenog, wutche ramsog, kah wutche lambsog ne adtahsehettit, ne anussehettit.
29.38 Kah pasuk nomposhimwe goat wutch matcheseae sephausuonk chaubok nagwutteae chikohtáe sephausuonk, kah ne wadchiik meetsue sephausuonk, kah wuttattamóe sephausuonk.
29.39 Yeush pish kittinheonaoash Jehovah, ut kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe mishádtuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄óut, chabokish kukquoshauaonganꝏ̄oash kah kuttenantamwe sephausuongash wutch kutchikohtae sephausuongash, kah wutch kummeetsue sephausuonganꝏ̄oash & wutch kꝏ̄tattamóe sephausuonganꝏ̄ash kah wutch kꝏ̄nohteáe sephausuongánꝏ̄oásh.
29.40 Kah Moses kcnꝏ̄nau wunnaumonuh Israel, neaunag wame Jchovah ananꝏ̄nomp Mosesoh,
30.1 KAh Moses kenꝏ̄nau wabuhkꝏ̄unutcheh ut chippanꝏ̄onganit, papaume wunnaumonuh Israel, nꝏ̄wau, Yeu Jehovah anannꝏ̄teamit.
30.2 Wosketomp quoshauwae quoshomont Jehovah, asuh chadchekeyeuwae chadchekeyeuadt, keneepinont ukketeahogkounuh: matta pish pohquenumꝏ̄ ukkuttꝏ̄onk, pish usseu neane wame sohwhemꝏ̄uk wutch wuttꝏ̄nut,
30.3 Kah mittamwossis quoshauwae quoshomont Jehovah, kah keneepinont wuhhogkuh nashpe keneepsuonk, ut weekit ꝏ̄shoh, ut wunnunksquainneat.
30.4 Kah ꝏ̄shoh nꝏ̄tamunit ukquoshauwaonk kah ukkeneepsuonk, ne nashpe keneepenont ukketeahogkôunoh, kah ꝏ̄shoh mat kenꝏ̄nukꝏ̄k: neit wame ukquoshómuwaongash pish menuhkohtaash, kah nishnoh kenepsuonk uttoh adt keneepinont ukketeahogkôunoh, pish menuhkohtaash.
30.5 Qút ꝏ̄shoh mat tapeneamuneg ne kesukok nꝏ̄tog, matta pasuk ukquoshauaongash, asuh ukkeneepissuongash, nish nashpe keneepinoncheh ukketeahogkôunoh, pish memenuhkohtanꝏ̄ash: kah Jehovah pish ummonaneteae ahquontamauau, newutche ꝏ̄shoh matta wuttapeneamunkꝏ̄un.
30.6 Kah ꝏ̄wessukiis, kah quoshoadt asuh ketꝏ̄kontog nashpe wussissetꝏ̄nash, uttoh adt keneepenomp ukketeahgkôunoh.
30.7 Kah wessukeh nꝏ̄tunkqut, kah mat kenꝏ̄nunk ne kesukok nꝏ̄tog, neit ukquoshauaongash pish menuhkohtaash, kah ukkeneepsuongash nish nashpe kenepinoncheh ukketeahogkôunoh pish menuhkohtaash.
30.8 Qut wessukeh ne kesukok nꝏ̄tunkqut, mattá tapeneamauunk, neit pish monteagqunnehteaou ukquoshauaonk ne appehtunkqut, kah wussissittꝏ̄ne ukkuttꝏ̄wongash nish nashpe kenepinoncheh ukketeahogkôunuh, kah Jehovah pish ummonaneteae ahquontamauoh.
30.9 Qut nishnoh ukquoshauwoank sekousq, kah noh pagkenit, uttoh adt keneepenont ukketeahogkôuneh, pish ummenuhkappehtunkqun.
30.10 Kah quosháuadt ut wessukeh wekit, kah keneepenont ukketeahogkôunoh nashpe chadchekeyeuwaonk.
30.11 Kah wessukeh nꝏ̄tunkqut, kah mat kenꝏ̄nukꝏ̄k, kah matta mat tapeneamâuunk: neit wame ukquoshauwaongash pish menuhkohtaash, kah nishnoh keneepissuonk ne nashpe keneepinon(t) ukketeahogkôunoh, pish menuhkohtaau.
30.12 Qut wessukeh papáne monteagqunnehte[]uunneg, ne kesukok nꝏ̄tog, uttoh áne sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk wutch wussissitꝏ̄nit, papaume ukquoshauaongash, asuh papaume ukketeahogkôune keneepsuonk, matta pish menuhkohtanꝏ̄, wessukeh monteagwunnehteoꝏ̄g, kah Jehovah pish ummonaneteae ahquontamauoh.
30.13 Nishnoh quoshaumuwaonk kah nishnoh keneepsue chadcheyeuwaonk onkapunnanónat ukketeahogkôunoh, wessukeh woh ummenuhkehteauunin, kah wessukeh woh wutwutteagwunnehteoꝏ̄un.
30.14 Qut wessukeh mꝏ̄hche matta kenꝏ̄nukꝏ̄gk asekesukokish: neit menuhketeau wame ukquoshaumuwaongash, kah wame ukkenepsuongash nish apehtunkqutchish, nish ummenuhkehteauunash, newutche matta ukkenꝏ̄nuh ne kesukok nꝏ̄tauont.
30.15 Qut noh pannuppe monteagwunnehteoꝏ̄g, mahche nish nꝏ̄tog: neit noh pish tahshinum ummatcheseonk.
30.16 Yeush kuhkꝏ̄waongash, nish Jehovah anannꝏ̄noncheh Mosesoh, nashaue wosketomp kah ummittamwussoh, nashaue wutꝏ̄shimau, kah wuttaunoh nunksquainit, ut ꝏ̄shoh weekit.
31.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
31.2 Anꝏ̄tau Midianitsog wutanꝏ̄taongnꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel, ne mahche nnag neit pish kummukkinnem en kummissinninnutu,
31.3 Kah Moses kenꝏ̄nau missinninnuh nꝏ̄wau, Kenauwamunꝏ̄k nawhutch wosketompaog wutch kenugke kenaau, en ayeuwuttinneat, kah ayeuwuhkontamwehettich Midian, kah ussek wutannꝏ̄tauonk Jehovah ut Midian.
31.4 Nequt muttannunk, nequt muttannunk wutch wame wutchippanꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wóut Israel, pish kummoncheahéoog en ayeuwuttinneat.
31.5 Nene wuttinne moeneau wutch ummuttannonganogkussunneaôut Israel, nequt muttannong wutch pasuk chippanꝏ̄ong, nabo neese muttannunganogkussuog kenauwameog wutche ayeuwuttuonk
31.6 Kah Moses nah ummoncheaheuh nequt muttannunk wutch pasuk chippanꝏ̄onk, en ayeuwuttinneat: nag kah Phineas wunnaumonuh Eleazar sephausuaen, en ayeuwuttinneat, kah wunneetupanatamwe auwohteaongash, kah quoshweongane monopuhpequonash wunnutcheganit.
31.7 Kah ayeuwuttamwog Midian, nean[u]nnꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh, kah nushaog nish noh nompaussoh.
31.8 Kah nushaog Midiane ketahfꝏ̄tamwoh, chahefitcheg onkatogig neg noshomugeg, Evi, kah Rekem, kah Zur, kah Hur, kah Reba, napanna tahsuog Midiane tahsꝏ̄tamwog, kah Balaam wonk wunnaumonuh Beor wunnushôuh nashpe togkodteg.
31.9 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel missinohteaog Midiane mittamwussissoh kah peissesumôuh, kah nemunnumwog sequttahhamwe neetasu, kah wame uffloksumꝏ̄óoh, kah wame máumachiyeuwóash.
31.10 Kah chikohsumwog wame keitꝏ̄tanash ut ne wadohkehettit, kah wonkonꝏ̄sunash nashpe nꝏ̄tau.
31.11 Kah neemunnumwog wáme sequttahhamꝏ̄ongash, kah wame wosketompae kah neetasue sequttahhamꝏ̄onk.
31.12 Kah pasꝏ̄áog missinoh, kah sequttahhamꝏ̄onk, kah tohqunnumꝏ̄onk en Mosesut, kah en Eleazarut sephausuen, kah en ummukkinneaonganꝏ̄óut wunnaumonuh Israel, en tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit, en Moabe mukoshquttaut, nish kishke Jordan kishke Jericho.
31.13 Kah Moscs kah Eleaz(a)r sephausuaen, kah wame mukkinneonganit sontimóog, sohhamwog wunnogskauónaout ut poquodchit tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit.
31.14 Kah Moses musquanumau ayeuhteáe aninnohsuéneuh, muttannongane mummugquompuh, & nequt pasukꝏ̄e mummugquompuh, neg wagig ayeuwuttinneat.
31.15 Kah Moses nah wuttinuh, kukketeahomwꝏ̄ wame mittamwussissog?
31.16 Kusseh, yeug matcheseâh(e)áog wunnaumonuh Israel, nashpe ukkenꝏ̄sꝏ̄waonk Balaam, ayeuhkonittue Jehovah, ut wuttinniyeuoganit Peor, kah na mo wesau[]haonk kenugke ummukkinneonganit Jehovah.
31.17 Newutche yeuyeu nushok nish noh nompaas, kenugke peissesit, kah nushok nish noh mittumwossis noh wahheont wosketompuh, neesissinunat wosketomp.
31.18 Qut wame mukkiésog kenugke muttamwossisut, neg matta wahteauꝏ̄gig neesinnꝏ̄onk wosketomp, neg pomantamwahheuk.
31.19 Kah kenaau tuppuksinꝏ̄k poquadchit tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit, nesausuk tahshikquinne, howan nashont keteahogkóunoh, kah howan masunont nashomukeh, pahkheuk kuhhogkaóog, kah kummissinnomꝏ̄ôog, nishikquinne, kah nesausuk tahshikquinne.
31.20 Kah pahketeaꝏ̄k nish noh hogkꝏ̄onk, kah nish noh hohkꝏ̄nie auwohteaonk, kah nish noh goatse weshagkane anakausuonk, kah nish noh mehtugque auwohteaonk.
31.21 Kah Eleazar sephausuen unnau kenauwameéneuh, neh ayonitcheh ayeuwuttinneat, yeu naumatue kuhkꝏ̄waonk, ne anannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh.
31.22 Webe gold, kah silver, wompuhshog, | mꝏ̄ôhshog, mohmuttahtag, kah lead.
31.23 Nish noh teag pannupwushómꝏ̄ug nꝏ̄t(a)ut, pish kuppannupwusháhtineau nꝏ̄taut, kah pish pohki, qut pish pahketeausu nashpe chuppannumóe nippe, kah nish noh teag matta pannupwus(ho)munꝏ̄g nꝏ̄taut, pish kuppanupwus(h)átine(a)u nippeit.
31.24 Kah pish k(u)gku(t)s(h)ittemwꝏ̄ kuthogkꝏ̄unꝏ̄oash ut neesausuk tahshikquinogkodtut, kah pish kuppahkesi(m)wꝏ̄, kah ne mahche nnag pish kuppetutteamwꝏ̄ tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit.
31.25 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau,
31.26 Ogkemꝏ̄k tohqunogig neg masu(n)omukuppanneg, missinninnu(o)g, kah puppinashimwog, ken kah Eleazar sephausuaen, kah kehch(e)u wutꝏ̄shinneunk ut mukkinneonganit.
31.27 Kah neese chippinnꝏ̄k neg tohqunomugeg, nashaue nag ayeuwuhteacheg, neg sohhogig ayeuuhkonat, kah nashaue wame mukkinneonk.
31.28 Kah chippinnumꝏ̄k ompeteaonk en Jehovah ut, wutch ayeuuhteaenuut, neg sohhogig ayeuuhkonat; pasuk keteahogkou wutch napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og, wutch missinninnuog, kah wutch kꝏ̄washinog kah wutch assesog, kah wutch sheepsog
31.29 Nemunnumok wutch w[]tchippiyeumꝏ̄out, kah aninnumau Eleazar sephausuaen wutche tahshinnumꝏ̄e magꝏ̄onk en Jehovah ut.
31.30 Kah wutch wutchippiyeumꝏ̄out Israel wunnaumonat, pish kenemun [r]equt chippissuog wutch napanna tahchinchagkodtut, wutch missinninnuog, wutch kꝏ̄washinog, wutch assesog, kah wutch floksut, wame nish noh wuttinussinneau puppinashimwog, kah neh aninnumau Levitsog, neg nanawehteungig tabernakle ummeechumehkausuwaonk Jehovah.
31.31 Kah Moses kah Eleazar sephausuaen wutusseneau nean annꝏ̄nont Jehoveh Mosesoh.
31.32 Kah sequetahamꝏ̄ongash, nish asqshúnkish tohqunnumukish, nish ayeuteaenuog tohqunnumohettiche, mo nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄e muttannunkanogkussuog & nesausuk tahshinchage muttannunganog kussuog, kah napanna tahshe muttannunganog kussuog sheepsog.
31.33 Kah nesausuk tahshinchage kah neese muttannonganogkussuog kꝏ̄wishinog.
31.34 Kah nequtta tahskinchage kah nequt muttannonganogkussuog assesog.
31.35 Kah nishwinchage kah neese muttannonganogkussuog missinninnuog neg wame mittamwussissog matta wahheunkig wosketompuh ut neesinat.
31.36 Kah na pohshe wutchippiyeumꝏ̄ neg sohhogig ayeuuhkonat mó unnogkemóog | nishwe pasukꝏ̄e muttannonk kah nishwinshag kah nesausuk tahshe muttannonk sheep.
31.37 Kah Jehovah shepse omwunnaonk, nequtta tahshe pasukꝏ̄ kah nesausuk tahshin[c]hag kah napanna.
31.38 Kah kowashineog nishwinchag kah nequtta tahshe muttannonganogkussuog, nag noh wutch Jehovah ompwunnaonk nesausuk tahshinchag kah nees.
31.39 Kah assesog shwinchage muttannonganogkussuog kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og neg noh wutch Jehovah ompwunnaonk nequtta tahshinchag kah pasuk.
31.40 Kah missinninnuog nabo nequtta tahshe muttannunk, neg noh wutch Jehovah ompwunnaonk, nishwinchagkussuog missinninnuog kah neesuog.
31.41 Kah Moses aninnumauau ompwuhteaonk tahshinumwe magꝏ̄onk Jehovah, en Eleazerut sephausuenuut, neanannꝏ̄nont Jehovah Moses.
31.42 Kah wutchippiyeumꝏ̄ont wunnaumonuh I[]rael, ne Moses chachabenompoh wutch ayeuuhteaenuut.
31.43 Onk wutchippiyeum mukkinneonk, mo nishwudt pasukꝏ̄e muttannong kah nishwinchage muttannonk & nesausuk tahshe muttannonk kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og sheepsog.
31.44 Kah shwinchag kah nequtta tahshe muttannunkanog kussuog kꝏ̄washinog.
31.45 Kah shwinchage muttannonganog kussuog assesog, kah napanna tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
31.46 Kah nabo nequtta tahshe muttannonganog kussuog missinninnuog.
31.47 Wutch chippiyeumꝏ̄out wunnaumouh Israel, Moses neemunau nequtchippissuoh napanna tahshinchag kussuog, missinninn(e)uh kah puppinashim, kah nah wuttinnumauonuh Levitsoh, neg nanawehteunkig Tabernakle ummeechumuhkausuwaonk Jehovah, ne annꝏ̄nont Jehovah Mosesoh,
31.48 Kah aninnohsuénuog neg nanawunoncheg muttannunganog kussu(o)h ut ayeuwuttinneat, muttannonganogkussue mummugquompaog, nequt pasukꝏ̄e mugquompaog pasꝏ̄sukauwaog Mosesoh.
31.49 Kah unnaog Mosesoh, kuttinneumog mahche nutogkemounnonog ayeuhteacheg neg agwe ut nunnutcheganunonut, kah wanne quenauwussuh pasuk.
31.50 Newaj paudtauog sephamauaonk Jehovah nish noh wuttinne tohqunnumun, golde nompakꝏ̄unash sasasugkinitteumꝏ̄ugish kah kehtìppetenapéash, pehtehhannitchabbeash, & sagkussuohhꝏ̄unash, & Tabletsash ayimunat wunnauwadtuonk wutche keteahogkónunnonog ut anaquabit Jehovah,
31.51 Kah Moses kah Eleazar sephausuen wunnemunnumauouh gold, wame wussukwhosue nompakouanash.
31.52 Kah wame sephausue gold, nish sephamauahetticheh Jehovah nashpe muttanongane mugquompaog, kah nequt pasukꝏ̄e mugquompaog: mo nabo nequtta pasukꝏ̄e muttannonganogkodtash shekelsash, kah nesausuk tahshe pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, kah napanna tahshinchagkod(t)ash,
31.53 Newutche áyeuhteaog, tohqunnumhetticheh nish noh pasuk wutche wuhhogkuh.
31.54 Kah Mo[s]es kah Eleazar sephusuaen nemunnumauwaog ukgoldumꝏ̄ muttannongane mugquompaog kah nequt pasukꝏ̄e mugquompuh, kah nag uppaudtauunau, en mukkinneae Tabernakleut wutche mehquontamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel ut anaquabit Je[n]ovah.
32.1 NAno wunnaumonuh Ruben, kah wunnaumonuh Gad mꝏ̄chekodchanaog neetassu, ka(h) namohettit ohke Jazar, kah ohke Gilead, kah kusseh, ne ayeuonk tapeneunkquot wutche neetahsuog.
32.2 Wunneechanuh Gad, kah wunneechanuh Ruben, peyaog kah kenꝏ̄naog Moses kah Eleazar sephausuaen, kah mukkieneae sontimóog, nꝏ̄waog.
32.3 Ataroth kah Dibon, kah Jazer, kah Nimrah, kah Heshbon kah Elèaleh kah Sheban kah Nebo kah Beon,
32.4 Wutohtimoin, ne Jehovah togkodtog anaquohtag Israelle muhk[i]nneonk, yeu ohke {tapeneunkquot} wutche netasuog, kah kittinneumog nꝏ̄neetasseumꝏ̄min.
32.5 Newutche nꝏ̄waog namehteauog kitteamonteanittuonk ut anaquabean, yeu ohke aninnumauunach kittinneumog wutch ahtóonk, kah ahque qushkodteasinan Jordan.
32.6 Kah Moses unnau wunnaumonuh Gad kah wunnaumonuh Ruben, sun pish kemattꝏ̄wóog ayeuhteaog, kah kenaau sun yeu pish kutapineau.
32.7 Kah tohwutch pohqenumóg wuttahhꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Israel, wutch qushkogkonat en ohkit ne Jehovah anumauont?
32.8 Yeu wutuffeneauop kꝏ̄shꝏ̄óg, annꝏ̄nog wutch Kadesh Barnea, kuhkinneamunat ohke.
32.9 Newutche kohkukquehettit en Eshkolle ꝏ̄nôuhkôiyeuut, kah naumhettit ohke, pokshadtauopanneg wuttahhꝏ̄oash wunnaumonuh Israel, matta woh wuttonaóut ohke ne Jehovah anumauont.
32.10 Kah ummusquanittamꝏ̄onk Jehovah nashqunop neit wadchit, kah chadchekeyeuau nꝏ̄wau.
32.11 Wunnamuhkut, wanne howáe wosketomp noh sohhogkup wutch Egypt, wutch neesneechage kodtumwohkomunat & paame, pish naumo ohke ne chadchekeimogkup | Abraham, kah Isaak, kah Jakob, newutche matta mamusse nutasukunkꝏ̄og.
32.12 Webe Kaleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh uk-Kenazit, kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun, newutche mamusse asuhkauópanneg Jehovah,
32.13 Kah ummusquanittamꝏ̄onk Jehovah nashqunau ayeuuhkone Israel, kah uppomushaheuh ut touohkomuk yauunchage kodtumwâe nô pajeh wame pometuonk né matchesemꝏ̄uk ut anaquabit Jehovah nukkomwémꝏ̄uk.
32.14 Kah kusse kenaau kenompekompaehtôuomwꝏ̄ kꝏ̄shuóg, kꝏ̄chetimwꝏ̄ matcheseaénuut, nano misheteauunat uhqueneunkque ummusquanittamꝏ̄onk Jehovah ayeuuhkone Israel.
32.15 Newutche nukkonóg wutch asuhkauónat, noh pish wonk wunnukonuh ut touohkomuk. kah kenaau pish wutch paguanoog wame yeug missinninnuog.
32.16 Kah nag uppasꝏ̄sukauóuh kah nꝏ̄waog, Nutayimumun yeu shepse chippinneutunkash wutche nunnetasseumunónog, kah otanash wutche nummukkiésumunónog,
32.17 Qut nenawun pish nukkenauwamee negonuhkauomun wunnaumonuh Israel, nó pajeh pasꝏ̄ogkut wutayeuonganꝏ̄óut. kah nummukkiesumunónog pish ayeuog qussukquanteutausue ꝏ̄tanahtu, newtche wadohkitcheg ne ohkeit.
32.18 Matta nukqushkꝏ̄mun en nekinónut, nô pajeh wunnaumonuh Israel ohtunk nishnoh pasuk wutohtoonk.
32.19 Newutche matta nꝏ̄weeche ohtomóunónog ongkoue Jordan, asuh ongkoue: newutche nutahtaonganun wutush pogkishin Jordan wutchepwoayeu.
32.20 Kah Moses nah wuttinuh, Yeu usseóg, kenauwameáe ayeuhteae moncheóg anaquabit Jehovah.
32.21 Kah tohneit kenaau wame kenauwamee qushkodteaóg en Jordan, ut anaquabit Jehovah nó pajeh wussohhꝏ̄kauónat wame ummatwomoh wutch anaquabit.
32.22 Kah ohke sohkomunat anaquabit Jehovah: neit ompetak pish kukqushkemwꝏ̄, kah matta pish kꝏ̄matchesonkaneumwꝏ̄ ut anaquabit Jehovah, ut anaquabhettit Israel, kah yeu ohke pish kꝏ̄tohtoonganinneau ut anaquabit Jehovah.
32.23 Qut ne matta usseôg, kusseh, kummatcheneheomwꝏ̄ Jehovah, kah pahke wahteauꝏ̄k kummatches(e)onganꝏ̄ kummshikonkumwꝏ̄.
32.24 Ayimꝏ̄k keitotanash wutch kummukkiésumꝏ̄ôog, kah chippinneutunkash wutch kutsheepsumog, kuh ussek neane sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk wutch kuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄óut.
32.25 Kah wunnaumonuh Gad, kah wunnaumonuh Reuben kenꝏ̄naog Mosesoh, nꝏ̄waog, Kittinneumog wutussenau n anam | [n]ꝏ̄teamwit nussontimómun.
32.26 Nummukkiyeumunónog, nummittamwussinnônog, nuffloksumunónog, kah wame nunnetasumunónog, na pish wutappineau Gileade otanahtu.
32.27 Qut kittinneumog pish nuppaumushaumun, nishnoh wosketomp kenauwamée wutch ayeuwuttuonk ayeuuhkonat ut anaquabit Jehovah, ne anꝏ̄wadt nussontimom(u)n.
32.28 Nemehkuh papaume nag, Moses annꝏ̄nau Eleazeroh sephausuénuh, & Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun, kah kehche wutꝏ̄shinneunk ut chippanꝏ̄onganꝏ̄óut ut wunnaumonat Israel
32.29 Kah Moses nah wuttinuh, Wunnaumonuh Gad, kah wunnaumonuh Reuben weeche paumushauómukquean Jordan, nish noh wosketomp kenauwamée wutche ayeuwuttuonk ánaquabit Jehovah kah ohke sohkomuk ut anaquabeôg, neit pish kittinnumauóog ohke Gilead wutche ohtôonk.
32.30 Kah matta kenauwamée weeche paumushómukꝏ̄an, neit pish ahtóog ohtoonk ut kenugke kenaau ohkeit Kanaan.
32.31 Kah wunnaumonuh Gad, kah wunnaumonuh Reuben, nampꝏ̄hamwog nꝏ̄waog, Neánont Jehovah kittinneumoh, ne nutussenan.
32.32 Pish nukkenauwamée pannupwushaumun anaquabit Jehovah en ohkit Kanaan onk woh nꝏ̄tihéinnean ohtóonk wutuhshin Jordan.
32.33 Kah Moses nah wuttinnumauoh, wunnaumonuh Gad kah wunnaumonuh Reuben, kah paushe wutchippanꝏ̄onk Manasses, wunnaumonuh Joseph, ukketassꝏ̄tamóonk Sihon, Amoritse ketassꝏ̄t, kah ukketassꝏ̄tamóonk Og Bashane kctassꝏ̄t, ohke kah nish otanash, kah sussippóiyeuash, otanash waéenu wutohtimoneat.
32.34 Kah wunnaumonuh Gad weekiteaog ut Dibon, kah Ataroth, kah Aroer.
32.35 Kah Atroth, Shophan, kah Jaazer kah Jogbehah.
32.36 Kah Bethnimrah, kah Bethharan, pummeneutausue kehtotanash: kah shepse chippinneutunkash.
32.37 Kah wunnaumonuh Reuban, weekitteaog ut Heshbon, kah Elealeh, kah Kirjathaim.
32.38 Kah Nebo, kah Baal-meon, (ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash ósꝏ̄wunnumuk) kah Shibmah, kah uppenowe hettamunâoash otanásh nish áyimohetticheh.
32.39 Kah wunnaumonuh Machir wunnaumonuh Manasss auog Gilead, kah wus[l]ohkomuneau, kah sohhꝏ̄hkauaog Amoritsoh neg wadohteupanneg.
32.40 Kah Moses aninnumauau Machiroh wunnaumonuh Manasseh Gilead kah na ꝏ̄tohkin.
32.41 Kah Jeir wunnaumonuh Manasseh, auog kah sohkomwog otanamesash, kah wuttissꝏ̄wetamunaoash Havoth-Jair.
32.42 Kah Nobah au sohkom Kenath, kah otanamesash, kah wutussowetamun Nobah, ne asꝏ̄wetamuk.
33.1 YEush uppomushaongash wunnaumonuh Israel, neg sohhogig wutch ohkit Egypt nashpe ukkenauwameonganꝏ̄óash, ut agwe wunnutcheganit Moses kah Aaron.
33.2 Kah Moses wussukhum wussohhamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash, neaunag uppomushaonganꝏ̄oash nashpe wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah: kah yeush uppomushaonganꝏ̄oash neaunag wussohhamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄oash.
33.3 Kah nag ꝏ̄mwog Rameses, ut negonne nepauzaut, ut nabo napanna wutteashikqunhomunat negonne nepauz: mohtompog mahche páumukáadtuonk, wunnaumonuh Israel sohhamwog nashpe qunuhqui menutcheg, ut anaquabhettit wame Egyptiansog.
33.4 (Newutche Egyptiansog posekinaog wame mohtomegitteomꝏ̄uh, neh Jehovah togkomoncheh ut kenugke nagoh: kah wonk ut ummanittꝏ̄mꝏ̄out Jehovah wutussen wussittumꝏ̄onk.)
33.5 Kah wunnaumonuh Israel ontsappinneau wutch Rameses, kah tuppuksinwog ut Sukkoth.
33.6 Kah ontsapuog wutch Sukkoth & tuppuksinwog ut Etham, ne kishke tôuohkomuk.
33.7 Kah ontsappuog wutch Etham, kah wonk nag qushkeog en Pihahiroth, ne anaquohtag Baal Zephon, kah tuppuksinwog anaquohtag Migdol.
33.8 Kah ontsapuog wutch anaquohtag Pihahiroth, kah pannupshag nóeu kehtahhannit, en touohkomukqut, kah nishikquinushaog ut Ethame touohkomukqut, kah tuppuksinwog ut Marah.
33.9 Kah ontsappuog wutch Marah, kah peyaog Elim: kah ut Elim na nabo neesinash tohkekomuash, kah nequtta takshinchag kah piogquodtash palme mehtugquash, kah na tuppuksiewog.
33.10 Kah ontsapuog wutch Elim, kah tuppuksinwog kishke msqui ketahhannit.
33.11 Kah ontsapuog wutch msqui kehtahtahhanit, kah tuppuksinwog ut Sine touohkomuk.
33.12 Kah moncheog wutch Sìne touohkomuk, kah tuppuksinwog ut Dophkah.
33.13 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Dophkah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Alush.
33.14 Káh ꝏ̄mwog wutch Alush, kah tuppuksinwog ut Rephidim, na matta nippeno wutche missinninnuog ꝏ̄tattamunaout.
33.15 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Rephidim, kah tuppuksinwog ut Sinai touohkomukqut.
33.16 Kah ontsapuog wutch touohkomuk Sinai, kah tuppukfinwog ut Kibroth-Hattaavah.
33.17 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Kibroth Hattaavah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Hazeroth.
33.18 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Hazeroth, kah tuppuksinwog ut Rithmah.
33.19 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Rithmah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Rimmon Parez.
33.20 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Rimmon-Parez, kah tuppuksinwog Libnah.
33.21 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Libnah, kah tuppusinwog ut Rissah.
33.22 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Rissah kah tuppuksinwog ut Kehelathah.
33.23 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Kehelathah kah tuppuksinwog ut wadchuut Shap[]er.
33.24 Kah ꝏ̄mwog wadchuut Shapher, kah tuppuksinwog ut Haradah.
33.25 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Haradah kah tuppuksinwog ut Mukheloth.
33.26 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Makheloth kah tuppuksinwog ut Tahath[.]
33.27 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Tahath, kah tuppukfinwog ut Tarah.
33.28 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Tarah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Mitchkah.
33.29 Kah moncheog wutch Mitchkah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Hashmonah,
33.30 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Hashmonath, kah tuppuksinwog ut Moseroth.
33.31 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Moseroth, kah tuppuksinwog ut Bene Jaakan,
33.32 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Bene-Jaakan, kah tuppuksinwng ut Hor-hagidgad.
33.33 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Hor hagidgad, kah tuppuksinwog ut Jotbathah.
33.34 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Jotbathah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Ebronah,
33.35 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Ebronah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Ezion Gaber,
33.36 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Ezion-Gaber. kah tuppuksinwog ut touo[n]komukqut Zin, ne Kadesh.
33.37 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Kadesh, kah tuppukfi(n)wog wadchuut Hor, kushke wutohki(t) Ed(o)m.
33.38 Kah Aaron sephausuaen ogquodch[]uau en wadchuut Hor, wutch neanꝏ̄wad Jehovah, kah na wuttit nuppun, yauunchage kodumwáe, mahche wunnaumonuh Israel sohogkuppanneg ohkit Egyp[], negonne kesukok n[]panna adt[]hsꝏ̄it nepauz
33.39 Kah Aaron mo nequt pasukꝏ̄e kodtumwohkom, kah neesneechag kah nish, ne napuk ut wadchuut Hor.
33.40 Kah ketassꝏ̄t Arad uk-Kananite (noh wadohteup sowaniyeu ut []hkit Kanaan) nꝏ̄tam peyaonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Israel.
33.41 Kah ꝏ̄mwog wadchuut Hor, kah tuppukfinwog ut Solmonah.
33.42 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Salmonah, kah tuppuksinwog ut Punon.
33.43 Kah ꝏ̄mwog P(u)non, kah tuppuksinwog ut Oboth.
33.44 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Oboth, kah tuppuksinwog ut Ijc-Abarim kishke Moab.
33.45 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Ijim, kah tuppuksinwog ut Dibon Gad.
33.46 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Dibon Gad, kah tuppuksinwog ut Almon-Diblathaim.
33.47 Kah ꝏ̄mwog Almon-Diblathaim, kah tuppuksinwog ut wadchuwehtu Abarim anaquohtag N(e)bo.
33.48 K[]h ꝏ̄mwog wadchuuttu Abarim, kah tuppuksinwog ut mukoshqutahtu Mo(a)b, kishke Jordan, kah Jericho.
33.49 Kah tuppuksinwog kishke Jordan wutch Beth-Jeshimoth nô pajeh Abel-Sittim ut mukoshqutahtu Moab.
33.50 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, ut mukoshqutahtu Moab kishke Jordan kah Jericho, nꝏ̄wau,
33.51 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, kah nag us, Qushkodteaog Jordan ut ohkit Kanaan.
33.52 Neit pish wame kutamaꝏ̄hkauomwꝏ̄ ne wadohkitcheg ohke, wutch anaqu(a)beog, kah pish wame kuppaguanomwꝏ̄ wuttinninneukontonkanꝏ̄uh, kah kuppaguanomwꝏ̄ wame sabahsumwe nunneukontunkanog, kah papaquanne kenꝏ̄kanumwꝏ̄ wame ukqunnunkquiyeumꝏ̄ash
33.53 Kah pish kutawushitteomwꝏ̄ ohke, kah na pish kꝏ̄tohkinneau. newutche ne kittinnumáuunneau ohke, kꝏ̄tohkinneáout.
33.54 Kah pish kutchadchaubenumwꝏ̄ ohke nashpe tanohtoadtuonk, wutche wutahtauunaout kenugke kutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄out, kah mon(a)hettit, pish kummꝏ̄cheke aninnumauóog, kah ogguhshettit pish kutogguhse ohtoonk aninnumauôog, nish noh wosketomp pish ayeu uttoh pagshik wuttittanohtoadtuonk, neaunag, wutchippanꝏ̄e wutteateashiyeûonganꝏ̄oash pish kutahtauuneau.
33.55 Qut matta sohhꝏ̄káuꝏ̄ôg neg noh wadohkitcheg wutch anaquabeog, neit pish n nih, yeug ashqshoncheg pish kummishkouutchinumwꝏ̄ ut kuskesukꝏ̄óut, kah pish ásinnekôu[s]sog ut kussissepoiyeumꝏ̄out, kah nag pish kummꝏ̄mꝏ̄skhikꝏ̄oog ut ohkit uttoh wadohkeóg.
33.56 Nano, pish n nih, kuttinhennumwꝏ̄, nean unnantamo(h)p nuttin(h)eonnaóut,
34.1 KAH Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Moseoh. nꝏ̄wau,
34.2 Annꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, kah nag us, peyôóg ohkit Kanaan (yeu ohke ne pagshik kuto(h)toonganꝏ̄óut, ohke Kanaan nashpe | sussippôe)
34.3 Neit kussowaniyeue sussippóiyeumꝏ̄ pis[h] wutch Zinne touohkomukqut, na pummekishke Edome sussippôiyeuash; kah pish kussowaniyeue su[]sippóiyeumꝏ̄, aongkoue sussippiyeuut salte kehtahhannit wutchepwoiyeu.
34.4 Kah kussussippóiyeumꝏ̄ pish quttukqshau wutch sowaniyeu, nó pajeh wadchuut Akrabbim, kah pamshau en Zin, kah na pannuppopôsuut pish wutch sowaniyeu, nó pajeh Kadesh Barnea, kah pish nano kutchituhshau weehque Hazar-add[]r, kah nano kutchituhshau wehque Azmon.
34.5 Kah sussippôe pish wáeyóhsheau wutch Azmon nó pajeh Egypte sepuut, kah na weehqshik pish keihtoh.
34.6 Kah kꝏ̄cheksúe sussippóiyeumꝏ̄óut pish kutahtômwꝏ̄ mishe keihtoh wutche kussussippóiyeumꝏ̄óut: yeu pish kꝏ̄cheksée sussippóiyeumꝏ̄.
34.7 Kah yeu pish kenanummiyeume sussuppóiyeumꝏ̄, wutch mishe kehtahhannit, pish kussohtikquóhhamúmwꝏ̄, wadchu Hor.
34.8 Wutch wadchuut Hor, pish kussohtikquohhamumwꝏ̄ paudshaat Hamath, kah sohwushait sussippói pish wehque Zedad.
34.9 Kah sussippoi pish nano monchemꝏ̄ wehque Ziphron, kah sohwushait pish ut Hazar-Enan: ne pish kenanummiyeume susfippóiyeumꝏ̄.
34.10 Kah pish kussohtikquohhamumwꝏ̄ kꝏ̄chepwôiye sussippóìyeumꝏ̄, wutch Hazar-Enan wehque Shepham.
34.11 Kah sussippói pish ꝏ̄mseumꝏ̄ wutch Shepham wehque Riblaah wutchepwoiyeu Ain; kah suffippói pish nano ꝏ̄mseumꝏ̄, kah pish wehqshin péquane ketahhannit Chinnereth wutchepwoiyau
34.12 Kah sussippoi pish ꝏ̄mseumꝏ̄ wehque Jordan, kah na sohwusháit pish salte keihtoh: ne pish kutohkeyeu kah sussippoi ne noh ohtag quinnuppu.
34.13 Kah Moses annꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Is[]ael, nꝏ̄wau, yeu ohke pish ohtauóg nashpe dtanohtóadtuonk, ne Jehovah annꝏ̄teamup aninnumauónat paskꝏ̄gun tahshit chippanꝏ̄ongash, kah pohshe chippanꝏ̄wonk.
34.14 Newutche wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Ruben, neaunag wekꝏ̄ash wutꝏ̄shineunk, kah wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Gad, neaunag wekꝏ̄ash wutꝏ̄shinneunk, mahche attumunumwog, kah paushe wutchippanꝏ̄onk Manasseh attumunumwog wutohtóonk.
34.15 Neese chippanꝏ̄wog, kah pohshe chippanꝏ̄onk mahche attumunumwog wutohtóonk wutúshame Jordan kishke Jericho, wutchepwóiyeu, nogque âhhut pashpishont.
34.16 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh, nꝏ̄wau.
34.17 Yeush ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄oash wosketompaog | neg pish chacháubenumwânshhikqueógig ohke, Eleazar sephausuaen, kah Joshua wunnaumonuh Nun.
34.18 Kah pish keneemunômwꝏ̄ pasuk sontim wutch ni[]h noh chippanꝏ̄wonk chachaubenumunat ohke nashpe ohtóongash.
34.19 Kah yeush ꝏ̄wesuongash wosketompaog: wutchippanꝏ̄onk Judah, Caleb wunnaumonuh Jephunneh
34.20 Kah wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Simeon, Shemuel wunnaumonuh Ammihud.
34.21 Wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk Benjamin, Elidad wunnaumonuh Chisson.
34.22 Kah sontim wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Dan, Bukki wunnaumonuh Jogli.
34.23 Sontim wutch wunnaumonat Joseph, wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Manasseh, Hanniel wunnaumonuh Ephod.
34.24 Kah sontim wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Ephraim, Kemuel wunnaumonuh Shiphtan.
34.25 Kah sontim wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Zebulon, Elizaphan wunnaumonuh Parnach.
34.26 Kah sontim wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Issachar, Paltiel wunnaumonuh Azzan.
34.27 Kah sontim wutch wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Asher, Ahihud wunnaumonuh Shelomi.
34.28 Kah sontim wutch wutchìppanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Naphtali, Pedahel wunnaumonuh Ammihud.
34.29 Yeug nnag neh Jehovah annꝏ̄teamupuhchadchaubenonat wutohtóonk wutch wunnaumonuh Israel ut ohkeit Kanaan.
35.1 KAh Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh ut Moabe mukoshquttaehtu, kishke Jordan kishke Jericho, nꝏ̄wau,
35.2 Annꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel magunat wutch wutohtꝏ̄onganꝏ̄out en Levitsut, ꝏ̄tanash wutohkinneat, kah pish kittinninnumau Levitsog paswohteagish ohteakonash wutche ohtaash waéenu.
35.3 Kah otanash pish ahtôog ayinneat, kah paswohtagish ohteakonash pish nish wutche wunnetasumꝏ̄uh, kah wutch wame ummaumachiyeuoash, kah wutch wame wunnetaseumoh.
35.4 Kah otanae paswohtagish ohteakonash, nish pish anumauôgish Levitsog, pish wutch otanae pummeneutunkanit, kah ongkoue nequt muttannongane ishquanogkod waéenu.
35.5 Kah pish kukquthumwꝏ̄ poquadchꝏ̄tanat wutcheksúeiyeu neese muttannongane | ishquanogkod, kah sowaniyeu neese mutannongane is(h)quanogkod, kah wutchesúeiyeu neese muttannongane ishquanogkod, kah nannummiyeu neese muttannongane ishquanogkod, kah otan pish nôeu ohteau: yeu pish wutche nagumau, paswohtagish ohteakonash.
35.6 Kah kenugke otanash nish pish anumauadcheh Levitsog, nequtta tahshinash keitotanash pish uspuhhꝏ̄onganuꝏ̄ash, nish pish kahtimogish wutch nushehteaen, onk woh na wutusishon: kah en nag pish kukkꝏ̄tnumauoog yauunchagkodtash keitotanash, kah neesunash.
35.7 Wame otanash nish pish anumauogish Levitsog, yauunchagkodtash kah shwosuk tahshinash keitotanash? yeush nashpe paswohtagish wutohteakonash.
35.8 Kah keitotanash nish pish magꝏ̄ogish, pish wutch wutohtóonganꝏ̄aut wunnaumonuh Israel, wutch nag monacheg, pish kummꝏ̄cheke mag, qut wutch nag oggussitche, pish kutogguhse mog, nish noh pasuk pish magꝏ̄ wutch otanahtu, en Levitsut, neaunag wutohtôonk ne ohtunk.
35.9 Kah Jehovah kenꝏ̄nau Mosesoh nꝏ̄wau,
35.10 Kenꝏ̄s wunnaumonuh Israel, kah nag us qushkodteaog Jordan, en ohkit Kanaan.
35.11 Neit pish kukkuhquttumumwꝏ̄ kitotanash uspuhhꝏ̄wae otanayeuꝏ̄ut, onk woh nushehteaen na usishau, noh nashont howane pehcheu.
35.12 Kah nish pish wutch kenâau uspuhhꝏ̄wae otanash wutch anꝏ̄tóaen, onk noh nushehteáen woh mo nuppꝏ̄, nó pajeh wunneepauunneat anaquabhettit mukkinneonk ut wussittumꝏ̄onganit[,]
35.13 Kah wutch otanash nish pish mogꝏ̄ogish nequtta tashinash otanash pish kutusphꝏ̄aonganꝏ̄oash.
35.14 Pish kummagumwꝏ̄ shwinash otanash wutushin Jordan, kah shwinash otanash pish kummagumwꝏ̄ ut ohkit Kanaan nish pish uspuhhꝏ̄aongane otanash.
35.15 Yeush nequtta tahshinash otanash pish uspuhhowaonganuꝏ̄ash, wutch wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wutch penuwohteaog, kah noh ne adt penꝏ̄wohteaut, onk woh nish noh pasuk noh nashteadt pehchu, na usi[]hau.
35.16 Kah togkomont nashpe moohshogque auwohteaonk (nuppꝏ̄ontog) noh nushehteaen: noh nushehteaen pish wunnamuhkut nushau.
35.17 Kah togkomont nashpe qussuk wutch wunnutchéganit, (uttoh woh adt nuppuk) kah nuppuk, noh nushehteaen: nushehteaen pish wunnamuhkut nushau.
35.18 Asuh togkomont nashpe metugque menutchegane auwohteaonk (uttoh woh adt nuppuk) kah nuppuk, noh nushehtean: nushehteaen pish wunnamuhkut nushau.
35.19 Noh ánꝏ̄(ta)uwanshteunk musqueheonk nagum pish nushau nu[]heteaenin nagkushkauont pish wunnushuh.
35.20 Qut konnukketahwhont wutch sekeneóadtinneat, asuh a[]kuhwheteae wadtuhkomont, kah nuppuk.
35.21 Asuh mekonittue togkomont nashpe wunnutcheganit, kah nuppuk, noh togkomont, pish wunamuhkut nushau, noh nushehteaen: noh anꝏ̄tauwanshteunk musqueheonk pish nu[]hau nushehteaenuh, nogkushkauont.
35.22 Qut matta sekeneaadtue konnukketahwhonk pehchu, asuh togkomont ne teag, matta askuhwheteae.
35.23 Asuh nashpe qussuk, uttah adt woh nuppuk matta nauunk, kah togkomont kah nuppinit, kah matta neh matwomegk, asuh mat kodnehikꝏ̄k.
35.24 Neit mukkinneonk pish wussittum nashaue nushehteaen, kah noh anꝏ̄tauwanshteunk musqueheonk neaunag yeush wussittumꝏ̄ongash.
35.25 Kah mukkinneonk pish uppohquohwhunuh nushehteaen, wutch wunnutcheganit noh anꝏ̄tauwanshteunk musqueheonk, kah mukkinneonk pish ukquehchuwunuh en wutuspꝏ̄hꝏ̄wae otanat, uttoh áshomp, kah na pish wuttaiin, nô pajeh wunnuppinat negone sephausuaen, noh sasequenomukup waneetupanatamwe pummee.
35.26 Qut nushehteaen woh toh uttꝏ̄che peyonk pequodche sussippoiyeuut uspuhhꝏ̄wae otanat, neashomp.
35.27 Kah noh anꝏ̄tauwanshteunk musqueheonk nameheont poquodche sussippoiyeuut wutuspuhꝏ̄wae otanat, kah noh anꝏ̄tauwanshteunk musqueheunk nushont, noh nushehteaen matta pish nushehteaenúꝏ̄.
35.28 Newutche woh appeup wutuspuhhꝏ̄wâe otanat nó pajeh wunnuppinat negonne sepheusuaen; qut mahche nuppuk negonne sephausuaen, nushehteaen pish qushkeu en wutohtoongan.
35.29 Nemehkuh yeush pish wussittumꝏ̄áe kuhkꝏ̄waonk wutche kenaau, pánnuppe kuppometuonganꝏ̄oash, ut wame kutayeuonganꝏ̄ôut.
35.30 Howan nashont howane, nushehteaen pish nushau nashpe wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ wauwacheg, qut pasuk wauwaen, matta pish ayeuuhkone wauwaunôuh howane nuppꝏ̄waheonat.
35.31 Nano, matta pish keneemunnumꝏ̄ taphettuonk, wutche uppomantamóenk nushéhteaen, noh kesukkóattog nuppun, qut pish wunnamuhkut nushau.
35.32 Kah matta pish keneemunnumꝏ̄ taphettuonk wutche nagum noh asishont wutuspuhhꝏ̄wae otanat, onk woh wonk qushkeu ayinneat wutohtoonganit, nô pajeh wunnuppunat negonne sephausuaen.
35.33 Nemehhuh matta pish kenishketea(u)ꝏ̄h | ohke uttoh ayeóg: newutch wusqueheonk neshkitteau ohke: kah ohke mattawoh uppahketeauun wutch wusqueheunk ne sꝏ̄ksquohtuhhamuk naut, qut wehe nashpe ꝏ̄sqheonk noh sꝏ̄ksquohtuhhogkup.
35.34 Newutche ahque nishketeauꝏ̄k ohke uttoh wodohkeyog, ut toh wôdohke, newutche nen Jehovah nꝏ̄weetom wunnaumonuh Israel.
36.1 KAh kehche wutꝏ̄shinneunk wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Gilead, wunnaumonuh Machir, wunnaumonuh Manasses, wutch wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄ wunnaumonuh Joseph, pasꝏ̄tsháog, kah kuttꝏ̄og ut anaquabit Moses, kah anaquabhettit sontimꝏ̄og kehche wutꝏ̄shineunk ut wunnaumonat Israel.
36.2 Kah nꝏ̄waog, Jehovah annꝏ̄nau nussontimomunonoh, magunat ohke, wutch ohtoonk, nashpe tanohtóodtuonk, en wunnaumonat Israel, kah Jehovah annꝏ̄nau nussontimomunonoh, aninumâuonat wutohtoonk Zelophehad neemattin, en wuttonit.
36.3 Kah wetauamahetttit howae wunnaumonaiinneuh onkatogane chippanꝏ̄wonkoh wunnaumonuh Israel, neit pish wutahtoonganꝏ̄ neemunnumun, wutch nꝏ̄shinónut wutohtaonganꝏ̄, kah pish ponumun kꝏ̄tne ohtoonganit ne chippanꝏ̄onk ne adt attumunit: neit pish amaunumun wutch tanohtóadtue kutohtoonganunônut.
36.4 Kah wut-jubilemhettit wunnaumonuh Israel neit pish wutohtoonganꝏ̄ ponamauóneau ut wutohtoonganꝏ̄óut ne chippanꝏ̄onk ne adt attumunit, neit pish wutohtoonganꝏ̄ amaunumauoneau, wutch wutohtoonganꝏ̄óut nꝏ̄shunônog wutchippanꝏ̄onganꝏ̄.
36.5 Kah Moses annꝏ̄nau wunnaumonuh Israel, neaunak wuttìnnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah, nꝏ̄wau, wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Joseph wunnomwaog.
36.6 Yeu ne Jehovah annꝏ̄teamwit, papaume wuttaunoh Zelophehad, nꝏ̄wau, wadtꝏ̄anumahetticheh, qut webe pish weetauomaog wutchippanꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh.
36.7 Nemehkuh wutohtoonk wunnaumonuh Israel matta pish ontohtano, wutch chippanꝏ̄onganit, yean chippanꝏ̄onganit, ne wutche nishnoh pasuk wunnaumonuh Israel, pish menuhkappu wutohtoonganit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wutchippanꝏ̄onk,
36.8 Kah nish noh wuttaunin noh ahtunk ohtóonk, noh toh un wutchippanꝏ̄onganit wunnaumonuh Israel, noh pish ummittamwusoh pasuk wutteateashiyeuonganit ꝏ̄shoh wutchippanꝏ̄onk, onk woh wunnaumonuh Israel oht[]u nishnoh wosketomp wutohtoonk ꝏ̄shoh.
36.9 Kah matta pish ohtoonk ontohtano wutch chippanꝏ̄onganit, yean chippanꝏ̄onganit, qut nishnoh wutchippanꝏ̄onk wunnaumonuh Israel, pish menuhkappu nehenwonche wutohtoonganit.
36.10 Nean annꝏ̄nomp Jehovah Mosesoh, ne wutusseneau wuttaunoh Zelophehad.
36.11 Newutche Mahlah, Tirzah, & Hoglah, kah Milchah, kah Noah, wuttaunoh Zelophahad, weetuwomâog ꝏ̄shuoh weemattꝏ̄oh wunnaumonuh.
36.12 Kah nag wetauadteaog wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄óut wunnaumonuh Manasses wunnaumonuh Joseph, kah wutahtoonk ohteau ut wutchippanꝏ̄onganit ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh wutteateashiyeuonganꝏ̄óut.
36.13 Yeush annꝏ̄teamꝏ̄ongash, kah wussittumꝏ̄ongash, anannꝏ̄teamwutcheh Jehovah nashpe wunnutcheg Moses, en wunnaumonat Israel, ut Moabe mukoshqutahtu, kishke Jordan, uttoh adt Jericho.
